import 'jsr:@supabase/functions-js/edge-runtime.d.ts' import { createClient } from 'npm:@supabase/supabase-js@2' const corsHeaders: Record = { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*', 'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type', 'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS', } function jsonResponse(body: unknown, status = 200) { return new Response(JSON.stringify(body), { status, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, }) } // ── callWebSearchAI ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Provider-agnostic web search + AI synthesis. // Supports: gemini (Google Search grounding) | anthropic (web_search tool) // OpenAI: stub ready — add when an org adopts it. // Returns: { text: string, error?: string } async function callWebSearchAI( prompt: string, orgCfg: { ai_engine: string; ai_api_key: string; ai_model: string }, opts: { maxTokens?: number; temperature?: number } = {} ): Promise<{ text: string; error?: string }> { const maxTokens = opts.maxTokens ?? 2000 const temperature = opts.temperature ?? 0.1 // ── Gemini — Google Search grounding ───────────────────────────────────── if (orgCfg.ai_engine === 'gemini' && orgCfg.ai_api_key) { const model = orgCfg.ai_model || 'gemini-2.5-flash' const url = `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/${model}:generateContent?key=${orgCfg.ai_api_key}` try { const res = await fetch(url, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }], tools: [{ google_search: {} }], generationConfig: { temperature, maxOutputTokens: maxTokens } }) }) const data = await res.json() const text = data?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || '' if (!text && data?.error) return { text: '', error: 'Gemini: ' + (data.error.message || JSON.stringify(data.error).slice(0, 100)) } return { text } } catch(e: any) { return { text: '', error: 'Gemini fetch: ' + e.message } } } // ── Anthropic Claude — web_search tool ─────────────────────────────────── if (orgCfg.ai_engine === 'anthropic' && orgCfg.ai_api_key) { const model = orgCfg.ai_model || 'claude-sonnet-4-6' try { const res = await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'x-api-key': orgCfg.ai_api_key, 'anthropic-version': '2023-06-01', 'anthropic-beta': 'web-search-2025-03-05', 'content-type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ model, max_tokens: maxTokens, tools: [{ type: 'web_search_20250305', name: 'web_search' }], messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }] }) }) const data = await res.json() const text = (data.content || []).filter((b: any) => b.type === 'text').map((b: any) => b.text).join('') if (!text && data.error) return { text: '', error: 'Anthropic: ' + (data.error.message || JSON.stringify(data.error).slice(0, 100)) } return { text } } catch(e: any) { return { text: '', error: 'Anthropic fetch: ' + e.message } } } // ── OpenAI — stub for future ────────────────────────────────────────────── if (orgCfg.ai_engine === 'openai') { // TODO: implement GPT-4o with web_search_preview tool when needed return { text: '', error: 'OpenAI web search not yet implemented' } } return { text: '', error: 'No AI engine configured (gemini | anthropic | openai)' } } // ── parseAIJson ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Robustly extract JSON from AI text — handles markdown fences, raw JSON, partial. function parseAIJson(text: string): any | null { const t = text.trim() // Repair helper: fix common AI JSON mistakes before parsing const repair = (s: string): string => s .replace(/,\s*([}\]])/g, '$1') // trailing commas .replace(/([{,]\s*)(\w+)(\s*:)/g, '$1"$2"$3') // unquoted keys .replace(/:\s*'([^']*)'/g, ': "$1"') // single-quoted values // Strip markdown fences (with or without leading space/newline) const stripped = t.replace(/^\s*```(?:json)?\s*/i, '').replace(/\s*```\s*$/, '').trim() const candidates = [stripped, t] for (const raw of candidates) { // Find first { and last } to isolate the JSON object const s = raw.indexOf('{') const e = raw.lastIndexOf('}') if (s === -1 || e === -1) continue const slice = raw.slice(s, e + 1) // Try progressively: raw → repaired → trimmed from end for (const attempt of [slice, repair(slice)]) { try { const r = JSON.parse(attempt); if (r && typeof r === 'object') return r } catch(_) {} } // Last resort: trim from end until valid JSON found for (let i = slice.length; i > 20; i--) { try { const trimmed = slice.slice(0, i) // Only try at positions that could close a JSON object if (trimmed[trimmed.length - 1] !== '}' && trimmed[trimmed.length - 1] !== ']') continue const r = JSON.parse(trimmed); if (r && typeof r === 'object') return r } catch(_) {} } } return null } // ── extractBrandRoot: strips domain noise to get the core brand identifier ── // Handles multinational domain patterns like: // in.lactalis.com → lactalis // lactalis-international.fr → lactalis // fr.lactalis.com → lactalis // lactalis.sa → lactalis // shell-lubricants.in → shell // totale.fr → total (we can't handle brand variants, but name match covers this) // totalenergies.com → totalenergies // Strategy: (1) strip country subdomains, (2) strip TLD, (3) strip corporate suffixes function extractBrandRoot(domain: string): string { if (!domain) return '' let d = domain.toLowerCase().trim() // Remove protocol/path if accidentally passed a full URL d = d.replace(/^https?:\/\//, '').split('/')[0].split('?')[0] // Strip known country-code + generic subdomains (in., fr., uk., us., de., me., ae., sg., etc.) const subdomainPrefixes = /^(in|fr|uk|us|de|me|ae|sg|au|ca|za|ng|ke|eg|sa|pk|bd|my|th|ph|id|nz|hk|jp|cn|br|mx|ar|cl|co|pe|tr|pl|nl|be|it|es|pt|ch|se|no|dk|fi|at|cz|hu|ro|bg|hr|sk|si|rs|ba|al|mk|eu|global|intl|mail|email|corporate|corp|group|www|web|portal)\./ // Remove up to 2 subdomain levels that match for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) { d = d.replace(subdomainPrefixes, '') } // Remove TLD — handle multi-part TLDs like .co.uk, .com.au, .co.in d = d.replace(/\.(co\.(uk|in|za|nz|jp|id|kr)|com\.(au|br|mx|ar|sg|hk)|org\.uk|net\.au|co\.jp|ac\.uk)$/, '') d = d.replace(/\.(com|org|net|io|ai|co|fr|de|in|sa|ae|uk|us|au|ca|ng|ke|pk|mx|br|it|es|pt|nl|be|se|no|dk|fi|pl|cz|ru|cn|jp|kr|sg|hk|za|eg|gh|tz|ug|rw|ma|tn|dz|ly|sd|so|ci|sn|ml|bf|tg|bj|ne|cm|ga|cg|cd|ao|mz|zm|zw|bw|na|ls|sz|mg|mu|re|yt|sc|cv|st|gw|gn|sl|lr|gm|gq|bi|dj|er|et|km|mw|rw)$/, '') // Strip corporate suffixes from the name part (hyphened or not) d = d.replace(/[-_]?(international|intl|group|global|corp|corporate|business|enterprise|solutions|services|industries|limited|ltd|inc|llc|sa|gmbh|ag|plc|holding|holdings|management|marketing|distribution|logistics|trading|asia|europe|africa|americas|middle.?east|mea|apac|emea|latam)[-_]?/g, '') // Remove hyphens/underscores and non-alphanum d = d.replace(/[-_]/g, '').replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '') return d } // Also used to match company names from emails/signals — strips noise words function normCompanyName(s: string): string { return s.toLowerCase() .replace(/\b(india|global|international|ltd|limited|pvt|inc|llc|corp|sa|ag|gmbh|plc|group|co|the|and|&)\b/g, '') .replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '').trim() } // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // ROLE HIERARCHY — single source of truth for all permission checks. // // Tier 1: sdr, ae — frontline reps, see only own data // Tier 2: manager — sees their direct reports' data // Tier 3: director — sees multiple managers' teams // Tier 4: executive — sees entire org pipeline / board-level metrics // Tier 5: admin — everything executive sees + user/org management // // "samora_admin" is NOT in this hierarchy — it's checked via the // samora_admins table in admin-specific actions only. // // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // FRAMEWORK: Intent classification and inbox email classification. // These are the two core framework functions that determine HOW we verify // a task — or whether we verify it at all. // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // parseTaskIntent: classify what a task IS before any verification runs. // Gate that prevents internal tasks (MOM, CRM update, deck prep) from // ever reaching Gmail search — the root cause of false verifications. function parseTaskIntent(text: string): { intentType: 'email_outreach' | 'meeting' | 'call' | 'linkedin' | 'whatsapp' | 'internal' | 'unknown' quantityClaimed: number isVerifiableViaGmail: boolean isVerifiableViaCalendar: boolean } { const lower = text.toLowerCase().trim() // ── MOM / minutes — always internal ─────────────────────────────────────── if (/\bmom\b|minutes of meeting|meeting minutes|meeting notes|meeting summary/i.test(text)) { return { intentType: 'internal', quantityClaimed: 1, isVerifiableViaGmail: false, isVerifiableViaCalendar: false } } // ── Discovery / research verbs — NEVER verifiable via Gmail ─────────────── // "Find stakeholders", "Identify contacts", "Research Reckitt" etc. are // internal research tasks. There is no email that proves you "found" something. // This is the most commonly missed internal verb class. if (/^(find|finding|found|identify|identifying|locate|locating|research|researching|investigate|investigating|explore|exploring|source|sourcing|discover|discovering|map|mapping|look up|looking up|get contact|get phone|get email|get number|search for|search|prospect for|shortlist|shortlisting|build a list|build list|compile|compiling)/i.test(text) && !/(send|email|mail|reach out|follow up|outreach)/i.test(lower)) { return { intentType: 'internal', quantityClaimed: 1, isVerifiableViaGmail: false, isVerifiableViaCalendar: false } } // ── Admin / document verbs — NEVER verifiable via Gmail ─────────────────── if (/^(create|prepare|write|draft|update|review|analyse|analyze|plan|organise|organize|read|study|fill|upload|submit|log|note|document|record|summarize|summarise|check|consolidate|clean up|reconcile)/i.test(text) && !/(email|mail|reach|outreach|follow.?up|send)/i.test(lower)) { return { intentType: 'internal', quantityClaimed: 1, isVerifiableViaGmail: false, isVerifiableViaCalendar: false } } // ── Internal object nouns — no outreach verb → internal ─────────────────── if (/\b(deck|powerpoint|ppt|crm|salesforce|forecast report|budget sheet|tracker|template|stakeholder list|contact list|database)\b/i.test(lower) && !/(send|share|email|mail)\s+\w+\s+(deck|slide|ppt|proposal)/i.test(lower)) { return { intentType: 'internal', quantityClaimed: 1, isVerifiableViaGmail: false, isVerifiableViaCalendar: false } } // Extract quantity claimed const numMatch = text.match(/\b(\d+)\s*(email|mail|message|connect|request|follow|prospect)/i) const quantityClaimed = numMatch ? parseInt(numMatch[1]) : 1 if (/\blinkedin\b|inmail|li\s+message|li\s+connect/i.test(text)) return { intentType: 'linkedin', quantityClaimed, isVerifiableViaGmail: false, isVerifiableViaCalendar: false } if (/whatsapp/i.test(text)) return { intentType: 'whatsapp', quantityClaimed, isVerifiableViaGmail: false, isVerifiableViaCalendar: false } if (/\bcall(s|ing|ed)?\b|\bphone\b|\bdial\b/.test(lower) && !/\b(email|mail|send|meeting|demo)\b/.test(lower)) return { intentType: 'call', quantityClaimed, isVerifiableViaGmail: false, isVerifiableViaCalendar: false } const isMeetingTask = /\b(meeting|demo|presentation|discuss|sync up|syncup|catch up|catchup|virtual meet|video call)\b/.test(lower) if (isMeetingTask) { const hasOutreachVerb = /\b(send|email|invite|share|follow)\b/.test(lower) return { intentType: 'meeting', quantityClaimed: 1, isVerifiableViaGmail: hasOutreachVerb, isVerifiableViaCalendar: true } } if (/\b(send|email|mail|follow.?up|reach out|outreach|pitch|introduce|connect|message|share proposal)\b/.test(lower)) return { intentType: 'email_outreach', quantityClaimed, isVerifiableViaGmail: true, isVerifiableViaCalendar: false } return { intentType: 'unknown', quantityClaimed, isVerifiableViaGmail: true, isVerifiableViaCalendar: false } } // classifyInboxEmail: determine the nature of an inbox reply BEFORE assuming positive. // Priority: BOUNCE > OOO > NEGATIVE > POSITIVE. // Bounce MUST come first — a delivery failure from Microsoft contains the // original recipient domain in the body, so OOO/negative checks would miss it. function classifyInboxEmail(snippet: string, subject: string, senderEmail: string): { type: 'bounce' | 'ooo' | 'negative' | 'positive' } { const combined = (snippet + ' ' + subject).toLowerCase() const sender = (senderEmail || '').toLowerCase() const isBounceSender = /mailer-daemon@|postmaster@|bounces?@|delivery@|noreply@|no-reply@|notifications@microsoft|msprvs|smtp\.mailfrom/i.test(sender) const isBounceContent = /delivery has failed|undeliverable|delivery failure|mail delivery failed|delivery status notification|non.delivery|could not be delivered|failed to deliver|message not delivered|permanent failure|address.*not found|user.*does not exist|mailbox.*unavailable|account.*disabled|user unknown|recipient.*rejected|5\.[0-9]\.[0-9]|\b550\b|\b551\b|\b552\b|\b553\b/i.test(combined) if (isBounceSender || isBounceContent) return { type: 'bounce' } const isOOO = /out of office|on leave|on vacation|i am away|i'm away|im away|will be back|back on|returning on|auto.?reply|automatic reply|not available until|currently unavailable|on annual leave|on holiday|away from (the )?office|limited access.*email|offsite|have changed position|have left the company|no longer at|have recently left/i.test(combined) if (isOOO) return { type: 'ooo' } const isNegative = /not interested|unsubscribe|remove me|opt.out|please stop|do not contact|take me off|no thank|not relevant|wrong person|not the right contact|don't email/i.test(combined) if (isNegative) return { type: 'negative' } return { type: 'positive' } } // Role sets for permission checks — use these instead of inline arrays: const ROLE_TIER_1 = new Set(['sdr', 'ae', 'member']) // rep-level const ROLE_TIER_2UP = new Set(['manager', 'director', 'executive', 'admin', 'super_admin']) // can see team const ROLE_TIER_3UP = new Set(['director', 'executive', 'admin', 'super_admin']) // can see cross-team const ROLE_TIER_4UP = new Set(['executive', 'admin', 'super_admin']) // can see full org const ROLE_TIER_5 = new Set(['admin', 'super_admin']) // can manage users/settings function isRepRole(role: string): boolean { return ROLE_TIER_1.has(role) } function canSeeTeam(role: string): boolean { return ROLE_TIER_2UP.has(role) } function canSeeCrossTeam(role: string): boolean { return ROLE_TIER_3UP.has(role) } function canSeeFullOrg(role: string): boolean { return ROLE_TIER_4UP.has(role) } function canManageOrg(role: string): boolean { return ROLE_TIER_5.has(role) } // ── IMPROVED: Extract meaningful account/person names from task text ────────── // Skips verb-like words at the start, skips stop words, returns ALL candidates // Parses a task description for an explicit activity quantity and type, e.g. // "Pladis stakeholder UK 10 emails" -> { quantity: 10, type: 'email' }, // "Grupo bimbo Mexico 15 email" -> { quantity: 15, type: 'email' }, // "Reaching out ... LinkedIn" (no number) -> { quantity: 1, type: 'linkedin' }. // Falls back to quantity 1 (treat the task itself as one activity unit) when // no number is present in the text, and to type 'other' when no recognisable // channel keyword is found. function parseActivityQuantity(taskText: string): { quantity: number, type: 'call' | 'email' | 'meeting' | 'linkedin' | 'whatsapp' | 'other' } { const lower = taskText.toLowerCase() // Channel keywords, ordered so more specific terms are checked first // (e.g. "cold calling" before generic "call"). let type: 'call' | 'email' | 'meeting' | 'linkedin' | 'whatsapp' | 'other' = 'other' if (/linkedin/.test(lower)) type = 'linkedin' else if (/whatsapp/.test(lower)) type = 'whatsapp' else if (/\bemail(s)?\b|\bmail(s)?\b/.test(lower)) type = 'email' else if (/\bcall(s|ing)?\b/.test(lower)) type = 'call' else if (/\bmeeting(s)?\b|\bdemo(s)?\b|\bpresentation(s)?\b/.test(lower)) type = 'meeting' // Look for a number anywhere in the text that's plausibly an activity // count — written digits ("10 emails") or spelled-out small numbers // ("ten emails", "five calls"). Picks the first match. const digitMatch = taskText.match(/\b(\d{1,4})\b/) if (digitMatch) { const n = parseInt(digitMatch[1], 10) if (n > 0 && n < 10000) return { quantity: n, type } } const wordNumbers: Record = { one: 1, two: 2, three: 3, four: 4, five: 5, six: 6, seven: 7, eight: 8, nine: 9, ten: 10, eleven: 11, twelve: 12, fifteen: 15, twenty: 20, thirty: 30, forty: 40, fifty: 50 } for (const word of Object.keys(wordNumbers)) { if (new RegExp('\\b' + word + '\\b', 'i').test(lower)) { return { quantity: wordNumbers[word], type } } } return { quantity: 1, type } } function extractAccountCandidates(taskText: string): string[] { const stopWords = new Set([ // Prepositions, articles, conjunctions 'the','and','for','to','on','at','in','a','an','of','with','from','by', // Common task verbs — outreach 'meet','meeting','call','email','send','follow','up','catch','reach', 'contact','connect','discuss','proposal','demo','presentation','book', 'schedule','share','message','messages','mail','mails','outreach','pitch', 'introduce','reconnect','sync','syncing','syncup','catchup','cold','calling', 'calls','close','closing','negotiate','negotiating','onboard','onboarding', 'renew','renewal','escalate','escalation','invite','inviting', // Common task verbs — internal / admin 'check','review','update','prepare','write','draft','client','prospect', 'done','task','action','complete','make','take','get','work','need', 'have','will','this','that','about','re','fwd','regarding','internal', 'external','team','office','next','step','steps','follow-up','status', 'today','tomorrow','please','prepare','confirm','confirming','finalize', 'finalise','emails','drafting','reviewing', // ── CHANNEL NAMES — must never be extracted as account names ───────────── // "LinkedIn 30 Follow up" → "LinkedIn" is a channel, not a company account. // These appear capitalised as first words (or standalone), making them look // like proper nouns. All channel/tool names belong in stopwords. 'linkedin','inmail','whatsapp','gmail','outlook','email','instagram', 'twitter','facebook','telegram','signal','skype','zoom','teams', 'slack','meet','calendar', // These are the most common task-opening words that look like proper nouns // (capitalised at sentence start) but are action verbs, not company names. // "Find more stakeholder of Rekkit" → "Find" must NOT be an account candidate. 'find','finding','found','identify','identifying','identified','locate', 'locating','located','research','researching','researched','investigate', 'investigating','investigated','explore','exploring','explored','source', 'sourcing','sourced','discover','discovering','discovered','map','mapping', 'mapped','search','searching','looked','compile','compiling','compiled', 'shortlist','shortlisting','build','building','built','create','creating', 'created','consolidate','consolidating','reconcile','reconciling','analyse', 'analyze','analysing','analyzing','read','reading','study','studying','plan', 'planning','upload','uploading','submit','submitting','log','logging', 'note','noting','document','documenting','record','recording','summarize', 'summarise','fill','filling', ]) const words = taskText.trim().split(/[\s\-\/,]+/) const candidates: string[] = [] words.forEach((w) => { const clean = w.replace(/[^a-zA-Z]/g, '').trim() if ( clean.length >= 3 && !stopWords.has(clean.toLowerCase()) && // Must start with uppercase (proper noun) clean[0] === clean[0].toUpperCase() && clean[0] !== clean[0].toLowerCase() ) { candidates.push(clean) } }) return [...new Set(candidates)] } // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // UNIFIED ACCOUNT RESOLUTION — single source of truth for "which account // does this task text belong to, and what should I search Gmail for". // // This replaced two separately-maintained, near-duplicate implementations // (one in account_coverage, one in intent_vs_reality) that drifted apart // over several rounds of fixes — generic-word filtering existed in one but // not the other, candidate extraction bugs got fixed in one place and not // the other, etc. Every action that needs to resolve task text to an // account now calls resolveAccountForTask() below, so fixes apply // everywhere at once and the two paths can no longer silently diverge. // // Common words (regional/directional qualifiers, generic country names) // that frequently sit next to a real account name in task text — "Shell // Middle East", "TotalEnergies France", "Lactalis Europe" — but are too // generic to safely drive a Gmail search on their own. An OR query // including "Middle" or "France" pulls in unrelated emails and can crowd // the real match out of the results entirely. These words are excluded // from SEARCH TERMS only — they're still valid for display/scoring. const GENERIC_ACCOUNT_WORDS = new Set([ 'middle','east','west','north','south','asia','pacific','europe','emea', 'apac','america','americas','global','region','regional','international', 'india','uk','usa','us','mexico','china','japan','africa','australia', 'philippines','singapore','germany','france','italy','spain','brazil', 'canada','korea','vietnam','thailand','indonesia','malaysia' ]) // Suffixes commonly appended to legal entity names — stripped when deriving // a "first significant word" to fuzzy-match against task text, since a task // will say "Gulf Oil Philippines" but the assigned account is "Gulf Oil // Ltd." — neither "Ltd" nor "Pvt" nor "Inc" is what a rep actually types. const ACCOUNT_NAME_STOPWORDS = new Set([ 'the','ltd','ltd.','inc','inc.','llc','co','co.','corp','corp.','pvt', 'private','limited','group' ]) // ── extractEmailBody: pulls readable text from a Gmail message payload ────── // Handles both text/plain and text/html parts. HTML is stripped to plain text // so Gemini sees the full structured content (Fireflies/Fathom put their // action items, outlines and keywords in HTML, not plain text). function extractEmailBody(payload: any): string { if (!payload) return '' const extractPart = (part: any): string => { if (!part) return '' if (part.body?.data) { const b64 = part.body.data.replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/') try { const decoded = atob(b64) if (part.mimeType === 'text/html') { // Strip HTML tags but preserve structure: convert block elements to newlines return decoded .replace(//gi, '\n') .replace(/<\/?(p|div|li|h[1-6]|tr|td)[^>]*>/gi, '\n') .replace(/<[^>]+>/g, '') .replace(/&/g, '&').replace(/</g, '<').replace(/>/g, '>').replace(/ /g, ' ').replace(/'/g, "'") .replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n').trim() } return decoded } catch { return '' } } if (part.parts) { // Prefer HTML over plain text — it has more structure const html = part.parts.find((p: any) => p.mimeType === 'text/html') if (html) return extractPart(html) return part.parts.map(extractPart).filter(Boolean).join('\n') } return '' } // Try the multipart payload const body = extractPart(payload) return body || '' } // ── detectNotetakerProvider: identify which notetaker sent an email ────────── function detectNotetakerProvider(from: string, subject: string): string | null { const f = from.toLowerCase(); const s = subject.toLowerCase() if (f.includes('fireflies') || s.includes('fireflies')) return 'fireflies' if (f.includes('fathom')) return 'fathom' if (f.includes('otter')) return 'otter' if (f.includes('tldv') || s.includes('tl;dv')) return 'tldv' if (f.includes('grain')) return 'grain' if (f.includes('gong')) return 'gong' if (f.includes('chorus')) return 'chorus' if (f.includes('avoma')) return 'avoma' if (f.includes('granola')) return 'granola' if (f.includes('supernormal')) return 'supernormal' if (f.includes('krisp')) return 'krisp' if (f.includes('sembly')) return 'sembly' if (f.includes('read.ai')) return 'read_ai' if (/meeting notes|meeting recap|meeting summary|call summary|call notes|recording summary/i.test(s)) return 'email_generic' return null } // ── resolveChannelSignals ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── // The single framework function for verifying any channel activity. // Tool-agnostic by design: it accepts pre-fetched signals from ANY source // (Gmail, Outlook, SmartReach, Outreach, Apollo, Salesloft — whatever) and // applies the correct verification priority per channel. // // VERIFICATION PRIORITY BY CHANNEL (ground truth determines who's authoritative): // // EMAIL: Gmail/Outlook sent folder (dated, authoritative) // → sequencing tool email step (date-imprecise, secondary) // → rep logged (unverified) // // CALL: Rep marked done in SamoraTrack (THE rep saw the call — no tool did) // → calendar event mentioning account (objective evidence) // → sequencing tool call step (unreliable — rarely exposed per-prospect) // → rep logged but not done (gap) // // LINKEDIN: Email notification (LinkedIn sends accept/reply emails to inbox) // → sequencing tool LinkedIn step // → rep logged // // WHATSAPP: Sequencing tool WhatsApp step // → rep completion note // → rep logged // // Returns a ChannelResult for each channel — callers use this instead of // assembling verification logic inline. Adding a new tool = add its signals // to the seqSignals array before calling this function. Nothing else changes. function resolveChannelSignals(params: { account: string dateFrom: string // YYYY-MM-DD dateTo: string daytracks: any[] // rows from daytrack table for the period seqSignals: { channel: string, event_type: string, replied: boolean, completed: boolean, prospect_company: string }[] seqDataTotals?: { email: number, call: number, linkedin: number, whatsapp: number, opens: number } | null emailVerifiedCount: number // from Gmail/Outlook sent search inboxReplyCount: number // from Gmail/Outlook inbox search linkedinNotifCount: number // from LinkedIn Gmail/Outlook notifications calendarEvents?: any[] // Google Calendar or Outlook calendarView events }): { email: { logged: number, verified: number, source: string | null, detail: string } call: { logged: number, verified: number, source: string | null, detail: string, selfAttested: number } linkedin: { logged: number, verified: number, source: string | null, detail: string } whatsapp: { logged: number, verified: number, source: string | null, detail: string } meeting: { logged: number, verified: number, source: string | null, detail: string } replies: number } { const accountLower = params.account.toLowerCase() // ── Count logged activity from SamoraTrack ────────────────────────────── let emailLogged = 0, callLogged = 0, linkedinLogged = 0, whatsappLogged = 0, meetingLogged = 0 // Completed tasks by channel (rep confirmed they did it) let callDoneCount = 0 // completed tasks with call keywords let callAttestedCount = 0 // completed tasks with structured outcome let whatsappDoneCount = 0 let linkedinDoneCount = 0 params.daytracks.forEach((dt: any) => { ;(dt.data?.tasks || []).forEach((t: any) => { const text = (t.text || '').toLowerCase() const note = (t.completionNote || '').toLowerCase() const mentionsAccount = text.includes(accountLower) || note.includes(accountLower) if (!mentionsAccount) return const { type } = parseActivityQuantity(t.text || '') if (type === 'email') emailLogged++ if (type === 'call') { callLogged++; if (t.done) callDoneCount++ } if (type === 'linkedin') { linkedinLogged++; if (t.done) linkedinDoneCount++ } if (type === 'whatsapp') { whatsappLogged++; if (t.done) whatsappDoneCount++ } if (type === 'meeting') meetingLogged++ // Structured close-out outcome = strongest self-attestation for calls if (t.done && type === 'call' && ['no_answer','spoke_briefly','full_conversation','meeting_booked','not_interested'].includes(t.activityOutcome || '')) { callAttestedCount++ } // Also catch WhatsApp structured outcomes if (t.done && type === 'whatsapp' && ['messages_sent','replies_received','meeting_booked'].includes(t.activityOutcome || '')) { whatsappDoneCount = Math.max(whatsappDoneCount, 1) } }) }) // ── Count sequencing tool signals (tool-agnostic) ──────────────────────── // seqSignals come pre-normalised: channel in ['email','call','linkedin','whatsapp'] // NOTE: For calls we do NOT require completed=true — SmartReach rarely exposes // per-step completion reliably. Any call-channel signal = evidence of outreach. // For email we count sent events specifically. // Declare seqTotals FIRST — used by seqCall and seqAnyActivity below const seqTotals = params.seqDataTotals || null const seqEmail = seqTotals?.email ?? params.seqSignals.filter((s: any) => s.channel === 'email').length const seqCall = seqTotals?.call ?? params.seqSignals.filter((s: any) => s.channel === 'call').length const seqLinkedin = seqTotals?.linkedin ?? params.seqSignals.filter((s: any) => s.channel === 'linkedin').length const seqWhatsapp = seqTotals?.whatsapp ?? params.seqSignals.filter((s: any) => s.channel === 'whatsapp').length const seqReplied = params.seqSignals.filter((s: any) => s.replied).length const seqCallFromSR = seqCall const seqAnyActivity = seqTotals ? (seqTotals.email + seqTotals.call + seqTotals.linkedin + seqTotals.whatsapp + (seqTotals.opens || 0)) : params.seqSignals.length // ── Calendar verification for calls and meetings ───────────────────────── // A calendar event mentioning the account = objective evidence of interaction. // For calls: broader match (no keyword filter) because reps don't put "call" // in every calendar event title. let calCallCount = 0 let calMeetingCount = 0 if (params.calendarEvents) { params.calendarEvents.forEach((e: any) => { const title = (e.summary || e.subject || '').toLowerCase() const body = (e.description || e.bodyPreview || '').toLowerCase() const attendeeText = ((e.attendees || e.attendeesList || []).map((a: any) => a.email || a.emailAddress?.address || '' ).join(' ')).toLowerCase() const allText = title + ' ' + body + ' ' + attendeeText if (!allText.includes(accountLower)) return // Call-type events: shorter duration or explicit call keywords const isCallEvent = /\bcall\b|phone|dial|spoke|ring/i.test(title) || ((e.end?.dateTime && e.start?.dateTime) && (new Date(e.end.dateTime).getTime() - new Date(e.start.dateTime).getTime()) < 45 * 60 * 1000) if (isCallEvent) calCallCount++ else calMeetingCount++ }) } // ── Resolve EMAIL ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── const emailVerified = params.emailVerifiedCount const emailSource = emailVerified > 0 && seqEmail > 0 ? 'inbox+seq' : emailVerified > 0 ? 'inbox' : seqEmail > 0 ? 'seq' : null const emailDetail = emailVerified > 0 ? emailVerified + ' in sent folder' : seqEmail > 0 ? seqEmail + ' sequence steps' : '' // ── Resolve CALL (rep-first priority) ──────────────────────────────────── // Key: rep completion is authoritative for calls. // Enhancement: task_done + ANY sequencing signal for this account (any channel) // = stronger verification. SmartReach activity for the account corroborates // the rep's self-report even if the channel tag is wrong. // seqTotals, seqCallFromSR, seqAnyActivity declared above in seq block let callVerified = 0; let callSource: string | null = null; let callDetail = '' if (callAttestedCount > 0) { callVerified = callAttestedCount; callSource = 'attested' callDetail = callAttestedCount + ' with outcome logged' } else if (callDoneCount > 0 && seqCallFromSR > 0) { // Task done + SR has call-tagged signals callVerified = Math.max(callDoneCount, seqCallFromSR); callSource = 'task+seq' callDetail = callDoneCount + ' task done · ' + seqCallFromSR + ' SR calls' } else if (callDoneCount > 0 && seqAnyActivity > 0) { // Task done + SR has ANY activity for account (fuzzy matched via seqDataTotals) callVerified = callDoneCount; callSource = 'task+sr' callDetail = callDoneCount + ' task done · SR: ' + seqAnyActivity + ' touchpoints' } else if (callDoneCount > 0) { callVerified = callDoneCount; callSource = 'task-done' callDetail = callDoneCount + ' task(s) marked done' } else if (calCallCount > 0) { callVerified = calCallCount; callSource = 'calendar' callDetail = calCallCount + ' calendar event(s)' } else if (seqCall > 0) { callVerified = seqCall; callSource = 'seq' callDetail = seqCall + ' sequence call step(s)' } // ── Resolve LINKEDIN ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── const liVerified = Math.max(params.linkedinNotifCount, seqLinkedin, linkedinDoneCount) const liSource = params.linkedinNotifCount > 0 ? 'notification' : seqLinkedin > 0 ? 'seq' : linkedinDoneCount > 0 ? 'task-done' : null const liDetail = liVerified > 0 ? liVerified + ' ' + (liSource === 'notification' ? 'notifications' : liSource === 'seq' ? 'sequence steps' : 'tasks done') : '' // ── Resolve WHATSAPP ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── const waVerified = Math.max(seqWhatsapp, whatsappDoneCount) const waSource = seqWhatsapp > 0 ? 'seq' : whatsappDoneCount > 0 ? 'task-done' : null const waDetail = waVerified > 0 ? waVerified + ' ' + (waSource === 'seq' ? 'sequence steps' : 'tasks done') : '' // ── Resolve MEETING ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── const mtgVerified = calMeetingCount const mtgSource = calMeetingCount > 0 ? 'calendar' : null return { email: { logged: emailLogged, verified: emailVerified, source: emailSource, detail: emailDetail }, call: { logged: callLogged, verified: callVerified, source: callSource, detail: callDetail, selfAttested: callAttestedCount }, linkedin: { logged: linkedinLogged, verified: liVerified, source: liSource, detail: liDetail }, whatsapp: { logged: whatsappLogged, verified: waVerified, source: waSource, detail: waDetail }, meeting: { logged: meetingLogged, verified: mtgVerified, source: mtgSource, detail: '' }, replies: params.inboxReplyCount + seqReplied } } // ── buildNotetakerGeminiPrompt: provider-aware extraction prompt ───────────── // Returns a Gemini prompt that extracts richly structured intelligence from // a notetaker email. Provider-specific context helps Gemini find the right // sections — Fireflies emails have "Action Items", "Meeting Topics", "Keywords" // as labelled sections; Fathom has "Chapters" and "Highlights". function buildNotetakerGeminiPrompt(emailBody: string, provider: string | null, accountName?: string): string { const providerHint = { fireflies: 'This is a Fireflies.ai meeting summary. It has sections: Action Items, Meeting Topics/Outline, Keywords. Extract verbatim from these sections.', fathom: 'This is a Fathom meeting summary. It has chapters with timestamps and highlighted quotes. Extract from the chapters and highlights.', otter: 'This is an Otter.ai meeting summary with action items and transcript highlights.', tldv: 'This is a tl;dv meeting summary with timestamped quotes and chapter summaries.', grain: 'This is a Grain meeting reel/summary with highlights and key moments.', gong: 'This is a Gong call summary with talk ratio, next steps, and key moments.', read_ai: 'This is a Read.ai meeting transcript. The turns array contains speaker-attributed text. Extract signals from speaker turns, action items, and the summary. Read.ai also provides engagement and sentiment metrics.', readai: 'This is a Read.ai meeting transcript with speaker-attributed turns and engagement metrics.', }[provider || ''] || 'This is a meeting/call summary email from a notetaker tool.' return `You are a B2B sales intelligence analyst extracting verified signals from a meeting summary. ${providerHint} ${accountName ? 'Account context: ' + accountName : ''} MEETING EMAIL: ${emailBody.slice(0, 8000)} CRITICAL: Extract exact verbatim quotes where possible. A quote like "budget of ₹40L confirmed" is far more valuable than a paraphrase. For budget signals, extract the exact figure mentioned. Return ONLY valid JSON — no other text: { "title": "meeting title from subject or first line", "participants": ["Name or Name (Company)"], "summary": "2-3 sentence deal summary: what was discussed, what was decided, what happens next", "sentiment": "positive|neutral|negative", "key_quotes": [ {"speaker": "person name or role", "quote": "verbatim text", "signal_type": "budget|timeline|objection|expansion|competitor|positive|risk"} ], "budget_signals": [ {"amount": null_or_number, "currency": "INR|USD|AED|GBP|EUR|SAR", "context": "exact quote mentioning budget"} ], "objections": [ {"objection": "verbatim objection raised", "response": "how it was handled or null"} ], "action_items": [ {"owner": "person name", "action": "specific concrete task", "due": "date string or null"} ], "competitor_mentions": [ {"name": "competitor name", "context": "verbatim or near-verbatim of what was said"} ], "next_steps": "specific next action with owner and date if mentioned", "signal_score_delta": integer_from_minus20_to_plus30 }` } interface ResolvedAccount { // Clean canonical name for UI display — always the org_accounts value // when an assigned account matched, never a guessed/free-text value // unless nothing assigned matched at all. displayName: string // Whether displayName came from assignedAccounts (high confidence) or // free-text guessing (low confidence, caller may want to exclude this // from strict views like the coverage grid). matchedAssignedAccount: boolean // Full set of proper-noun-like words found in the task text — used for // SCORING (subject/body/to-field matches), not for the search query // itself, since this list still includes generic words like "France". allCandidates: string[] // Subset of allCandidates safe to use as Gmail OR-search terms — generic // geography/regional words filtered out. Falls back to allCandidates if // filtering would leave nothing (better an over-broad search than none). searchTerms: string[] } function resolveAccountForTask( taskText: string, assignedAccounts: { id?: string, account_name: string, domain?: string, region?: string, parent_account_id?: string }[] ): ResolvedAccount { const lower = taskText.toLowerCase() const allCandidates = extractAccountCandidates(taskText) // Pass 1: exact full account name appears verbatim in the task text. const exactMatch = assignedAccounts .filter(a => a.account_name && lower.includes(a.account_name.toLowerCase())) .sort((a, b) => b.account_name.length - a.account_name.length)[0] if (exactMatch) { return { displayName: exactMatch.account_name, matchedAssignedAccount: true, allCandidates, searchTerms: strongAccountSearchTerms(allCandidates.length ? allCandidates : [exactMatch.account_name]) } } // Pass 2: first significant word of an assigned account appears in the // task text as a whole word — catches regional/divisional variants // ("Gulf Oil Philippines" for assigned account "Gulf Oil Ltd."). const fuzzyMatch = assignedAccounts .filter(a => { if (!a.account_name) return false const firstWord = a.account_name.split(/\s+/).find(w => !ACCOUNT_NAME_STOPWORDS.has(w.toLowerCase().replace(/\./g, ''))) if (!firstWord || firstWord.length < 3) return false const wordRe = new RegExp('\\b' + firstWord.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + '\\b', 'i') return wordRe.test(taskText) }) .sort((a, b) => b.account_name.length - a.account_name.length)[0] if (fuzzyMatch) { return { displayName: fuzzyMatch.account_name, matchedAssignedAccount: true, allCandidates, searchTerms: strongAccountSearchTerms(allCandidates.length ? allCandidates : [fuzzyMatch.account_name]) } } // Pass 3: edit-distance fuzzy match — catches typos and misspellings. // "Rekkit" → "Reckitt" (edit distance 1), "Lactalis" → "Lactalis" etc. // Only applies when the task has at least one candidate of reasonable length. // We compare normalised (lowercase, no punctuation) forms. // Edit distance threshold: ≤ 2 for names ≥ 6 chars, ≤ 1 for shorter names. const levDist = (a: string, b: string): number => { const m = a.length, n = b.length const dp: number[][] = Array.from({length: m+1}, (_, i) => Array.from({length: n+1}, (_, j) => i === 0 ? j : j === 0 ? i : 0)) for (let i = 1; i <= m; i++) for (let j = 1; j <= n; j++) dp[i][j] = a[i-1] === b[j-1] ? dp[i-1][j-1] : 1 + Math.min(dp[i-1][j], dp[i][j-1], dp[i-1][j-1]) return dp[m][n] } const typoMatch = assignedAccounts.find(a => { if (!a.account_name) return false const aNorm = a.account_name.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z]/g, '') // Compare against each candidate extracted from the task return allCandidates.some(c => { const cNorm = c.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z]/g, '') if (cNorm.length < 4 || aNorm.length < 4) return false const threshold = Math.max(aNorm.length, cNorm.length) >= 8 ? 2 : 1 return levDist(cNorm, aNorm) <= threshold }) }) if (typoMatch) { return { displayName: typoMatch.account_name, matchedAssignedAccount: true, allCandidates, searchTerms: strongAccountSearchTerms(allCandidates.length ? allCandidates : [typoMatch.account_name]) } } // Pass 4: no assigned account matched — free-text guess. return { displayName: allCandidates[0] || '', matchedAssignedAccount: false, allCandidates, searchTerms: strongAccountSearchTerms(allCandidates) } } function strongAccountSearchTerms(allCandidates: string[]): string[] { const strong = allCandidates.filter(c => !GENERIC_ACCOUNT_WORDS.has(c.toLowerCase())) return strong.length ? strong : allCandidates // fall back if filtering removed everything } // ── IMPROVED: Score how well an email/calendar event matches a task ─────────── function scoreMatch(taskText: string, candidates: string[], subject: string, toField: string, snippet: string): number { const taskLower = taskText.toLowerCase() const subjectLower = (subject || '').toLowerCase() const toLower = (toField || '').toLowerCase() const snippetLower = (snippet || '').toLowerCase() let score = 0 for (const candidate of candidates) { const cLower = candidate.toLowerCase() // Exact match in subject = strongest signal — works for both external // outreach ("Re: Ferrero Proposal") and internal handoffs ("Ferrero NDA status"). if (subjectLower.includes(cLower)) score += 12 // Match in body/snippet — equally strong, since internal emails about an // account often name it in the body rather than the subject or To field. if (snippetLower.includes(cLower)) score += 10 // Match in To field (external prospect's domain or name) — useful but not // required, since internal emails (e.g. to a colleague) won't have this. if (toLower.includes(cLower)) score += 6 // Partial match (first 4+ chars) — weak signal, kept as a tiebreaker only. if (cLower.length >= 4 && subjectLower.includes(cLower.slice(0, 4))) score += 2 } return score } // ── notetakerGmailQueryFragment: Gmail search OR clause for all notetakers ─── // Single source of truth — used across local_intelligence, extract_intelligence, // and scan_notetaker_emails. Add new tools here once, propagates everywhere. const NOTETAKER_SENDER_DOMAINS = [ 'fireflies.ai','fathom.video','otter.ai','tldv.io','notes.microsoft.com', 'gong.io','chorus.ai','grain.com','grain.co','granola.ai','rev.com', 'zoom.us','avoma.com','wudpecker.io','sembly.ai','supernormal.com', 'krisp.ai','read.ai','noty.ai','superhuman.com','clari.com' ] const NOTETAKER_SUBJECT_PATTERNS = [ 'meeting notes','meeting recap','meeting summary','call summary', 'call notes','transcript','recording summary','meeting minutes', 'notes from','summary of your call','your meeting recap','meeting report' ] function notetakerGmailQueryFragment(): string { const senders = NOTETAKER_SENDER_DOMAINS.map(d => 'from:' + d).join(' OR ') const subjects = NOTETAKER_SUBJECT_PATTERNS.map(s => 'subject:"' + s + '"').join(' OR ') return '(' + senders + ' OR ' + subjects + ')' } // Any code that does `someJson?.find(...)` or `.length` on a raw fetch().json() // result without this guard will throw "X.find is not a function" whenever // Postgrest errors (bad column, RLS denial, etc.) instead of surfacing the // real error. Always pass REST responses through this before using array methods. function asArray(json: unknown): any[] { return Array.isArray(json) ? json : [] } // Detects Google's "token doesn't have the scope we need" response. This means // the stored access/refresh token was granted without gmail.readonly — usually // because the user partially approved the consent screen, or connected before // the scope list changed. Refreshing the token does NOT fix this; the user // must disconnect and reconnect Gmail to re-grant the correct scopes. function isScopeError(json: any): boolean { const reason = json?.error?.details?.find?.((d: any) => d.reason)?.reason ?? json?.error?.errors?.[0]?.reason return json?.error?.code === 403 && ( reason === 'ACCESS_TOKEN_SCOPE_INSUFFICIENT' || reason === 'insufficientPermissions' || String(json?.error?.message || '').includes('insufficient authentication scopes') ) } // Detects Gemini's "you've hit your daily/per-minute quota" response. This is // a billing/plan limit, not a transient network blip — on the free tier it's // commonly capped at 20 requests/day for a model, so a single extraction run // over many accounts/emails can exhaust it quickly. We retry briefly (Gemini // tells us exactly how long to wait via retryDelay) but if it's still // exhausted after that, there is nothing more retrying will do — the caller // should stop burning further calls and surface a clear "quota exhausted" // signal instead of failing once per remaining email. function isGeminiQuotaError(json: any): boolean { return json?.error?.code === 429 || json?.error?.status === 'RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED' } function getGeminiRetryDelayMs(json: any): number { const detail = json?.error?.details?.find?.((d: any) => d['@type']?.includes('RetryInfo')) const raw = detail?.retryDelay // e.g. "25s" if (!raw) return 5000 const secs = parseFloat(String(raw).replace('s', '')) return isNaN(secs) ? 5000 : Math.min(Math.ceil(secs * 1000) + 500, 30000) } // Calls Gemini with one retry on a quota/rate-limit response, waiting the // time Gemini itself recommends. Returns the parsed response JSON either way // — caller still needs to check isGeminiQuotaError on the result, since a // second 429 means we should give up rather than retry indefinitely. async function callGeminiWithRetry(url: string, body: any): Promise { const res1 = await fetch(url, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify(body) }) const data1 = await res1.json() if (!isGeminiQuotaError(data1)) return data1 await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, getGeminiRetryDelayMs(data1))) const res2 = await fetch(url, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify(body) }) return await res2.json() } // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // UNIFIED GMAIL TOKEN REFRESH — single source of truth, replacing 7 // separately hand-copied refresh blocks that all shared the same blind // spot: if Google's refresh_token grant itself failed (revoked token, // expired refresh_token, bad client credentials — any reason), every copy // of this code silently kept using the OLD, already-expired access_token // and proceeded anyway. That produces a 401 UNAUTHENTICATED on every // subsequent Gmail API call, which (before this fix) had no error handling // of its own — so the whole action would just look like "found: 0 // evidence everywhere" with the real cause buried in an unread API error. // // This helper makes refresh failure an explicit, checkable outcome instead // of a silent pass-through. interface TokenRefreshResult { accessToken: string refreshed: boolean // True if a refresh was attempted (token was expired/near-expiry) AND it // failed to produce a new access token. Callers MUST check this and stop // with a clear "reconnect Gmail" message rather than proceeding — the // access_token they'd otherwise use is known-dead at this point. refreshFailed: boolean refreshError?: any } async function getValidGmailToken( tokenRow: { access_token: string, refresh_token: string, expires_at: string, user_id?: string }, targetUserId: string, SUPABASE_URL: string, SB_SERVICE: string, GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID: string, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET: string ): Promise { // ── Clock-drift-safe validity check ──────────────────────────────────── // Deno's Date.now() runs ~1 hour behind real UTC in some Supabase edge // function environments. We cannot trust it for expiry comparisons. // Instead: ask the database "is this token still valid?" using PostgreSQL's // own clock (now()), which is always correct UTC. // We also use a 10-minute buffer so we proactively refresh before expiry // rather than waiting until Gmail calls start returning 401. let stillValid = false try { const checkRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/rpc/is_gmail_token_valid', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ p_user_id: targetUserId }) } ) stillValid = await checkRes.json() === true } catch(e) { // If the DB check fails, fall back to attempting a refresh stillValid = false } if (stillValid) { return { accessToken: tokenRow.access_token, refreshed: false, refreshFailed: false } } // ── Token expired or near-expiry — refresh it ────────────────────────── const body = new URLSearchParams() body.set('client_id', GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID) body.set('client_secret', GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET) body.set('refresh_token', tokenRow.refresh_token) body.set('grant_type', 'refresh_token') const ref = await fetch('https://oauth2.googleapis.com/token', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' }, body }) const refData = await ref.json() if (!refData.access_token) { return { accessToken: '', refreshed: false, refreshFailed: true, refreshError: refData.error || refData } } // ── Save refreshed token using DB clock for expires_at ───────────────── const expiresInSeconds = refData.expires_in ?? 3600 await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/rpc/update_gmail_token_expiry', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ p_user_id: targetUserId, p_access_token: refData.access_token, p_expires_in: expiresInSeconds }) }) return { accessToken: refData.access_token, refreshed: true, refreshFailed: false } } // ── getValidMicrosoftToken ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Microsoft OAuth 2.0 token refresh — same pattern as getValidGmailToken but // using the Microsoft identity platform endpoint. Works for personal accounts // (Hotmail, Outlook.com) and work/school accounts (M365, Exchange Online). async function getValidMicrosoftToken( tokenRow: { access_token: string, refresh_token: string, expires_at: string, user_id?: string }, targetUserId: string, SUPABASE_URL: string, SB_SERVICE: string ): Promise { const MS_CLIENT_ID = Deno.env.get('MICROSOFT_CLIENT_ID') ?? '' const MS_CLIENT_SECRET = Deno.env.get('MICROSOFT_CLIENT_SECRET') ?? '' if (!MS_CLIENT_ID || !MS_CLIENT_SECRET) { return { accessToken: '', refreshed: false, refreshFailed: true, refreshError: 'MICROSOFT_CLIENT_ID / MICROSOFT_CLIENT_SECRET not configured in edge function secrets' } } // Check if still valid using DB clock (same pattern as Google — avoids Deno clock drift) let stillValid = false try { const checkRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/rpc/is_gmail_token_valid', // reuse same DB function — it checks by user_id { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ p_user_id: targetUserId }) } ) stillValid = await checkRes.json() === true } catch(e) { stillValid = false } if (stillValid) return { accessToken: tokenRow.access_token, refreshed: false, refreshFailed: false } // Refresh using Microsoft identity platform token endpoint // 'common' tenant supports both personal (Hotmail) and work accounts (M365) const body = new URLSearchParams() body.set('client_id', MS_CLIENT_ID) body.set('client_secret', MS_CLIENT_SECRET) body.set('refresh_token', tokenRow.refresh_token) body.set('grant_type', 'refresh_token') body.set('scope', 'Mail.Read Calendars.Read offline_access User.Read') const ref = await fetch('https://login.microsoftonline.com/common/oauth2/v2.0/token', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' }, body }) const refData = await ref.json() if (!refData.access_token) { return { accessToken: '', refreshed: false, refreshFailed: true, refreshError: refData.error_description || refData.error || refData } } const expiresInSeconds = refData.expires_in ?? 3600 await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/rpc/update_gmail_token_expiry', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ p_user_id: targetUserId, p_access_token: refData.access_token, p_expires_in: expiresInSeconds }) }) // Also save the new refresh_token if Microsoft rotated it if (refData.refresh_token && refData.refresh_token !== tokenRow.refresh_token) { await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&provider=eq.microsoft', { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ refresh_token: refData.refresh_token }) }) } return { accessToken: refData.access_token, refreshed: true, refreshFailed: false } } // ── getEmailToken ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Provider-aware router: fetches and validates the token for the right provider. // All callers that previously called getValidGmailToken directly can call this // instead and stop caring which email provider the rep uses. async function getEmailToken( targetUserId: string, SUPABASE_URL: string, SB_SERVICE: string, GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID: string, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET: string ): Promise<{ tokenResult: TokenRefreshResult, provider: string, email: string }> { const tokRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&select=*&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const tokRows = asArray(await tokRes.json()) if (!tokRows?.length) return { tokenResult: { accessToken: '', refreshed: false, refreshFailed: true, refreshError: 'not_connected' }, provider: '', email: '' } const tokRow = tokRows[0] const provider = tokRow.provider || 'google' const email = tokRow.email || '' if (provider === 'microsoft') { const tokenResult = await getValidMicrosoftToken(tokRow, targetUserId, SUPABASE_URL, SB_SERVICE) return { tokenResult, provider: 'microsoft', email } } else { const tokenResult = await getValidGmailToken(tokRow, targetUserId, SUPABASE_URL, SB_SERVICE, GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET) return { tokenResult, provider: 'google', email } } } // ── Microsoft Graph search functions ───────────────────────────────────────── // Drop-in equivalents for the Gmail API calls used in account_coverage and IVR. // Same inputs/outputs — callers don't need to know which API they're hitting. // Search sent items — equivalent to Gmail "in:sent" query async function searchOutlookSent( accessToken: string, searchTerms: string[], // account name / keywords brandRoot: string, // for domain-based recipient matching fromEpoch: number, // Unix timestamp toEpoch: number ): Promise<{ count: number, messages: any[] }> { if (!searchTerms.length && !brandRoot) return { count: 0, messages: [] } const fromISO = new Date(fromEpoch * 1000).toISOString() const toISO = new Date(toEpoch * 1000).toISOString() // Build OData filter — date range is reliable; we filter by account name client-side // (Graph's $search + $filter combination is unreliable across account types) const filter = `sentDateTime ge ${fromISO} and sentDateTime le ${toISO}` const url = 'https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/me/mailFolders/SentItems/messages' + '?$filter=' + encodeURIComponent(filter) + '&$top=50&$select=id,subject,toRecipients,sentDateTime,internetMessageId' const res = await fetch(url, { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } }) if (!res.ok) return { count: 0, messages: [] } const data = await res.json() const messages = data.value || [] // Client-side filter: account name in subject OR recipient domain matches brand root const lowerTerms = searchTerms.map(t => t.toLowerCase()) const filtered = messages.filter((m: any) => { const subject = (m.subject || '').toLowerCase() const recipients = (m.toRecipients || []).map((r: any) => (r.emailAddress?.address || '').toLowerCase() ).join(' ') const matchesName = lowerTerms.some(t => subject.includes(t) || recipients.includes(t)) const matchesDomain = brandRoot.length >= 4 && recipients.includes(brandRoot) return matchesName || matchesDomain }) return { count: filtered.length, messages: filtered } } // Search inbox — equivalent to Gmail "in:inbox from:{domain}" query for reply detection async function searchOutlookInbox( accessToken: string, searchTerms: string[], brandRoot: string, fromEpoch: number, toEpoch: number ): Promise<{ count: number, messages: any[] }> { const fromISO = new Date(fromEpoch * 1000).toISOString() const toISO = new Date(toEpoch * 1000).toISOString() const filter = `receivedDateTime ge ${fromISO} and receivedDateTime le ${toISO}` const url = 'https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/me/mailFolders/Inbox/messages' + '?$filter=' + encodeURIComponent(filter) + '&$top=20&$select=id,subject,from,receivedDateTime,bodyPreview' const res = await fetch(url, { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } }) if (!res.ok) return { count: 0, messages: [] } const data = await res.json() const messages = data.value || [] const lowerTerms = searchTerms.map(t => t.toLowerCase()) const filtered = messages.filter((m: any) => { const fromEmail = (m.from?.emailAddress?.address || '').toLowerCase() const fromName = (m.from?.emailAddress?.name || '').toLowerCase() const subject = (m.subject || '').toLowerCase() return lowerTerms.some(t => fromEmail.includes(t) || fromName.includes(t) || subject.includes(t)) || (brandRoot.length >= 4 && fromEmail.includes(brandRoot)) }) return { count: filtered.length, messages: filtered } } // Search calendar — equivalent to Google Calendar events query async function searchOutlookCalendar( accessToken: string, searchTerms: string[], fromDate: string, // YYYY-MM-DD toDate: string ): Promise<{ events: any[] }> { const url = 'https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/me/calendarView' + '?startDateTime=' + encodeURIComponent(fromDate + 'T00:00:00Z') + '&endDateTime=' + encodeURIComponent(toDate + 'T23:59:59Z') + '&$top=50&$select=id,subject,start,end,attendees,bodyPreview,organizer' const res = await fetch(url, { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } }) if (!res.ok) return { events: [] } const data = await res.json() const events = data.value || [] // Filter to events mentioning the account const lowerTerms = searchTerms.map(t => t.toLowerCase()) const filtered = events.filter((e: any) => { const text = (e.subject + ' ' + (e.bodyPreview || '') + (e.attendees || []).map((a: any) => a.emailAddress?.address || '').join(' ')).toLowerCase() return lowerTerms.some(t => text.includes(t)) }) return { events: filtered } } // Standard error response for a dead/unrefreshable Gmail connection — // distinct from isScopeError (which means the token IS valid but lacks a // permission) and from "Gmail not connected" (no token row exists at all). // This means a token row exists but Google rejected the refresh attempt — // almost always because the user revoked access, changed their Google // password, or the refresh_token was invalidated after prolonged inactivity. // Reconnecting (not just refreshing) is the only fix. function gmailReconnectNeededResponse(isManager: boolean, gmailEmail?: string) { return jsonResponse({ connected: true, reconnectNeeded: true, gmailEmail: gmailEmail || '', error: (isManager ? 'This rep\u2019s' : 'Your') + ' Gmail connection has expired or been revoked and could not be refreshed. ' + (isManager ? 'They need' : 'Go') + ' to the SAM tab and click "Connect Gmail" again to fully re-authenticate \u2014 this is different from the permissions-scope issue and requires a fresh sign-in, not just re-granting access.' }, 401) } Deno.serve(async (req) => { if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders }) if (req.method !== 'POST') return jsonResponse({ error: 'Method not allowed' }, 405) try { const SUPABASE_URL = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL') ?? '$' + (apolloCompany.total_funding / 1e6).toFixed(0) + 'M raised' : null, company_technologies: apolloCompany?.technologies?.slice(0, 8).map((t: any) => t.name || t) || [], intent_signals: intentSignals, summary: geminiSummary, verdict: buyingVerdict, signals: geminiSignals, regional_signals: regionalSignals, regional_summary: regionalSummary, country_signals: countrySignals, country_summary: countrySummary, deal_region: dealRegion || null, _debug: { engine: orgCfg.ai_engine, hasKey: !!orgCfg.ai_api_key, companyName, signalCount: geminiSignals.length, summaryLen: geminiSummary.length } }) } if (action === 'lusha_debug') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { email } = payload const getKey = async (p: string) => { const k = 'enrichment_' + p + '_key' const u = asArray(await (await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_settings?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&key=eq.' + k + '&select=value&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } })).json()) if (u[0]?.value) return u[0].value const o = asArray(await (await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_settings?org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&key=eq.' + k + '&select=value&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } })).json()) return o[0]?.value || null } const lushaKey = await getKey('lusha') if (!lushaKey) return jsonResponse({ error: 'No Lusha key found' }) const res = await fetch('https://api.lusha.com/v2/person?email=' + encodeURIComponent(email), { headers: { 'api_key': lushaKey } }) const raw = await res.json() return jsonResponse({ ok: true, status: res.status, raw, keys: raw.data ? Priority 2: first entry in additional_domains array if (!domain && row.additional_domains?.length) { domain = (row.additional_domains[0] || '').replace(/^https?:\/\//, '').replace(/\/.*$/, '').toLowerCase().trim() } // Priority 3: derive from account name // "Ferrero India IR" → strip location/deal qualifiers → "ferrero.com" // "Pladis Global" → "pladis.com" if (!domain && row.account_name) { const stopWords = ['india','middle','east','mena','africa','sea','apac','emea','global','group', ok: true, domain, account_name: row.account_name || '' }) } if (action === 'enrich_account') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { account_id, account_name, '').toLowerCase().trim() if (!acctDomain && acctRow0.additional_domains?.length) { acctDomain = (acctRow0.additional_domains[0] || '').replace(/^https?:\/\//, '').replace(/\/.*$/, || '').toLowerCase().split(/[\s\-_\/]+/).filter((w: string) => w.length > 2 && !stopWords2.includes(w)) if (np[0]) acctDomain = np[0].replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '') + '.com' } const acctNameNorm = fetch('https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + encodeURIComponent('in:sent to:@' + acctDomain) + '&maxResults=30', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + at } }) const (Date.now() - new Date(act.last).getTime()) / 86400000 : 999 return { org_id: orgCfg.org_id, account_id, email: c.email, full_name: c.full_name || c.email.split('@')[0].replace(/[._-]/g, ' ').replace(/\b\w/g, (l: string) => l.toUpperCase()), first_name: c.first_name || null, last_name: c.last_name || null, title: c.title || null, seniority: c.seniority || null, department: c.department || null, location: c.location || null, linkedin_url: c.linkedin_url || null, phone: c.phone || null, provider: c.provider, enriched_at: now, contact_count: act.count || 0, last_contacted_at: act.last || null, signal_status: daysSince <= 7 ? 'engaged' : daysSince <= 30 ? 'active' : act.last ? 'dark' : 'uncontacted' } }) const insertRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/stakeholders', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'resolution=merge-duplicates,return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify(rows) }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, count: rows.length, discovered: discoveredEmails.length, enriched: rows.filter((r: any) => r.provider !== 'gmail_inferred').length, providers: [...new Set(rows.map((r: any) => r.provider))], domain: acctDomain, contacts: rows.map((r: any) => ({ full_name: r.full_name, title: r.title, email: r.email, provider: r.provider })) }) } if (action === 'save_stakeholder_role') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? Pure DB + rules, runs on your own data. // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // ── compute_deal_health ───────────────────────────────────────────────── // Computes health_score (0-100) for every open deal in the org. // Inputs: signal_score, MEDDPICC completeness, stakeholder recency, // days since last contact, close date proximity. // No AI. Runs nightly or on demand. Feeds forecast + coaching alerts. if (action === 'compute_deal_health') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey // Get all open deals for this org const dealsRes = await Signal score (0-30 pts) ─────────────────────────────────────── const ss = Math.min(deal.signal_score || 0, 100) score += Math.round(ss * 0.30) // ── MEDDPICC completeness (0-25 pts) ───────────────────────────── const m = meddMap[deal.id] if (m) { const fields = ['metrics_status','economic_buyer_status','decision_criteria_status', 'decision_process_status','paper_process_status','identified_pain_status', 'champion_status','competition_status'] const filled = fields.filter(f => m[f] === 'confirmed' || m[f] === 'partial').length score += Math.round((filled / 8) * 25) } // ── Stakeholder recency (0-20 pts) ─────────────────────────────── const stk = stkMap[deal.id] if (stk?.lastContact) { const daysSince = (now - new Date(stk.lastContact).getTime()) / 86400000 if (daysSince <= 7) score += 20 else if (daysSince <= 14) score += 14 else if (daysSince <= 30) score += 8 else score += 2 } // ── Champion identified (0-10 pts) ─────────────────────────────── if (stk?.hasChampion) score += 10 // ── Close date proximity (0-15 pts, negative near but dark) ────── if (deal.expected_close) { const daysToClose = (new Date(deal.expected_close).getTime() - now) / 86400000 if (daysToClose > 0 && daysToClose <= 30) score += 15 else if (daysToClose > 30 && daysToClose <= 60) score += 10 else if (daysToClose > 60) score += 5 // Penalty: close soon but no recent contact if (daysToClose <= 30 && stk?.lastContact) { const daysDark = (now - new Date(stk.lastContact).getTime()) / 86400000 if (daysDark > 14) score -= 10 } } score = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, score)) // Append to signal_score_history const histEntry = { date: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0], score, health: score } updates.push(fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + deal.id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ health_score: score, // Append to history — keep last 90 entries signal_score_history: { type: 'jsonb_concat', value: histEntry } }) } )) } // Batch update health scores (simpler than jsonb_concat via REST) for (const deal of deals) { const stk = stkMap[deal.id] const m = meddMap[deal.id] let sc = 0 const ss = Math.min(deal.signal_score || 0, 100) sc += Math.round(ss * 0.30) if (m) { const fields = ['metrics_status','economic_buyer_status','decision_criteria_status','decision_process_status','paper_process_status','identified_pain_status','champion_status','competition_status'] sc += Math.round((fields.filter(f => m[f]==='confirmed'||m[f]==='partial').length / 8) * 25) } if (stk?.lastContact) { const d = (now - new Date(stk.lastContact).getTime()) / 86400000 sc += d<=7?20:d<=14?14:d<=30?8:2 } if (stk?.hasChampion) sc += 10 if (deal.expected_close) { const d2c = (new Date(deal.expected_close).getTime() - now) / 86400000 sc += d2c>0&&d2c<=30?15:d2c<=60?10:5 if (d2c<=30&&stk?.lastContact&&(now-new Date(stk.lastContact).getTime())/86400000>14) sc -= 10 } sc = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, sc)) const histEntry = JSON.stringify({ date: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0], score: deal.signal_score||0, health: sc }) await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/rpc/append_health_history', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ p_account_id: deal.id, p_entry: histEntry, p_health_score: sc }) }).catch(() => { // Fallback: just update health_score return fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + deal.id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ health_score: sc }) }) }) } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, dealsScored: deals.length }) } // ── generate_coaching_alerts ──────────────────────────────────────────── // Rules-based coaching alerts. No AI. Generated on demand or nightly. // Types: dark_account | no_champion | meddpicc_gap | close_at_risk | velocity_stall if (action === 'generate_coaching_alerts') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const now = Date.now() const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] // Clear expired/stale alerts for this org first await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/coaching_alerts?org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&expires_at=lt.' + today, { method: 'DELETE', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) // Get all open deals with rep + close date const dealsRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&deal_value=not.is.null&deal_status=not.in.(won,lost)' + '&select=id,account_name,deal_value_usd,expected_close,signal_score,health_score,user_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const deals = asArray(await dealsRes.json()) // Get user profiles (manager info) const profilesRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&select=user_id,manager_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const profiles = asArray(await profilesRes.json()) const managerMap: Record = {} profiles.forEach((p: any) => { managerMap[p.user_id] = p.manager_id }) // Get stakeholder last contact per deal const stkRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/stakeholders?org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&select=account_id,last_contacted_at,meddpicc_role', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const stks = asArray(await stkRes.json()) const stkDeal: Record = {} stks.forEach((s: any) => { const ex = stkDeal[s.account_id] if (!ex || (s.last_contacted_at||'') > ex.lastContact) stkDeal[s.account_id] = { lastContact: s.last_contacted_at||'', hasChampion: ex?.hasChampion||s.meddpicc_role==='champion' } else if (s.meddpicc_role==='champion') stkDeal[s.account_id].hasChampion = true }) // Get MEDDPICC per deal const meddRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/meddpicc?org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&select=account_id,economic_buyer_status,champion_status,identified_pain_status,decision_criteria_status', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const meddMap: Record = {} asArray(await meddRes.json()).forEach((m: any) => { meddMap[m.account_id] = m }) const alerts: any[] = [] const expires = new Date(Date.now() + 7*86400000).toISOString() for (const deal of deals) { const stk = stkDeal[deal.id] const medd = meddMap[deal.id] const daysToClose = deal.expected_close ? (new Date(deal.expected_close).getTime() - now) / 86400000 : 999 const daysDark = stk?.lastContact ? (now - new Date(stk.lastContact).getTime()) / 86400000 : 999 const val = deal.deal_value_usd || 0 const managerId = managerMap[deal.user_id] const base = { org_id: orgCfg.org_id, account_id: deal.id, rep_user_id: deal.user_id, manager_id: managerId, deal_value_usd: val, due_date: deal.expected_close, expires_at: expires } // RULE 1: Dark account — no contact >14 days, deal closing <30 days if (daysDark > 14 && daysToClose < 30 && daysToClose > 0) { alerts.push({ ...base, alert_type: 'dark_account', severity: 'high', title: `${deal.account_name} going dark — ${Math.round(daysToClose)} days to close`, detail: `Last contact was ${Math.round(daysDark)} days ago. Close date is ${deal.expected_close}. Re-engage now.` }) } // RULE 2: No champion on high-value deal if (!stk?.hasChampion && (!medd || medd.champion_status !== 'confirmed') && val > 50000) { alerts.push({ ...base, alert_type: 'no_champion', severity: 'high', title: `No champion on $${Math.round(val/1000)}K deal — ${deal.account_name}`, detail: 'High-value deal has no internal advocate identified. Ask your contact who will champion this internally.' }) } // RULE 3: Economic buyer missing, deal closing <45 days if (medd && medd.economic_buyer_status !== 'confirmed' && daysToClose < 45 && val > 30000) { alerts.push({ ...base, alert_type: 'meddpicc_gap', severity: 'medium', title: `Economic buyer unknown — ${deal.account_name} closes in ${Math.round(daysToClose)}d`, detail: 'Who signs the purchase order has not been identified. Clarify this before submitting proposal.' }) } // RULE 4: Close date passed or within 7 days, deal still open if (daysToClose < 7 && daysToClose > -30) { alerts.push({ ...base, alert_type: 'close_at_risk', severity: 'high', title: `Close date ${daysToClose < 0 ? 'PASSED' : 'in ' + Math.round(daysToClose) + 'd'} — ${deal.account_name}`, detail: daysToClose < 0 ? `Deal was supposed to close ${Math.abs(Math.round(daysToClose))} days ago. Update close date or action immediately.` : `${deal.account_name} is due to close in ${Math.round(daysToClose)} days. Confirm status with stakeholders.` }) } // RULE 5: Long account silence on any deal (>21 days, no close date pressure) if (daysDark > 21 && daysToClose > 30) { alerts.push({ ...base, alert_type: 'velocity_stall', severity: 'low', title: `${deal.account_name} inactive for ${Math.round(daysDark)} days`, detail: `No contact recorded in ${Math.round(daysDark)} days. Deal may be stalling — reach out to maintain momentum.` }) } } // Upsert alerts (delete existing same-type for same account, then insert) let inserted = 0 for (const alert of alerts) { // Skip if same alert type already exists for this account const checkRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/coaching_alerts?account_id=eq.' + alert.account_id + '&alert_type=eq.' + alert.alert_type + '&dismissed=eq.false&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const existing = asArray(await checkRes.json()) if (existing.length) continue // already have this alert await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/coaching_alerts', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify(alert) }) inserted++ } // Log to activity_log await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/activity_log', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: orgCfg.org_id, user_id: userId, action: 'generate_coaching_alerts', entity_type: 'system', detail: `Generated ${inserted} new alerts from ${deals.length} deals` }) }).catch(() => {}) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, alertsGenerated: inserted, dealsChecked: deals.length }) } // ── get_coaching_alerts ───────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns active coaching alerts for the current user (or all if manager) if (action === 'get_coaching_alerts') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const role = payload.role || callerRole const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] let filter = `org_id=eq.${orgCfg.org_id}&dismissed=eq.false&expires_at=gte.${today}&order=severity.desc,created_at.desc&limit=50` if (!['manager','director','executive','admin','super_admin'].includes(role)) { filter += '&rep_user_id=eq.' + userId } const res = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/coaching_alerts?' + filter, { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const alerts = asArray(await res.json()) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, alerts }) } // ── dismiss_alert ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── if (action === 'dismiss_alert') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/coaching_alerts?id=eq.' + payload.alert_id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ dismissed: true }) }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true }) } // ── compute_forecast ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Builds verified forecast from health scores. No AI. // verified: health >= 70 | nurture: 40-69 | at_risk: < 40 if (action === 'compute_forecast') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] const startOfMonth = today.slice(0, 7) + '-01' const dealsRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&deal_value=not.is.null&deal_status=not.in.(won,lost)' + '&select=id,deal_value_usd,close_probability,health_score,signal_score', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const deals = asArray(await dealsRes.json()) const wonRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&deal_status=eq.won&deal_closed_at=gte.' + startOfMonth + '&select=deal_actual_value_usd,deal_value_usd', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const lostRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&deal_status=eq.lost&deal_closed_at=gte.' + startOfMonth + '&select=deal_value_usd', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const wonDeals = asArray(await wonRes.json()) const lostDeals = asArray(await lostRes.json()) let verified = 0, atRisk = 0, nurture = 0, total = 0, atRiskCount = 0 for (const d of deals) { const val = d.deal_value_usd || 0 const prob = (d.close_probability || 50) / 100 const weighted = val * prob total += val const h = d.health_score ??
