d.signal_score ?? 50 if (h >= 70) { verified += weighted } else if (h >= 40) { nurture += weighted } else { atRisk += weighted; atRiskCount++ } } const wonMtd = wonDeals.reduce((s: number, d: any) => s + (d.deal_actual_value_usd || d.deal_value_usd || 0), 0) const lostMtd = lostDeals.reduce((s: number, d: any) => s + (d.deal_value_usd || 0), 0) // Snapshot to DB const snapshot = { org_id: orgCfg.org_id, snapshot_date: today, total_pipeline_usd: Math.round(total), verified_usd: Math.round(verified), at_risk_usd: Math.round(atRisk), nurture_usd: Math.round(nurture), won_mtd_usd: Math.round(wonMtd), lost_mtd_usd: Math.round(lostMtd), deal_count: deals.length, at_risk_count: atRiskCount } await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/forecast_snapshots', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'resolution=merge-duplicates,return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify(snapshot) }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, ...snapshot }) } // ── refresh_stakeholder_signals ───────────────────────────────────────── // Re-scans Gmail for activity on all known stakeholder emails. // Updates last_contacted_at, contact_count, signal_status per contact. // Runs for a specific account or all accounts (manager call). if (action === 'refresh_stakeholder_signals') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { account_id } = payload // Get Gmail token for this user const tokRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=*&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const tokRows = asArray(await tokRes.json()) if (!tokRows.length) return jsonResponse({ ok: false, error: 'Gmail not connected' }) const provider = tokRows[0].provider || 'google' const tokenResult = provider === 'microsoft' ? await getValidMicrosoftToken(tokRows[0], userId, SUPABASE_URL, SVC) : await getValidGmailToken(tokRows[0], userId, SUPABASE_URL, SVC, GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET) if (tokenResult.refreshFailed) return jsonResponse({ ok: false, error: 'Gmail token refresh failed' }) const at = tokenResult.accessToken // Get stakeholders to refresh let stkFilter = 'org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id if (account_id) stkFilter += '&account_id=eq.' + account_id stkFilter += '&email=not.is.null&select=id,email,account_id' const stkRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/stakeholders?' + stkFilter + '&limit=100', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const stakeholders = asArray(await stkRes.json()) let refreshed = 0 for (const stk of stakeholders) { try { const q = encodeURIComponent('to:' + stk.email + ' OR from:' + stk.email) const mRes = await fetch('https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + q + '&maxResults=20', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + at } }) const mData = await mRes.json() const msgs = mData.messages || [] if (!msgs.length) continue // Get date of most recent message const latestRes = await fetch('https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages/' + msgs[0].id + '?format=metadata&metadataHeaders=Date', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + at } }) const latestData = await latestRes.json() const dateHdr = latestData.payload?.headers?.find((h: any) => h.name === 'Date')?.value || '' const lastDate = new Date(dateHdr) const lastDateStr = isNaN(lastDate.getTime()) ? '' : lastDate.toISOString().split('T')[0] const daysSince = lastDateStr ? (Date.now() - lastDate.getTime()) / 86400000 : 999 const status = daysSince <= 7 ? 'engaged' : daysSince <= 30 ? 'active' : daysSince <= 90 ? 'dark' : 'uncontacted' await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/stakeholders?id=eq.' + stk.id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ last_contacted_at: lastDateStr || null, contact_count: msgs.length, signal_status: status }) }) refreshed++ } catch(e) {} } // Update account refresh timestamp if (account_id) { await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + account_id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ last_stakeholder_refresh: new Date().toISOString() }) }) } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, refreshed, total: stakeholders.length }) } // ── infer_meddpicc_from_transcripts ───────────────────────────────────── // Scans meeting transcripts for MEDDPICC signals. Rules-based NLP. // No external AI — keyword + pattern matching on existing transcript text. if (action === 'infer_meddpicc_from_transcripts') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { account_id } = payload // Get transcripts for this account const txRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/meeting_transcripts?account_id=eq.' + account_id + '&select=id,summary,action_items,key_quotes,budget_signals,objections,participants&order=meeting_date.desc&limit=10', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const txRows = asArray(await txRes.json()) if (!txRows.length) return jsonResponse({ ok: false, error: 'No transcripts found for this account' }) // Combine all text for analysis const allText = txRows.map((t: any) => [t.summary, t.action_items, t.key_quotes, t.budget_signals, t.objections].filter(Boolean).join(' ') ).join(' ').toLowerCase() // Participant names (potential champion/economic buyer) const allParticipants: string[] = txRows.flatMap((t: any) => t.participants || []) const externalParticipants = allParticipants.filter(p => !p.toLowerCase().includes('@') || (!orgCfg.email_provider || !p.toLowerCase().includes(orgCfg.email_provider))) // Rule-based MEDDPICC inference const inferences: Record = {} // Champion — someone who "will advocate", "is pushing for", "is sponsoring" if (/champion|sponsor|advocate|pushing for|driving this|internal support|fighting for/.test(allText)) { inferences['champion_status'] = 'partial' // Try to extract champion name from context const champMatch = allText.match(/(\w+ \w+)\s+(?:will champion|is championing|is sponsoring|will advocate|is driving)/i) if (champMatch) inferences['champion_name'] = champMatch[1] } // Economic buyer — budget authority keywords if (/sign.?off|budget authority|cfo|chief financial|vp finance|approves the|signs the|po approval|purchase order|final approval/.test(allText)) { inferences['economic_buyer_status'] = 'partial' } // Identified pain — explicit problem statements if (/problem|challenge|issue|pain|struggling|inefficien|manual process|losing|costing us|can.t see|no visibility/.test(allText)) { inferences['identified_pain_status'] = 'confirmed' const painMatch = allText.match(/(?:main |key |biggest )?(?:problem|challenge|issue|pain)[^.]*\./i) if (painMatch) inferences['identified_pain_value'] = painMatch[0].slice(0, 200) } // Metrics — outcome numbers mentioned if (/\d+%|\$\d+|reduce.*by|increase.*by|save.*hours|roi|payback|kpi|metric/.test(allText)) { inferences['metrics_status'] = 'partial' const metricMatch = allText.match(/(?:reduce|increase|save|improve)[^.]*\d+[^.]*\./i) if (metricMatch) inferences['metrics_value'] = metricMatch[0].slice(0, 200) } // Competition — competitor mentions const competitors = ['salesforce','hubspot','dynamics','pipedrive','zoho','monday','freshsales','fieldassist','bizom'] const foundComps = competitors.filter(c => allText.includes(c)) if (foundComps.length) { inferences['competition_status'] = 'confirmed' inferences['competition_value'] = 'Mentioned: ' + foundComps.join(', ') } // Decision process — approval chain mentioned if (/it.?sign.?off|legal|procurement|committee|board approval|multiple approvals|stakeholder buy-in/.test(allText)) { inferences['decision_process_status'] = 'partial' } if (!Object.keys(inferences).length) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, inferred: 0, message: 'No clear MEDDPICC signals in transcripts' }) // Get existing MEDDPICC record const meddRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/meddpicc?account_id=eq.' + account_id + '&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const existing = asArray(await meddRes.json())[0] if (existing) { // Only update fields that are currently 'unknown' — don't overwrite human input const checkRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/meddpicc?account_id=eq.' + account_id + '&select=*&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const curr = asArray(await checkRes.json())[0] || {} const safeUpdate: Record = {} for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(inferences)) { if (!curr[k] || curr[k] === 'unknown') safeUpdate[k] = v } if (Object.keys(safeUpdate).length) { await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/meddpicc?account_id=eq.' + account_id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ ...safeUpdate, updated_at: new Date().toISOString(), updated_by: userId }) }) } } else { // Create new MEDDPICC record await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/meddpicc', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: orgCfg.org_id, account_id, ...inferences, updated_at: new Date().toISOString(), updated_by: userId }) }) } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, inferred: Object.keys(inferences).length, fields: inferences }) } if (action === 'get_connector_token') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey // Re-use existing token or generate fresh one const existingRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/mcp_sessions?email=eq.' + encodeURIComponent(orgCfg.email || '') + '&limit=1&select=token,expires_at', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const existing = asArray(await existingRes.json()) // Return existing token if still valid for >1 day if (existing.length && existing[0].expires_at > Date.now() + 86400000) { const host = Deno.env.get('HOST') || 'https://samoratrack.vercel.app' return jsonResponse({ ok: true, token: existing[0].token, host, reused: true }) } // Mint a new token — encode user_id + timestamp for uniqueness const newToken = btoa(userId + ':' + Date.now()).replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '').slice(0, 32) const expiresAt = Date.now() + 7 * 24 * 3600 * 1000 // 7 days // Fetch user email for the session record const profileRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=email', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const profileRows = asArray(await profileRes.json()) const userEmail = profileRows[0]?.email || '' // Need the user's refresh token to store — fetch from gmail_tokens (same auth source) const tokRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=access_token,refresh_token&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const tokRows = asArray(await tokRes.json()) // Store in mcp_sessions — the Vercel connector reads this table await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/mcp_sessions', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'resolution=merge-duplicates,return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify({ token: newToken, access_token: anonKey, // Vercel connector uses this to call edge fn on behalf of user refresh_token: tokRows[0]?.refresh_token || '', expires_at: expiresAt, email: userEmail }) }) // Also store the actual Supabase JWT so the connector can make authenticated calls // We store the user's current JWT — the connector uses it to call the edge function await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/mcp_sessions?token=eq.' + newToken, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ access_token: authHeader.replace('Bearer ', '') }) }) const host = Deno.env.get('HOST') || 'https://samoratrack.vercel.app' return jsonResponse({ ok: true, token: newToken, host, expires_at: expiresAt, reused: false }) } if (action === 'get_email_provider') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const tokRes2 = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=provider,email&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const rows2 = asArray(await tokRes2.json()) if (!rows2?.length) return jsonResponse({ connected: false, provider: null, email: null }) return jsonResponse({ connected: true, provider: rows2[0].provider || 'google', email: rows2[0].email }) } if (action === 'connect_gmail') { const { code, redirect_uri } = payload if (!code) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Missing code' }, 400) const body = new URLSearchParams() body.set('client_id', GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID) body.set('client_secret', GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET) body.set('code', code) body.set('grant_type', 'authorization_code') if (redirect_uri) body.set('redirect_uri', redirect_uri) const tokenRes = await fetch('https://oauth2.googleapis.com/token', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' }, body, }) const tokens = await tokenRes.json() if (!tokens.access_token) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Token exchange failed: ' + JSON.stringify(tokens) }, 400) const profileRes = await fetch('https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/profile', { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${tokens.access_token}` } }) const profile = await profileRes.json() const email = profile?.emailAddress ?? 'unknown' const expiresAt = new Date(Date.now() + (tokens.expires_in ?? 3600) * 1000).toISOString() const { error: dbErr } = await supabase.from('gmail_tokens').upsert({ user_id: userId, access_token: tokens.access_token, refresh_token: tokens.refresh_token, expires_at: expiresAt, email, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() }) if (dbErr) return jsonResponse({ error: dbErr.message }, 500) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, email }) } // ── admin_list_orgs ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns all orgs + their settings for the Samora admin dashboard sidebar. // Gated to samora_admins only — regular users get 403. if (action === 'admin_list_orgs') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const adminCheck = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/samora_admins?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const adminRows = await adminCheck.json() if (!Array.isArray(adminRows) || !adminRows.length) { return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 403) } // Join orgs with their settings in one pass — avoids N+1 fetches const [orgsRes, settingsRes] = await Promise.all([ fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/organisations?select=id,name,org_code,created_at&order=created_at.asc', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }), fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_settings?select=*', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) ]) const orgs = asArray(await orgsRes.json()) const settings = asArray(await settingsRes.json()) const settingsByOrg: Record = {} settings.forEach((s: any) => { settingsByOrg[s.org_id] = s }) const result = orgs.map((o: any) => { const s = settingsByOrg[o.id] || {} return { org_id: o.id, name: o.name, display_name: s.display_name || o.name, org_code: o.org_code, created_at: o.created_at, active: true, settings: { email_provider: s.email_provider || 'gmail', ai_engine: s.ai_engine || 'gemini', ai_model: s.ai_model || 'gemini-2.5-flash', deal_stages: s.deal_stages || [], features: s.features || {}, channels: s.channels || {}, role_labels: s.role_labels || {}, stale_days: s.stale_days || 10, unanswered_days:s.unanswered_days || 3, lookback_days: s.lookback_days || 90, intel_lookback_days: s.intel_lookback_days || 30 // Credentials intentionally omitted — never sent to client } } }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, orgs: result }) } // ── admin_create_org ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Creates a new client organisation + seeds org_settings in one call. // Samora admin only. if (action === 'admin_create_org') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const adminCheck = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/samora_admins?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const adminRows = await adminCheck.json() if (!Array.isArray(adminRows) || !adminRows.length) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 403) const { name, org_code, display_name, default_currency, email_provider, ai_engine } = payload if (!name) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Organisation name is required' }, 400) // Create org in organisations table const orgRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/organisations', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=representation' }, body: JSON.stringify({ name: name, org_code: org_code || name.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '').slice(0, 12) }) }) const orgData = await orgRes.json() const newOrg = Array.isArray(orgData) ? orgData[0] : orgData if (!newOrg?.id) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Failed to create org', detail: orgData }, 500) // Seed org_settings await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_settings', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: newOrg.id, display_name: display_name || name, default_currency: default_currency || 'USD', email_provider: email_provider || 'gmail', ai_engine: ai_engine || 'gemini' }) }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, org: newOrg }) } // ── admin_list_users ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns all users + their profiles for a specific org. Samora admin only. if (action === 'admin_list_users') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const adminCheck = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/samora_admins?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const admCheck = await adminCheck.json() if (!Array.isArray(admCheck) || !admCheck.length) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 403) const { org_id } = payload if (!org_id) return jsonResponse({ error: 'org_id required' }, 400) const usersRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?org_id=eq.' + org_id + '&select=user_id,email,role,created_at&order=created_at.asc', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const users = asArray(await usersRes.json()) // For each user, get their account count for (const u of users) { const acctRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?user_id=eq.' + u.user_id + '&org_id=eq.' + org_id + '&select=id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const accts = asArray(await acctRes.json()) u.account_count = accts.length } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, users }) } // ── admin_create_user ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Creates a new user (Supabase Auth + user_profiles) and assigns them to // an org with a role. Samora admin only. if (action === 'admin_create_user') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const adminCheck = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/samora_admins?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const adm = await adminCheck.json() if (!Array.isArray(adm) || !adm.length) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 403) const { org_id, email, password, name, role } = payload if (!org_id || !email || !password) return jsonResponse({ error: 'org_id, email, password required' }, 400) // Create user in Supabase Auth via admin API const authRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/auth/v1/admin/users', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ email: email, password: password, email_confirm: true // auto-confirm so they can log in immediately }) }) const authData = await authRes.json() if (!authData?.id) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Failed to create auth user', detail: authData }, 500) // Create user profile const profileRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify({ user_id: authData.id, org_id: org_id, email: email, role: (role || 'member').toLowerCase() }) }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, user: { id: authData.id, email, role: role || 'member' } }) } // ── admin_assign_accounts ───────────────────────────────────────────────── // Bulk-assign accounts to a rep within an org. Creates parent rows if // needed, handles region assignment. Samora admin only. if (action === 'admin_assign_accounts') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const adminCheck = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/samora_admins?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const adm = await adminCheck.json() if (!Array.isArray(adm) || !adm.length) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 403) const { org_id, user_id: targetUserId, accounts } = payload // accounts: [{name, domain?, region?}] if (!org_id || !targetUserId || !accounts?.length) { return jsonResponse({ error: 'org_id, user_id, accounts[] required' }, 400) } const created: string[] = [] const skipped: string[] = [] for (const acct of accounts) { const name = (acct.name || '').trim() if (!name) continue // Check if this exact name+user combo already exists const existRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + org_id + '&user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&account_name=ilike.' + encodeURIComponent(name) + '&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const existing = asArray(await existRes.json()) if (existing.length) { skipped.push(name); continue } // Find or create parent if this account already exists for other reps let parentId = null const parentRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + org_id + '&account_name=ilike.' + encodeURIComponent(name) + '®ion=eq.Global&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const parentRows = asArray(await parentRes.json()) if (parentRows.length) { parentId = parentRows[0].id } else { // Check if other reps have this account (potential parent needed) const othersRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + org_id + '&account_name=ilike.' + encodeURIComponent(name) + '&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const others = asArray(await othersRes.json()) if (others.length) { // Create parent anchor const newParent = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=representation' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id, account_name: name, region: 'Global' }) }) const np = asArray(await newParent.json()) if (np[0]?.id) { parentId = np[0].id // Link existing rows to parent too await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + org_id + '&account_name=ilike.' + encodeURIComponent(name) + '&parent_account_id=is.null®ion=is.null', { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ parent_account_id: parentId }) }) } } } const row: Record = { org_id, user_id: targetUserId, account_name: name, domain: acct.domain || null } if (acct.region) row.region = acct.region if (parentId) row.parent_account_id = parentId await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify(row) }) created.push(name) } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, created, skipped }) } // ── scan_external_signals ──────────────────────────────────────────────── // Scans public sources (Google News) for each account in the calling // user's org (or a specific org if called by a Samora admin). Classifies // headlines into buying signal types and persists to account_signals. // // Runs per-account, per-region: "Ferrero India" gets different news // results than "Ferrero Middle East". No API key needed for Google News // RSS — it's completely free and public. // // Signal types detected: // expansion — new market, new office, geographic expansion // hiring — job postings, team growth, hiring spree // leadership — new CXO, senior hire, board appointment // funding — funding round, investment, acquisition // partnership — strategic alliance, joint venture // earnings — quarterly results, revenue growth/decline // restructuring — layoffs, restructuring, cost-cutting (negative signal) // product_launch — new product, service launch // // ── scan_external_signals ──────────────────────────────────────────────── // Scans public web sources for buying signals across all named accounts // in the org. Uses Gemini with Google Search grounding — one API call // searches the entire web, classifies results, and returns source URLs. // Accounts are batched 5 per call for speed. // // This replaces the old sequential RSS+classify approach which was slow // (one HTTP + one Gemini call per account) and shallow (news headlines // only). The grounded approach is faster (4 calls for 20 accounts), // deeper (full web, not just news), and returns verifiable source URLs. if (action === 'scan_external_signals') { const { org_id: targetOrgId } = payload const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey let orgId = targetOrgId if (!orgId) { const pRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=org_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const pData = asArray(await pRes.json()) orgId = pData?.[0]?.org_id } if (!orgId) return jsonResponse({ error: 'No org found' }, 400) // Get all scannable accounts (deduplicated by name+region) const acctRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=id,account_name,region,parent_account_id,domain', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const allAccounts = asArray(await acctRes.json()) const parentIds = new Set(allAccounts.filter((a: any) => a.parent_account_id).map((a: any) => a.parent_account_id)) const scannable = allAccounts.filter((a: any) => { return !(parentIds.has(a.id) && !a.parent_account_id && !a.domain && !a.region) && a.account_name }) const seen = new Set() const unique: any[] = [] for (const a of scannable) { const key = (a.account_name + '||' + (a.region || '')).toLowerCase() if (seen.has(key)) continue seen.add(key) unique.push(a) } if (!unique.length) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, accountsScanned: 0, results: [] }) const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] const results: any[] = [] // ── Batch accounts into groups of 5 for efficient Gemini calls ──── const BATCH_SIZE = 5 const batches: any[][] = [] for (let i = 0; i < unique.length; i += BATCH_SIZE) { batches.push(unique.slice(i, i + BATCH_SIZE)) } // ── Process batches in parallel (max 3 concurrent) ──────────────── const processBatch = async (batch: any[]) => { const accountList = batch.map(a => { const region = a.region && a.region !== 'Global' ? a.region : '' return a.account_name + (region ? ' (' + region + ')' : '') }) if (GEMINI_URL && GEMINI_KEY) { // ── Gemini with Google Search grounding ─────────────────────── // One call searches the web for all accounts in the batch, // classifies signals, and returns source URLs via grounding metadata. try { const accountListStr = accountList.map((name, i) => (i+1) + '. ' + name).join('\n') const prompt = `You are an enterprise sales intelligence analyst. For each company below, search for recent news, events, and signals that indicate a potential buying window for B2B technology/services vendors. Companies to research: ${accountListStr} For each company, find and classify signals into these categories: - expansion: new markets, new offices, geographic expansion, market entry - hiring: job postings in relevant roles, team growth, hiring plans - leadership: new CXO, senior hires, board appointments, key departures - funding: funding rounds, investment received, IPO activity, acquisitions - partnership: strategic alliances, joint ventures, channel partnerships - earnings: quarterly results, revenue growth/decline, financial milestones - restructuring: layoffs, cost-cutting, reorganization (negative signal) - product_launch: new product, service launch, major platform update Return ONLY a JSON array. Each element: { "company": "exact company name from list above", "signals": [ { "type": "expansion|hiring|leadership|funding|partnership|earnings|restructuring|product_launch", "headline": "one-line summary of the signal", "detail": "2-3 sentence context of why this is a buying signal", "source_hint": "publication or source name if identifiable", "confidence": 0-100, "recency": "days_ago or approximate date" } ] } Rules: - Only include genuinely recent signals (last 30 days preferred, max 90 days) - Skip irrelevant noise (sports sponsorships, celebrity endorsements, general industry commentary) - Confidence 80+ = verified from multiple sources, 50-79 = single credible source, below 50 = rumor/speculation - If no meaningful signals found for a company, include it with empty signals array - Return valid JSON only, no markdown fences, no commentary` const gRes = await fetch(GEMINI_URL, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }], tools: [{ google_search: {} }], generationConfig: { temperature: 0.1, maxOutputTokens: 4000 } }) }) const gData = await gRes.json() // Extract grounding metadata (source URLs) const groundingChunks = gData?.candidates?.[0]?.groundingMetadata?.groundingChunks || [] const sourceUrls: { title: string, url: string }[] = groundingChunks .filter((c: any) => c.web?.uri) .map((c: any) => ({ title: c.web.title || '', url: c.web.uri })) // Parse the structured response const gText = gData?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || '' const cleaned = gText.replace(/```json|```/g, '').trim() let parsed: any[] = [] try { parsed = JSON.parse(cleaned) } catch(e) { /* parse failed */ } if (Array.isArray(parsed)) { for (const companyResult of parsed) { const companyName = companyResult.company || '' const matchedAccount = batch.find(a => { const searchName = a.account_name + (a.region && a.region !== 'Global' ? ' (' + a.region + ')' : '') return searchName === companyName || a.account_name.toLowerCase() === companyName.toLowerCase() || companyName.toLowerCase().includes(a.account_name.toLowerCase()) }) if (!matchedAccount) continue const signals = companyResult.signals || [] let inserted = 0 // Dedup against today's signals const existRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signals?account_id=eq.' + matchedAccount.id + '&detected_at=gte.' + today + '&select=raw_text', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const existing = asArray(await existRes.json()) const existingTexts = new Set(existing.map((e: any) => (e.raw_text || '').slice(0, 80).toLowerCase())) for (const sig of signals) { if (!sig.type || !sig.headline) continue if (existingTexts.has(sig.headline.slice(0, 80).toLowerCase())) continue const scoreWeight = sig.type === 'funding' ? 15 : sig.type === 'leadership' ? 14 : sig.type === 'expansion' ? 12 : sig.type === 'hiring' ? 10 : sig.type === 'product_launch' ? 10 : sig.type === 'partnership' ? 8 : sig.type === 'earnings' ? 6 : sig.type === 'restructuring' ? -8 : 5 // Find a matching source URL from grounding metadata const matchingSource = sourceUrls.find(s => s.title.toLowerCase().includes(matchedAccount.account_name.toLowerCase()) || sig.headline.toLowerCase().split(' ').some((w: string) => w.length > 4 && s.title.toLowerCase().includes(w)) ) try { await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signals', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: orgId, account_id: matchedAccount.id, signal_type: sig.type, source: 'web_grounded', raw_text: sig.headline.slice(0, 500), extracted: { headline: sig.headline, detail: sig.detail || null, source_name: sig.source_hint || matchingSource?.title || null, source_url: matchingSource?.url || null, region: matchedAccount.region || null, recency: sig.recency || null, search_query: companyName }, score_weight: scoreWeight, confidence: sig.confidence || 60, expires_at: new Date(Date.now() + 30 * 86400000).toISOString(), is_active: true }) }) inserted++ } catch(e) { /* non-fatal */ } } results.push({ account: matchedAccount.account_name, region: matchedAccount.region || null, signalsDetected: signals.length, signalsInserted: inserted, sources: sourceUrls.filter(s => s.title.toLowerCase().includes(matchedAccount.account_name.toLowerCase()) ).slice(0, 3) }) } // Add entries for accounts that Gemini didn't return results for for (const a of batch) { if (!results.find(r => r.account === a.account_name && r.region === (a.region || null))) { results.push({ account: a.account_name, region: a.region || null, signalsDetected: 0, signalsInserted: 0, sources: [] }) } } } } catch(e) { // Gemini grounded search failed — mark all in batch as failed for (const a of batch) { results.push({ account: a.account_name, region: a.region || null, signalsDetected: 0, signalsInserted: 0, error: String(e).slice(0, 200) }) } } } else { // No Gemini configured — skip external scan, return empty for (const a of batch) { results.push({ account: a.account_name, region: a.region || null, signalsDetected: 0, signalsInserted: 0, note: 'No AI engine configured — enable Gemini in org settings to scan external signals' }) } } } // Run batches with concurrency limit of 3 const concurrency = 3 for (let i = 0; i < batches.length; i += concurrency) { const chunk = batches.slice(i, i + concurrency) await Promise.all(chunk.map(b => processBatch(b))) } const totalSignals = results.reduce((s: number, r: any) => s + (r.signalsInserted || 0), 0) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, accountsScanned: unique.length, batchesUsed: batches.length, totalSignalsDetected: results.reduce((s: number, r: any) => s + (r.signalsDetected || 0), 0), totalSignalsInserted: totalSignals, engine: 'gemini_grounded_search', geminiConfigured: !!(GEMINI_URL && GEMINI_KEY), results }) } // ── upsert_deal_value ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Called when a rep saves deal fields (value, currency, units, close date // etc.) for a specific account. Automatically fetches the current FX rate // and persists deal_value_usd so pipeline rollup is always in USD without // the frontend needing to know about conversion logic. if (action === 'upsert_deal_value') { const { account_id, deal_value, deal_currency, licenses_units, contract_months, close_probability, expected_close, deal_type, signal_score, revenue_streams, deal_value_usd: clientUsd } = payload if (!account_id) return jsonResponse({ error: 'account_id required' }, 400) const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey // Fetch live FX rate for this currency → USD let dealValueUsd: number | null = null let fxRateUsed: number | null = null const currency = (deal_currency || 'USD').toUpperCase() if (deal_value != null && currency !== 'USD') { // Check our cached rates first (max 24 hours old) const cachedRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/fx_rates?from_currency=eq.' + currency + '&to_currency=eq.USD&order=fetched_at.desc&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const cached = asArray(await cachedRes.json()) const cacheAge = cached[0] ? Date.now() - new Date(cached[0].fetched_at).getTime() : Infinity const cacheValid = cacheAge < 86400000 // 24 hours if (cacheValid && cached[0]?.rate) { fxRateUsed = cached[0].rate } else { // Fetch live rate from exchangerate-api (free tier, no key needed for basic) try { const fxRes = await fetch( 'https://api.exchangerate-api.com/v4/latest/' + currency ) const fxData = await fxRes.json() if (fxData?.rates?.USD) { fxRateUsed = fxData.rates.USD // Cache it for next time await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/fx_rates', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify({ from_currency: currency, to_currency: 'USD', rate: fxRateUsed }) }) } } catch(e) { // FX fetch failed — fall back to cached rate even if stale if (cached[0]?.rate) fxRateUsed = cached[0].rate } } if (fxRateUsed) dealValueUsd = Math.round(deal_value * fxRateUsed * 100) / 100 } else if (deal_value != null && currency === 'USD') { dealValueUsd = deal_value fxRateUsed = 1.0 } const update: Record = {} if (deal_value != null) { update.deal_value = deal_value; update.deal_currency = currency } // If client computed the USD total (multi-stream), use that; otherwise use FX-converted single value if (clientUsd != null) { update.deal_value_usd = clientUsd; update.fx_updated_at = new Date().toISOString() } else if (dealValueUsd != null) { update.deal_value_usd = dealValueUsd; update.fx_rate_used = fxRateUsed; update.fx_updated_at = new Date().toISOString() } if (licenses_units != null) update.licenses_units = licenses_units if (contract_months != null) update.contract_months = contract_months if (close_probability != null) update.close_probability = close_probability if (expected_close != null) update.expected_close = expected_close if (deal_type != null) update.deal_type = deal_type if (signal_score != null) update.signal_score = signal_score if (revenue_streams != null) update.revenue_streams = revenue_streams const upRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + account_id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=representation' }, body: JSON.stringify(update) } ) const upData = await upRes.json() if (!upRes.ok) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Update failed', detail: upData }, 500) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, deal_value_usd: dealValueUsd, fx_rate_used: fxRateUsed, currency, account: asArray(upData)[0] }) } // ── get_pipeline ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns pipeline summary for a manager: all accounts with deal values // across all reps in the org, rolled up in USD with probability weighting. // Reps can call this too but only see their own accounts. if (action === 'get_pipeline') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const callerRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=role,org_id,manager_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const callerData = asArray(await callerRes.json()) const callerRole = callerData?.[0]?.role || 'member' const orgId = callerData?.[0]?.org_id // ── Region normalisation via DB function ────────────────────────────── // normalise_region() lives in PostgreSQL so mappings can be updated // without redeploying the edge function — just update the SQL function. const normalizeRegion = async (region: string | null): Promise => { if (!region) return 'Global' try { const res = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/rpc/normalise_region', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ input_region: region }) }) const result = await res.json() return typeof result === 'string' ? result : region } catch(e) { return region } } // ── Tiered visibility ───────────────────────────────────────────────── let repUserIds: string[] = [userId] if (canSeeFullOrg(callerRole)) { const allRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=user_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) repUserIds = asArray(await allRes.json()).map((u: any) => u.user_id) } else if (canSeeCrossTeam(callerRole)) { const teamRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=user_id,manager_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const allUsers = asArray(await teamRes.json()) const directManagers = allUsers.filter((u: any) => u.manager_id === userId).map((u: any) => u.user_id) const teamSet = new Set([userId, ...directManagers]) allUsers.forEach((u: any) => { if (directManagers.includes(u.manager_id)) teamSet.add(u.user_id) }) repUserIds = Array.from(teamSet) } else if (canSeeTeam(callerRole)) { const reportsRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&manager_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=user_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const reports = asArray(await reportsRes.json()) repUserIds = [userId, ...reports.map((r: any) => r.user_id)] } // ── Build rep email lookup ──────────────────────────────────────────── // Fetch email for all reps in scope so the frontend can show names const repProfilesRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&user_id=in.(' + repUserIds.join(',') + ')&select=user_id,email', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const repEmailMap: Record = {} asArray(await repProfilesRes.json()).forEach((u: any) => { repEmailMap[u.user_id] = u.email || u.user_id }) // ── Pre-normalise all unique regions in one batch ──────────────────── // Collect all unique region strings, normalise them via DB function, // then use the results as a sync lookup inside the map() calls below. const allAcctRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&user_id=in.(' + repUserIds.join(',') + ')&select=region', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const allAcctRegions = asArray(await allAcctRes.json()).map((a: any) => a.region) const uniqueRegions = [...new Set([...allAcctRegions, null])] const regionNormCache: Record = {} await Promise.all(uniqueRegions.map(async (r: any) => { regionNormCache[r || ''] = await normalizeRegion(r) })) const normRegion = (r: string | null) => regionNormCache[r || ''] || r || 'Global' const acctFilter = 'org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&user_id=in.(' + repUserIds.join(',') + ')' + '&deal_value=not.is.null' + '&deal_status=not.in.(won,lost)' + // exclude closed deals from active pipeline '&select=id,account_name,region,deal_value,deal_value_usd,deal_currency,' + 'deal_type,close_probability,expected_close,signal_score,licenses_units,' + 'contract_months,user_id,parent_account_id,company_linkedin_url,health_score' const verifiedRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?' + acctFilter, { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const verifiedRaw = asArray(await verifiedRes.json()) // ── Fetch unverified pipeline (AI-extracted value hints) ───────────── const hintsFilter = 'org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&signal_type=eq.value_hint&is_active=eq.true' + '&select=account_id,extracted,confidence,detected_at' const hintsRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signals?' + hintsFilter + '&order=detected_at.desc', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const hintsRaw = asArray(await hintsRes.json()) // Build account lookup for hints const acctLookupRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&user_id=in.(' + repUserIds.join(',') + ')' + '&select=id,account_name,region,user_id,deal_value', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const acctLookup: Record = {} asArray(await acctLookupRes.json()).forEach((a: any) => { acctLookup[a.id] = a }) // ── Three-tier pipeline classification ─────────────────────────────── // Tier 1 — VERIFIED: rep entered a value AND signal score >= 40 // Concrete evidence from both sides: rep committed to a number and // the conversation data backs it up. High confidence in the pipeline. // // Tier 2 — PARTIAL: rep entered a value BUT signal score < 40 (or null) // Rep's own estimate with limited conversation evidence. Common early // in a deal when a rep logs a target value after one intro call. // // Tier 3 — UNVERIFIED: no rep value, only AI-extracted hint from meetings // Gemini detected a budget/value mention in a transcript but the rep // hasn't confirmed it. Directional only — should not go in the forecast. // const VERIFIED_SCORE_THRESHOLD = 40 // signal score required for full verification const stageLabels = orgCfg.deal_stages.reduce((m: any, s: any) => { m[s.key] = s.label; return m }, {} as Record) // Stage-to-score proxy — used when signal_score hasn't been persisted yet. // A deal at commercial stage has clearly had significant activity; treating // it as partial (score = null) would be misleading. Once local_intelligence // runs and persists a real score, that takes precedence. const stageScoreProxy: Record = { commercial: 65, value_prop: 45, prospective: 25, unknown: 20 } const allWithValues = verifiedRaw.map((a: any) => { const dealStageKey = a.deal_type || 'unknown' const proxyScore = stageScoreProxy[dealStageKey] ?? 20 // Use real signal_score if set, otherwise fall back to stage proxy const score = a.signal_score ?? proxyScore const hasValue = a.deal_value != null const tier = hasValue && score >= VERIFIED_SCORE_THRESHOLD ? 'verified' : hasValue ? 'partial' : 'unverified' const prob = tier === 'verified' ? (a.close_probability ?? score ?? 50) : tier === 'partial' ? (a.close_probability ?? Math.min(score, 35)) : 25 const valueUsd = a.deal_value_usd || 0 return { id: a.id, account: a.account_name, region: normRegion(a.region), rawRegion: a.region, deal_value: a.deal_value, deal_currency: a.deal_currency, deal_value_usd: valueUsd, deal_type: dealStageKey, stage: dealStageKey, close_probability: prob, expected_close: a.expected_close, signal_score: score, signal_score_source: a.signal_score != null ? 'measured' : 'stage_proxy', licenses_units: a.licenses_units, contract_months: a.contract_months, weighted_value_usd: Math.round(valueUsd * prob / 100), rep_user_id: a.user_id, rep_email: repEmailMap[a.user_id] || null, tier, revenue_streams: [], product_name: null, icp_score: null, icp_notes: null, // Legacy compat — verified = true only for tier 1 verified: tier === 'verified', verification_reason: tier === 'verified' ? 'Rep-stated value + signal score ' + score + ' ≥ ' + VERIFIED_SCORE_THRESHOLD : tier === 'partial' ? 'Rep-stated value, but ' + (score === null ? 'no signal score yet' : 'signal score ' + score + ' < ' + VERIFIED_SCORE_THRESHOLD) : 'AI-extracted hint only', company_linkedin_url: a.company_linkedin_url || null, health_score: a.health_score ?? null } }) const verified = allWithValues.filter((d: any) => d.tier === 'verified') const partial = allWithValues.filter((d: any) => d.tier === 'partial') // Unverified: AI-extracted hints for accounts with NO rep-entered value const repValueAccountIds = new Set(verifiedRaw.map((a: any) => a.id)) const hintsByAccount: Record = {} hintsRaw.forEach((h: any) => { if (repValueAccountIds.has(h.account_id)) return // rep already has a value — don't show as unverified const acct = acctLookup[h.account_id] if (!acct) return if (!hintsByAccount[h.account_id] || h.confidence > hintsByAccount[h.account_id].confidence) { hintsByAccount[h.account_id] = { ...h, acct } } }) const unverified = Object.values(hintsByAccount).map((h: any) => { const ext = h.extracted || {} const amountUsd = ext.amount_usd || (ext.amount && ext.currency === 'INR' ? ext.amount * 0.012 : ext.amount || 0) return { id: h.account_id, account: h.acct.account_name, region: normRegion(h.acct.region), rawRegion: h.acct.region, deal_value: ext.amount || null, deal_currency: ext.currency || 'USD', deal_value_usd: Math.round(amountUsd), deal_type: 'new_business', stage: 'prospective', close_probability: 20, // very conservative — no rep commitment expected_close: null, signal_score: null, licenses_units: null, contract_months: null, weighted_value_usd: Math.round(amountUsd * 0.2), rep_user_id: h.acct.user_id, rep_email: repEmailMap[h.acct.user_id] || null, tier: 'unverified', verified: false, hint_context: ext.context || null, confidence: h.confidence, verification_reason: 'AI-extracted from meeting/email — rep confirmation needed' } }) const all = [...verified, ...partial, ...unverified] // ── Region × Stage breakdown ────────────────────────────────────────── const regionBuckets: Record = {} all.forEach((d: any) => { if (!regionBuckets[d.region]) { regionBuckets[d.region] = { region: d.region, total_usd: 0, weighted_usd: 0, verified_usd: 0, partial_usd: 0, unverified_usd: 0, deals: 0, stages: {} } } const rb = regionBuckets[d.region] rb.total_usd += d.deal_value_usd rb.weighted_usd += d.weighted_value_usd rb.deals++ if (d.tier === 'verified') rb.verified_usd += d.deal_value_usd else if (d.tier === 'partial') rb.partial_usd += d.deal_value_usd else rb.unverified_usd += d.deal_value_usd if (!rb.stages[d.stage]) rb.stages[d.stage] = { usd: 0, deals: 0 } rb.stages[d.stage].usd += d.deal_value_usd rb.stages[d.stage].deals++ }) // ── Summaries ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── const totalUsd = all.reduce((s: number, d: any) => s + d.deal_value_usd, 0) const verifiedUsd = verified.reduce((s: number, d: any) => s + d.deal_value_usd, 0) const partialUsd = partial.reduce((s: number, d: any) => s + d.deal_value_usd, 0) const unverifiedUsd = unverified.reduce((s: number, d: any) => s + d.deal_value_usd, 0) const weightedUsd = all.reduce((s: number, d: any) => s + d.weighted_value_usd, 0) const closingThisQuarter = all.filter((d: any) => { if (!d.expected_close) return false const dt = new Date(d.expected_close) const now = new Date() const qEnd = new Date(now.getFullYear(), Math.floor(now.getMonth()/3)*3 + 3, 0) return dt <= qEnd }).reduce((s: number, d: any) => s + d.deal_value_usd, 0) // ── Intelligent prompts per role ────────────────────────────────────── const prompts: string[] = [] const tier = canSeeFullOrg(callerRole) ? 'org' : canSeeCrossTeam(callerRole) ? 'cross_team' : canSeeTeam(callerRole) ? 'team' : 'self' if (tier === 'self') { const hotDeals = verified.filter((d: any) => (d.signal_score || 0) >= 60) if (hotDeals.length) prompts.push('🔥 ' + hotDeals.length + ' fully verified deal' + (hotDeals.length>1?'s':'') + ' with strong signals — prioritise this week') if (partial.length) prompts.push('⚡ ' + partial.length + ' deal' + (partial.length>1?'s need':'needs') + ' more activity to verify — run SAM Intelligence to boost signal score') const stale = verified.filter((d: any) => d.expected_close && new Date(d.expected_close) < new Date()) if (stale.length) prompts.push('⚠️ ' + stale.length + ' deal' + (stale.length>1?'s are':'is') + ' past expected close date — update or reprice') if (unverified.length) prompts.push('〜 ' + unverified.length + ' AI-extracted hint' + (unverified.length>1?'s':'') + ' need your confirmation — add a deal value to move them to pipeline') } else if (tier === 'team') { if (verified.length) prompts.push('✅ ' + verified.length + ' fully verified deal' + (verified.length>1?'s':'') + ' — $' + Math.round(verifiedUsd/1000) + 'K in high-confidence pipeline') if (partial.length) prompts.push('⚡ ' + partial.length + ' partial deal' + (partial.length>1?'s':'') + ' ($' + Math.round(partialUsd/1000) + 'K) — reps need to generate more signals to verify') const teamWithNoDeals = repUserIds.filter((id: string) => id !== userId && !allWithValues.find((d: any) => d.rep_user_id === id)).length if (teamWithNoDeals > 0) prompts.push('👤 ' + teamWithNoDeals + ' rep' + (teamWithNoDeals>1?'s have':' has') + ' no deals in pipeline — review account assignments') } else if (tier === 'cross_team') { const weakRegions = Object.values(regionBuckets).filter((r: any) => r.verified_usd === 0) if (weakRegions.length) prompts.push('🌍 ' + weakRegions.length + ' region' + (weakRegions.length>1?'s have':' has') + ' zero verified pipeline — needs attention') prompts.push('📊 $' + Math.round(verifiedUsd/1000) + 'K verified · $' + Math.round(partialUsd/1000) + 'K partial · $' + Math.round(unverifiedUsd/1000) + 'K unverified across ' + Object.keys(regionBuckets).length + ' regions') } else { if (closingThisQuarter > 0) prompts.push('📅 $' + Math.round(closingThisQuarter/1000) + 'K expected to close this quarter · $' + Math.round(weightedUsd/1000) + 'K weighted forecast') const convRate = totalUsd > 0 ? Math.round(verifiedUsd / totalUsd * 100) : 0 prompts.push('🎯 ' + convRate + '% of pipeline is fully verified · ' + Math.round(partialUsd/totalUsd*100||0) + '% partial · ' + Math.round(unverifiedUsd/totalUsd*100||0) + '% AI-only') } // ── Fetch closed deals (won + lost) from org_accounts.deal_status ────── let wonDeals: any[] = [] let lostDeals: any[] = [] try { const closedRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts' + '?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&user_id=in.(' + repUserIds.join(',') + ')' + '&deal_status=in.(won,lost)' + '&select=id,account_name,deal_status,deal_close_reason,deal_actual_value_usd,deal_value_usd,deal_closed_at,user_id' + '&order=deal_closed_at.desc&limit=100', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const closedRaw = asArray(await closedRes.json()) closedRaw.forEach((o: any) => { const entry = { id: o.id, account: o.account_name, actual_value_usd: o.deal_actual_value_usd || o.deal_value_usd || 0, deal_value_usd: o.deal_value_usd || 0, close_reason: o.deal_close_reason || null, closed_at: o.deal_closed_at, rep_user_id: o.user_id } if (o.deal_status === 'won') wonDeals.push(entry) else lostDeals.push(entry) }) } catch(e) { /* non-fatal */ } // ── Fetch product breakdown from account_opportunities ──────────────── // Products live in account_opportunities joined to org_products, not org_accounts let productBreakdown: Record = {} try { const oppRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_opportunities' + '?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&status=eq.open' + '&select=deal_value_usd,product:org_products(name)', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const opps = asArray(await oppRes.json()) opps.forEach((o: any) => { const pName = o.product?.name || 'No product' if (!productBreakdown[pName]) productBreakdown[pName] = { value: 0, count: 0 } productBreakdown[pName].value += o.deal_value_usd || 0 productBreakdown[pName].count += 1 }) } catch(e) { /* non-fatal */ } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, callerTier: tier, callerRole, deals: all, // full deal array — used by frontend filters and charts verified, partial, unverified, won: wonDeals, lost: lostDeals, productBreakdown, verificationThreshold: VERIFIED_SCORE_THRESHOLD, regionBreakdown: Object.values(regionBuckets).sort((a: any, b: any) => b.total_usd - a.total_usd), summary: { total_deals: all.length, verified_deals: verified.length, partial_deals: partial.length, unverified_deals: unverified.length, total_value_usd: Math.round(totalUsd), verified_value_usd: Math.round(verifiedUsd), partial_value_usd: Math.round(partialUsd), unverified_value_usd: Math.round(unverifiedUsd), weighted_value_usd: Math.round(weightedUsd), closing_this_quarter_usd: Math.round(closingThisQuarter), }, prompts, stageLabels, dealStages: orgCfg.deal_stages }) } // ── get_products ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns the org's product catalog. Used by the deal form and Samora admin. if (action === 'get_products') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const res = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_products?org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&is_active=eq.true&order=sort_order.asc,created_at.asc&select=*', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, products: asArray(await res.json()) }) } // ── upsert_product ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Creates or updates a product in the org's catalog. // Org admins + Samora admins can call this. if (action === 'upsert_product') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const callerRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=role', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const callerRole = asArray(await callerRes.json())?.[0]?.role // Check samora admin OR org admin const samoraRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/samora_admins?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const isSamoraAdmin = asArray(await samoraRes.json()).length > 0 if (!canManageOrg(callerRole) && !isSamoraAdmin) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 403) const { id, name, description, category, keywords, is_active, sort_order } = payload if (!name) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Product name required' }, 400) const productData: Record = { org_id: orgCfg.org_id, name, description: description || null, category: category || null, keywords: keywords || [], is_active: is_active !== false, sort_order: sort_order || 0 } let res if (id) { res = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_products?id=eq.' + id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=representation' }, body: JSON.stringify(productData) }) } else { res = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_products', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=representation' }, body: JSON.stringify(productData) }) } const data = await res.json() if (!res.ok) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Save failed', detail: data }, 500) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, product: asArray(data)[0] }) } // ── delete_product ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── if (action === 'delete_product') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { id } = payload if (!id) return jsonResponse({ error: 'id required' }, 400) // Soft delete — keep historical data intact await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_products?id=eq.' + id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ is_active: false }) }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true }) } // ── upsert_opportunity ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Creates or updates one opportunity (account × product). // Probability is always derived — never user-input. if (action === 'upsert_opportunity') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { opportunity_id, account_id, product_id, deal_value, deal_currency, revenue_streams, deal_value_usd: clientUsd, stage, expected_close, deal_type, licenses_units, notes } = payload if (!account_id) return jsonResponse({ error: 'account_id required' }, 400) // Fetch current signals for this account+product to derive probability const signalFilter = 'account_id=eq.' + account_id + (product_id ? '&product_id=eq.' + product_id : '') + '&is_active=eq.true&select=signal_type,score_weight' const sigsRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signals?' + signalFilter, { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const sigs = asArray(await sigsRes.json()) const sigTypes = sigs.map((s: any) => s.signal_type) const sigScore = sigs.length > 0 ? Math.min(100, sigs.reduce((sum: number, s: any) => sum + (s.score_weight || 0), 0)) : null // Derive probability from stage + signal types (DB function) let probability = 30 let probabilityBasis = stage ? (stage + ' stage') : 'No stage set' try { const probRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/rpc/derive_close_probability', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ p_stage: stage || 'prospective', p_signal_score: sigScore, p_signal_types: sigTypes }) }) const probData = await probRes.json() if (probData?.probability) { probability = probData.probability; probabilityBasis = probData.basis || probabilityBasis } } catch(e) { /* use defaults */ } // FX conversion let dealValueUsd = clientUsd || null const currency = (deal_currency || 'USD').toUpperCase() if (deal_value != null && !clientUsd) { if (currency === 'USD') { dealValueUsd = deal_value } else { try { const fxRes = await fetch('https://api.exchangerate-api.com/v4/latest/' + currency) const fxData = await fxRes.json() if (fxData?.rates?.USD) dealValueUsd = Math.round(deal_value * fxData.rates.USD * 100) / 100 } catch(e) { /* use client value */ } } } // Tier classification const tier = sigScore !== null && sigScore >= 40 && deal_value != null ? 'verified' : deal_value != null ? 'partial' : 'unverified' const oppData: Record = { account_id, product_id: product_id || null, org_id: orgCfg.org_id, rep_user_id: userId, deal_value: deal_value || null, deal_currency: currency, deal_value_usd: dealValueUsd, revenue_streams: revenue_streams || [], stage: stage || 'prospective', signal_score: sigScore, close_probability: probability, probability_basis: probabilityBasis, expected_close: expected_close || null, deal_type: deal_type || 'new_business', licenses_units: licenses_units || null, notes: notes || null, tier } let res if (opportunity_id) { res = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_opportunities?id=eq.' + opportunity_id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=representation' }, body: JSON.stringify(oppData) }) } else { res = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_opportunities', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=representation' }, body: JSON.stringify(oppData) }) } const data = await res.json() if (!res.ok) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Save failed', detail: data }, 500) // ── Sync totals back to org_accounts ───────────────────────────────────── // The account chip and pipeline both read from org_accounts.deal_value. // After saving an opportunity, sum all opportunities for this account and // write the total back so both views stay in sync. try { const allOppsRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_opportunities?account_id=eq.' + account_id + '&select=deal_value_usd,deal_value,deal_currency,stage,signal_score,close_probability,revenue_streams', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const allOpps = asArray(await allOppsRes.json()) const totalUsd = allOpps.reduce((s: number, o: any) => s + (o.deal_value_usd || 0), 0) const maxScore = allOpps.reduce((m: number, o: any) => Math.max(m, o.signal_score || 0), 0) const bestProb = allOpps.reduce((m: number, o: any) => Math.max(m, o.close_probability || 0), 0) const bestStage = allOpps.find((o: any) => o.stage === 'commercial')?.stage || allOpps.find((o: any) => o.stage === 'value_prop')?.stage || allOpps[0]?.stage || 'prospective' // Merge all revenue streams const allStreams = allOpps.flatMap((o: any) => o.revenue_streams || []) await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + account_id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ deal_value_usd: Math.round(totalUsd), deal_value: allOpps[0]?.deal_value || totalUsd, deal_currency: allOpps[0]?.deal_currency || 'USD', signal_score: maxScore || null, close_probability: bestProb || null, deal_type: bestStage, revenue_streams: allStreams }) }) } catch(e) { /* non-fatal — opportunity is saved, sync is best-effort */ } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, opportunity: asArray(data)[0], probability, probabilityBasis }) } // ── get_opportunities ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns all opportunities for an account, joined with product info. if (action === 'get_opportunities') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { account_id } = payload if (!account_id) return jsonResponse({ error: 'account_id required' }, 400) const res = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_opportunities?account_id=eq.' + account_id + '&select=*,product:org_products(id,name,category,description)&order=created_at.asc', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, opportunities: asArray(await res.json()) }) } // ── sync_sequencing ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Provider-agnostic sequencing data sync. // Reads org_settings.sequencing_provider to determine which adapter to call. // Each adapter normalises provider data → sequencing_signals table rows. // Currently supported: smartreach // Future: outreach, apollo, lemlist, instantly — add new adapters below. if (action === 'sync_sequencing') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const provider = orgCfg.sequencing_provider as string | null const apiKey = orgCfg.sequencing_api_key as string | null const teamId = orgCfg.sequencing_team_id as string | null const orgId = orgCfg.org_id as string if (!provider) return jsonResponse({ error: 'No sequencing provider configured.' }, 400) if (!apiKey) return jsonResponse({ error: 'No sequencing API key configured.' }, 400) const acctRes2 = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=id,account_name,domain,user_id,additional_domains', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const accounts2 = asArray(await acctRes2.json()) // Fetch SamoraTrack user profiles to map emails → user_ids const profileRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=user_id,email', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const samoraProfiles: Record = {} // email → user_id asArray(await profileRes.json()).forEach((p: any) => { if (p.email) samoraProfiles[p.email.toLowerCase()] = p.user_id }) // Pre-compute brand root for every stored account once const accountRoots = accounts2.map((a: any) => ({ ...a, nameRoot: normCompanyName(a.account_name || ''), domainRoot: extractBrandRoot(a.domain || ''), extraRoots: (a.additional_domains || []).map((d: string) => extractBrandRoot(d)) })) // Matching priority chain: // 1. Exact normalised name match // 2. Email domain → account domain root (most reliable when company field is blank) // 3. Email domain → account name root // 4. Company name root → account name (partial) // 5. Additional domains // Unmatched → stored with account_id=null but still synced (visible in diagnostic) const matchAccount2 = (company: string, prospectEmail?: string): { id: string, user_id: string } | null => { if (!company && !prospectEmail) return null const companyRoot = normCompanyName(company) const emailDomain = prospectEmail ? (prospectEmail.split('@')[1] || '') : '' const emailBrandRoot = emailDomain ? extractBrandRoot(emailDomain) : '' let best: any = null; let bestScore = 0 for (const a of accountRoots) { let score = 0 if (a.nameRoot && companyRoot && a.nameRoot === companyRoot) score = 100 else if (emailBrandRoot && a.domainRoot && emailBrandRoot === a.domainRoot) score = 95 else if (emailBrandRoot && a.extraRoots.includes(emailBrandRoot)) score = 90 else if (emailBrandRoot && a.nameRoot && a.nameRoot.startsWith(emailBrandRoot) && emailBrandRoot.length >= 4) score = 85 else if (companyRoot.length >= 4 && a.nameRoot && (a.nameRoot.startsWith(companyRoot) || companyRoot.startsWith(a.nameRoot))) score = 75 else if (companyRoot.length >= 4 && a.domainRoot && a.domainRoot.startsWith(companyRoot)) score = 65 if (score > bestScore) { bestScore = score; best = a } } return bestScore >= 65 ? { id: best.id, user_id: best.user_id } : null } // Diagnostic counters — surface match rate to help admins fix mapping const matchDiag = { matched: 0, unmatched: 0, noCompanyNoEmail: 0, unmatchedSamples: [] as string[] } const syncSmartReach = async () => { const SR_BASE = 'https://api.smartreach.io/api/v3' const srH = { 'X-API-KEY': apiKey!, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } const campRes2 = await fetch(SR_BASE + '/campaigns?team_id=' + teamId, { headers: srH }) if (!campRes2.ok) throw new Error('SmartReach campaigns: ' + campRes2.status) const campaigns2 = ((await campRes2.json()).campaigns || []).filter((c: any) => c.status !== 'archived') // Fetch SmartReach team members to map SR user → Samora user // This lets us assign rep_user_id via campaign ownership, not just account ownership const srMemberMap: Record = {} // SR member_id/email → Samora user_id try { const membersRes = await fetch(SR_BASE + '/team?team_id=' + teamId, { headers: srH }) if (membersRes.ok) { const membersData = await membersRes.json() const members = membersData.members || membersData.team_members || [] members.forEach((m: any) => { const email = (m.email || m.member_email || '').toLowerCase() if (email && samoraProfiles[email]) { srMemberMap[m.id || m.member_id || email] = samoraProfiles[email] srMemberMap[email] = samoraProfiles[email] } }) } } catch(e) { /* team member fetch is non-fatal */ } let totalSynced = 0; if (sr.ok) cmpStats = await sr.json() } catch(e) {} // ── Fetch campaign steps to properly classify channel per step ──── // SmartReach campaigns can have multi-channel steps: // step.type = 'email' | 'phone' | 'linkedin' | 'whatsapp' | 'manual' // Without step data we default everything to 'email' — which makes // calls invisible in coverage and IVR verification. const stepChannels: Record = {} // step_number → channel let hasCalls = false, hasLinkedin = false, hasWhatsapp = false try { const stepsRes = await fetch(SR_BASE + '/campaigns/' + cmp.id + '/steps?team_id=' + teamId, { headers: srH }) if (stepsRes.ok) { const stepsData = await stepsRes.json() const steps = stepsData.steps || stepsData.campaign_steps || stepsData.data?.steps || [] steps.forEach((s: any) => { const sType = (s.type || s.step_type || '').toLowerCase() const sNum = s.step_number || s.sequence_number || s.order || 0 const ch = sType === 'phone' || sType === 'call' ? 'call' : sType === 'linkedin' || sType === 'li_message' || sType === 'inmail' ? 'linkedin' : sType === 'whatsapp' ? 'whatsapp' : 'email' stepChannels[sNum] = ch if (ch === 'call') hasCalls = true if (ch === 'linkedin') hasLinkedin = true if (ch === 'whatsapp') hasWhatsapp = true }) } } catch(e) { /* non-fatal — fall back to name-based detection */ } // Campaign-level channel hint from name (existing fallback) const campName = (cmp.name || '').toLowerCase() if (!hasCalls && /\bcall\b|calling|phone|dialer|cold.?call/i.test(campName)) hasCalls = true if (!hasLinkedin && /\blinkedin\b|inmail/i.test(campName)) hasLinkedin = true if (!hasWhatsapp && /whatsapp/i.test(campName)) hasWhatsapp = true // Determine primary channel for the campaign (for tagging when // step-level data isn't available per-prospect) const primaryChannel = hasCalls ? 'call' : hasLinkedin ? 'linkedin' : hasWhatsapp ? prospRes2.json()).campaign_prospects || [] // ── Campaign activity log — call completions per prospect ────────── // SmartReach's activity log exposes when reps mark call steps done. // This is the ONLY reliable source for per-prospect call data. // prospect_status_in_campaign only has email booleans. const callCompletedProspects = new Set() if (hasCalls) { try { const actRes = await || null if (curStep && stepChannels[curStep]) return stepChannels[curStep] if (cp.call_disposition || cp.call_status || stat2.call_made || stat2.call_completed) return 'call' if || 'member' let scopedRepIds3: string[] = [userId] if (canSeeFullOrg(callerRole3)) { const allRes3 = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?org_id=eq.' + orgId3 + '&select=user_id', {
