Object.values(byRepMap3).map((r:any)=>({...r,campaigns:Array.from(r.campaigns),open_rate:r.sent>0?Math.round(r.opened/r.sent*100):0,reply_rate:r.sent>0?Math.round(r.replied/r.sent*100):0})).sort((a:any,b:any)=>b.sent-a.sent) const byAcctMap3: Record = {} prospects3.forEach((p:any) => { const k=p.account_id||p.prospect_company||'unknown' if (!byAcctMap3[k]) byAcctMap3[k]={account_id:p.account_id,account_name:p.account_name||p.prospect_company,contacts:0,sent:0,opened:0,replied:0,clicks:0,campaigns:new Set(),contacts_detail:[]} byAcctMap3[k].contacts++ if (p.sent) byAcctMap3[k].sent++ if (p.opened) byAcctMap3[k].opened++ if (p.replied) byAcctMap3[k].replied++ byAcctMap3[k].clicks+=p.clicks||0 if (p.campaign_name) byAcctMap3[k].campaigns.add(p.campaign_name) byAcctMap3[k].contacts_detail.push({name:p.prospect_name,email:p.prospect_email,replied:p.replied,opened:p.opened,opens:p.opens}) }) const byAccount3 = Object.values(byAcctMap3).map((a:any)=>({...a,campaigns:Array.from(a.campaigns),open_rate:a.sent>0?Math.round(a.opened/a.sent*100):0,reply_rate:a.sent>0?Math.round(a.replied/a.sent*100):0,signal:a.replied>0?'hot':a.opened>0?'warm':a.sent>0?'cold':'none'})).sort((a:any,b:any)=>((b.replied?100:0)+(b.opened?50:0)+b.sent)-((a.replied?100:0)+(a.opened?50:0)+a.sent)) const byCampMap3: Record = {} prospects3.forEach((p:any) => { const k=p.campaign_id||'unknown' if (!byCampMap3[k]) byCampMap3[k]={campaign_id:k,campaign_name:p.campaign_name,prospects:0,sent:0,opened:0,replied:0,bounced:0,hot_accounts:new Set()} byCampMap3[k].prospects++ if (p.sent) byCampMap3[k].sent++ if (p.opened) byCampMap3[k].opened++ if (p.replied) { byCampMap3[k].replied++; if (p.account_name) byCampMap3[k].hot_accounts.add(p.account_name) } if (p.bounced) byCampMap3[k].bounced++ }) const byCampaign3 = Object.values(byCampMap3).map((c:any)=>({...c,hot_accounts:Array.from(c.hot_accounts),open_rate:c.sent>0?Math.round(c.opened/c.sent*100):0,reply_rate:c.sent>0?Math.round(c.replied/c.sent*100):0})).sort((a:any,b:any)=>b.reply_rate-a.reply_rate) const hotSignals3 = prospects3.filter((p:any)=>p.replied).map((p:any)=>({prospect_name:p.prospect_name,prospect_email:p.prospect_email,prospect_company:p.prospect_company,account_name:p.account_name,account_id:p.account_id,campaign_name:p.campaign_name,opens:p.opens})) return jsonResponse({ ok:true, period_days:days, org_summary:orgSummary3, by_rep:byRep3, by_account:byAccount3, by_campaign:byCampaign3, hot_signals:hotSignals3, benchmarks:{open_rate:{good:35,avg:25,label:'Industry avg: 25-35%'},reply_rate:{good:12,avg:7,label:'Industry avg: 7-12%'},bounce_rate:{good:3,avg:5,label:'Good: <3%'}}, synced_at:orgCfg.sequencing_synced_at||null }) } // ── close_opportunity ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Mark a deal as won or lost. Records the actual close value for won deals, // reason for lost deals, and inserts a signal history snapshot. // ── update_opportunity_field ────────────────────────────────────────────── if (action === 'update_opportunity_field') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { opportunity_id, field, value } = payload const ALLOWED = ['expected_close','deal_type','deal_value','deal_value_usd','close_probability'] if (!ALLOWED.includes(field)) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Field not editable: ' + field }, 400) const res = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + opportunity_id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ [field]: value }) }) if (!res.ok) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Update failed' }, 500) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, field, value }) } // ── get_sent_today ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns sent emails from a given date — used by auto-complete to verify // email tasks. Lightweight: only fetches subject, to, snippet, not bodies. if (action === 'get_sent_today') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { date } = payload const targetDate = date || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] const tokRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=*&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const tokRows = asArray(await tokRes.json()) if (!tokRows?.length) return jsonResponse({ emails: [] }) const provider = tokRows[0].provider || 'google' const tokenResult = provider === 'microsoft' ? await getValidMicrosoftToken(tokRows[0], userId, SUPABASE_URL, SVC) : await getValidGmailToken(tokRows[0], userId, SUPABASE_URL, SVC, GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET) if (tokenResult.refreshFailed) return jsonResponse({ emails: [] }) const at = tokenResult.accessToken const afterEpoch = Math.floor(new Date(targetDate + 'T00:00:00Z').getTime() / 1000) const beforeEpoch = Math.floor(new Date(targetDate + 'T23:59:59Z').getTime() / 1000) if (provider === 'microsoft') { const res = await fetch('https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/me/mailFolders/SentItems/messages?$filter=sentDateTime ge ' + encodeURIComponent(targetDate + 'T00:00:00Z') + ' and sentDateTime le ' + encodeURIComponent(targetDate + 'T23:59:59Z') + '&$top=30&$select=subject,toRecipients,bodyPreview', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + at } }) const d2 = await res.json() return jsonResponse({ emails: (d2.value||[]).map((m: any) => ({ subject: m.subject, to: (m.toRecipients||[]).map((r: any) => r.emailAddress?.address).join(', '), snippet: m.bodyPreview })) }) } else { const q = encodeURIComponent('in:sent after:' + afterEpoch + ' before:' + beforeEpoch) const res = await fetch('https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + q + '&maxResults=30', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + at } }) const listData = await res.json() const msgIds = (listData.messages || []).slice(0, 30) const emails: any[] = [] for (const m of msgIds.slice(0, 20)) { const mr = await fetch('https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages/' + m.id + '?format=metadata&metadataHeaders=Subject&metadataHeaders=To', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + at } }) const md = await mr.json() const hdrs = md.payload?.headers || [] emails.push({ subject: hdrs.find((h: any) => h.name==='Subject')?.value || '', to: hdrs.find((h: any) => h.name==='To')?.value || '', snippet: md.snippet || '' }) } return jsonResponse({ emails, count: msgIds.length }) } } // ── process_ooo_mails ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Scans inbox for OOO auto-replies, extracts the return date, and creates // a follow-up task on the first business day after they return. // Rule: "Sibi returns 17 July (Fri)" → task created for Mon 20 July. if (action === 'process_ooo_mails') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { days = 7 } = payload const sinceEpoch = Math.floor((Date.now() - days * 86400000) / 1000) // Fetch email token const tokRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=*&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const tokRows = asArray(await tokRes.json()) if (!tokRows?.length) return jsonResponse({ error: 'No email connected', tasks: [] }) const provider = tokRows[0].provider || 'google' const tokenResult = provider === 'microsoft' ? await getValidMicrosoftToken(tokRows[0], userId, SUPABASE_URL, SVC) : await getValidGmailToken(tokRows[0], userId, SUPABASE_URL, SVC, GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET) if (tokenResult.refreshFailed) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Token expired', tasks: [] }) const at = tokenResult.accessToken // Search inbox for OOO mails const oooQuery = encodeURIComponent('in:inbox (subject:"out of office" OR subject:"auto reply" OR subject:"automatic reply" OR subject:"on leave" OR subject:"away from office") after:' + sinceEpoch) const gmailRes = await fetch('https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + oooQuery + '&maxResults=20', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + at } }) const gmailData = await gmailRes.json() const messages = gmailData.messages || [] // Return date extraction patterns const returnPatterns = [ /(?:back|return|returning|available|resume|resuming)\s+(?:on\s+)?(\d{1,2}(?:st|nd|rd|th)?\s+(?:Jan(?:uary)?|Feb(?:ruary)?|Mar(?:ch)?|Apr(?:il)?|May|Jun(?:e)?|Jul(?:y)?|Aug(?:ust)?|Sep(?:tember)?|Oct(?:ober)?|Nov(?:ember)?|Dec(?:ember)?)\s*(?:\d{4})?)/i, /(?:back|return|returning|available|resume)\s+(?:on\s+)?(\d{1,2}[\/\-]\d{1,2}(?:[\/\-]\d{2,4})?)/i, /until\s+(\d{1,2}(?:st|nd|rd|th)?\s+(?:Jan(?:uary)?|Feb(?:ruary)?|Mar(?:ch)?|Apr(?:il)?|May|Jun(?:e)?|Jul(?:y)?|Aug(?:ust)?|Sep(?:tember)?|Oct(?:ober)?|Nov(?:ember)?|Dec(?:ember)?)\s*(?:\d{4})?)/i, /until\s+(\d{1,2}[\/\-]\d{1,2}(?:[\/\-]\d{2,4})?)/i, ] function nextBusinessDay(dateStr: string): string | null { const d = new Date(dateStr) if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return null d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1) // day AFTER return // Skip weekends if (d.getDay() === 6) d.setDate(d.getDate() + 2) if (d.getDay() === 0) d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1) return d.toISOString().split('T')[0] } const tasksCreated: any[] = [] for (const msg of messages.slice(0, 10)) { try { const msgRes = await fetch('https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages/' + msg.id + '?format=metadata&metadataHeaders=From&metadataHeaders=Subject', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + at } }) const msgData = await msgRes.json() const headers = msgData.payload?.headers || [] const fromHeader = headers.find((h: any) => h.name === 'From')?.value || '' const subjectHeader = headers.find((h: any) => h.name === 'Subject')?.value || '' const snippet = msgData.snippet || '' // Extract sender name const senderName = fromHeader.replace(/<[^>]+>/, '').trim().replace(/"/g, '') || fromHeader.split('@')[0] // Try to extract return date from subject + snippet const searchText = subjectHeader + ' ' + snippet let returnDate: string | null = null for (const pattern of returnPatterns) { const m = searchText.match(pattern) if (m) { const parsed = new Date(m[1] + (m[1].match(/\d{4}/) ? '' : (' ' + new Date().getFullYear()))) if (!isNaN(parsed.getTime()) && parsed > new Date()) { returnDate = parsed.toISOString().split('T')[0] break } } } if (!returnDate) continue const taskDate = nextBusinessDay(returnDate) if (!taskDate) continue // Check if task already exists for this person on this date const dtRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/daytrack?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&day_key=eq.' + taskDate + '&select=data', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const dtRows = asArray(await dtRes.json()) const existingTasks: string[] = dtRows[0]?.data?.tasks?.map((t: any) => t.text?.toLowerCase() || '') || [] const senderLower = senderName.toLowerCase().slice(0, 15) if (existingTasks.some(t => t.includes(senderLower) && t.includes('ooo'))) continue // Build task text const taskText = 'From OOO Mail: ' + senderName + ' is back from leave today — reach out and re-engage' // Upsert into daytrack const dt = dtRows[0]?.data || { tasks: [], wins: [], issues: [] } dt.tasks = dt.tasks || [] dt.tasks.push({ text: taskText, done: false, priority: true, source: 'ooo_auto', oooFrom: fromHeader, oooReturnDate: returnDate, created: new Date().toISOString() }) const method = dtRows.length ? 'PATCH' : 'POST' const url = SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/daytrack?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&day_key=eq.' + taskDate await fetch(method === 'POST' ? SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/daytrack' : url, { method, headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', ...(method==='POST'?{'Prefer':'resolution=merge-duplicates'}:{}) }, body: JSON.stringify(method === 'POST' ? { user_id: userId, day_key: taskDate, data: dt } : { data: dt }) }) tasksCreated.push({ taskDate, taskText, senderName, returnDate }) } catch(e) { /* non-fatal, skip this message */ } } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, tasksCreated, oooMailsFound: messages.length }) } if (action === 'close_opportunity') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { opportunity_id, status, close_reason, actual_value_usd } = payload // opportunity_id is org_accounts.id (the deal card ID from the pipeline) if (!opportunity_id || !status) return jsonResponse({ error: 'opportunity_id and status required' }, 400) if (!['won','lost','open'].includes(status)) return jsonResponse({ error: 'status must be won|lost|open' }, 400) const now = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] const update: any = { deal_status: status, deal_closed_at: status !== 'open' ? now : null, deal_close_reason: close_reason || null, deal_actual_value_usd: actual_value_usd ? parseFloat(actual_value_usd) : null } const res = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + opportunity_id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify(update) }) if (!res.ok) { const err = await res.text() return jsonResponse({ error: 'Failed to close deal: ' + err }, 500) } // Snapshot signal history at close if (status !== 'open') { const acctRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + opportunity_id + '&select=signal_score,deal_type,org_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const acct = asArray(await acctRes.json())[0] if (acct) { await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signal_history', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: orgCfg.org_id, account_id: opportunity_id, signal_score: acct.signal_score || 0, pipeline_tier: status === 'won' ? 'closed_won' : 'closed_lost', deal_type: acct.deal_type, source: status === 'won' ? 'closed_won' : 'closed_lost' }) }) } } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, status, closed_at: now }) } // ── get_team_digest ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns a structured overview of every rep in the caller's visible scope. // Used by the Claude MCP connector so a manager can ask "how is the team doing?" // and get a complete picture: tasks, wins, pipeline, signal quality, gaps. if (action === 'get_team_digest') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { date } = payload const targetDate = date || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] const orgId = orgCfg.org_id // Verify caller has team visibility const callerRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=role,org_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const callerData = asArray(await callerRes.json()) const callerRole = callerData?.[0]?.role || 'member' if (!canSeeTeam(callerRole)) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Team digest requires manager role or above' }, 403) // Get visible reps using the same scoping as get_pipeline const allProfilesRes = await const directs = allProfiles.filter((u: any) => u.manager_id === userId).map((u: any) => u.user_id) visibleRepIds = [userId, ...directs, ...allProfiles.filter((u: any) => directs.includes(u.manager_id)).map((u: any) => u.user_id)] } else { visibleRepIds = [userId, ...allProfiles.filter((u: any) => u.manager_id === userId).map((u: any) => u.user_id)] } const repMap: Record = {} allProfiles.forEach((u: any) => { repMap[u.user_id] = u }) // Fetch daytracks for visible reps on target date const dtRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/daytrack?user_id=in.(' + Fetch pipeline signal scores per rep const acctRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&user_id=in.(' + visibleRepIds.join(',') + ')&select=user_id,account_name,signal_score,deal_type,deal_value_usd', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const accounts = asArray(await acctRes.json()) const accountsByRep: Record = {} accounts.forEach((a: any) => { if (!accountsByRep[a.user_id]) accountsByRep[a.user_id] = []; accountsByRep[a.user_id].push(a) }) const repDigests = visibleRepIds.map(repId => { const profile = repMap[repId] || {} const dt = daytracks.find((d: any) => d.user_id === repId) const tasks = dt?.data?.tasks || [] const wins = dt?.data?.wins || [] const issues = dt?.data?.issues || [] const repAccts = accountsByRep[repId] || [] const scores = repAccts.map((a: any) => a.signal_score).filter(Boolean) const avgSignal = scores.length ? Math.round(scores.reduce((a: number, b: number) => a + b, 0) / scores.length) : null const hotAccounts = repAccts.filter((a: any) => (a.signal_score || 0) >= 60) const doneTasks = tasks.filter((t: any) => t.done) const verifiedTasks = doneTasks.filter((t: any) => ['verified','verified_hot','attested','task_done'].includes(t.signal || '')) return { rep_email: profile.email, rep_name: (profile.email || '').split('@')[0].split('.').map((w: string) => w.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+w.slice(1)).join(' '), role: profile.role, date: targetDate, tasks_total: tasks.length, tasks_done: doneTasks.length, completion_pct: tasks.length > 0 ? Math.round(doneTasks.length / tasks.length * 100) : 0, wins: wins.length, issues: issues.length, pipeline_accounts: repAccts.length, hot_accounts: hotAccounts.length, avg_signal_score: avgSignal, total_pipeline_usd: repAccts.reduce((s: number, a: any) => s + (a.deal_value_usd || 0), 0), top_accounts: hotAccounts.slice(0, 3).map((a: any) => ({ name: a.account_name, signal: a.signal_score, stage: a.deal_type })), logged_tasks: tasks.slice(0, 5).map((t: any) => ({ text: t.text, done: t.done, priority: t.priority })), has_logged_today: tasks.length > 0 } }) // Manager summary const loggedCount = repDigests.filter(r => r.has_logged_today).length const notLoggedReps = repDigests.filter(r => !r.has_logged_today).map(r => r.rep_name) const avgCompletion = repDigests.length ? Math.round(repDigests.reduce((s, r) => s + r.completion_pct, 0) / repDigests.length) : 0 return jsonResponse({ ok: true, date: targetDate, manager_summary: { total_reps: repDigests.length, reps_logged_today: loggedCount, reps_not_logged: notLoggedReps, avg_completion_rate: avgCompletion + '%', total_wins_today: repDigests.reduce((s, r) => s + r.wins, 0) }, reps: repDigests }) } // ── get_analytics ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Aggregated analytics for the Samora Analytics dashboard. // Returns: pipeline summary, rep performance, region/product breakdown, // signal trend (from history table), coverage stats, won/lost analysis. if (action === 'get_analytics') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { period = 'month' } = payload // month | quarter | year const callerRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=role,org_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const callerData = asArray(await callerRes.json()) const orgId = callerData?.[0]?.org_id const callerRole = callerData?.[0]?.role || 'member' if (!orgId) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Not found' }, 404) const now = new Date() let since: Date if (period === 'quarter') { since = new Date(now.getFullYear(), Math.floor(now.getMonth()/3)*3, 1) } else if (period === 'year') { since = new Date(now.getFullYear(), 0, 1) } else { since = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth(), 1) } // month default const sinceStr = since.toISOString().split('T')[0] // ── Scope to visible reps ───────────────────────────────────────────── let scopedUserIds: string[] = [] const allProfilesRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=user_id,email,role,manager_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const allProfiles = asArray(await allProfilesRes.json()) if (canSeeFullOrg(callerRole)) { scopedUserIds = allProfiles.map((u: any) => u.user_id) } else if (canSeeTeam(callerRole)) { scopedUserIds = [userId, ...allProfiles.filter((u: any) => u.manager_id === userId).map((u: any) => u.user_id)] } else { scopedUserIds = [userId] } const repEmailMap: Record = {} allProfiles.forEach((u: any) => { repEmailMap[u.user_id] = u.email }) // ── Fetch core data in parallel ─────────────────────────────────────── const [acctRes, oppRes, histRes, seqRes, daytRes] = await Promise.all([ fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&user_id=in.(' + scopedUserIds.join(',') + ')&select=id,account_name,signal_score,deal_type,deal_value_usd,region,icp_score,user_id,additional_domains', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }), fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_opportunities?account_id=in.(select:id:from:org_accounts:org_id.eq.' + orgId + ')&select=id,account_id,status,closed_at,close_reason,actual_value_usd,deal_value_usd,probability', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }).catch(() => null), fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signal_history?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&recorded_at=gte.' + sinceStr + 'T00:00:00Z&order=recorded_at.asc&limit=500&select=account_id,signal_score,pipeline_tier,recorded_at,source', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }), fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/sequencing_signals?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&rep_user_id=in.(' + scopedUserIds.join(',') + ')&select=rep_user_id,event_type,replied,account_id&created_at=gte.' + sinceStr + 'T00:00:00Z', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }), fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/daytrack?user_id=in.(' + scopedUserIds.join(',') + ')&day_key=gte.' + sinceStr + '&select=user_id,day_key,data', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) ]) const accounts = asArray(await acctRes.json()) const opps = oppRes ? asArray(await oppRes.json()) : [] const signalHistory = asArray(await histRes.json()) const seqSigs = asArray(await seqRes.json()) const daytracks = asArray(await daytRes.json()) // ── Pipeline summary ────────────────────────────────────────────────── const VERIFIED_THRESHOLD = 40 let totalPipeline = 0, verifiedPipeline = 0, partialPipeline = 0, aiPipeline = 0, weightedForecast = 0 accounts.forEach((a: any) => { const val = a.deal_value_usd || 0 const score = a.signal_score || 0 totalPipeline += val if (val > 0 && score >= VERIFIED_THRESHOLD) { verifiedPipeline += val; weightedForecast += val * 0.7 } else if (val > 0 && score > 0) { partialPipeline += val; weightedForecast += val * 0.3 } else if (val > 0) { aiPipeline += val; weightedForecast += val * 0.1 } }) // ── By rep ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── const byRepMap: Record = {} scopedUserIds.forEach(uid => { byRepMap[uid] = { user_id: uid, email: repEmailMap[uid] || uid, rep_name: (repEmailMap[uid]||'').split('@')[0].split('.').map((w: string) => w.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+w.slice(1)).join(' '), pipeline: 0, verified: 0, partial: 0, deals: 0, avg_signal: 0, signal_scores: [] as number[], tasks_done: 0, tasks_total: 0, wins: 0 } }) accounts.forEach((a: any) => { if (!byRepMap[a.user_id]) return const val = a.deal_value_usd || 0 const score = a.signal_score || 0 byRepMap[a.user_id].pipeline += val if (val > 0 && score >= VERIFIED_THRESHOLD) byRepMap[a.user_id].verified += val else if (val > 0) byRepMap[a.user_id].partial += val if (val > 0) byRepMap[a.user_id].deals++ if (score > 0) byRepMap[a.user_id].signal_scores.push(score) }) daytracks.forEach((d: any) => { if (!byRepMap[d.user_id]) return const tasks = d.data?.tasks || [] byRepMap[d.user_id].tasks_total += tasks.length byRepMap[d.user_id].tasks_done += tasks.filter((t: any) => t.done).length byRepMap[d.user_id].wins += (d.data?.wins || []).length }) const byRep = Object.values(byRepMap).map((r: any) => ({ ...r, avg_signal: r.signal_scores.length ? Math.round(r.signal_scores.reduce((a: number, b: number) => a+b, 0) / r.signal_scores.length) : 0, completion_rate: r.tasks_total > 0 ? Math.round(r.tasks_done / r.tasks_total * 100) : 0, signal_scores: undefined // don't send raw array })).sort((a: any, b: any) => b.pipeline - a.pipeline) // ── By region ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── const byRegionMap: Record = {} accounts.forEach((a: any) => { const r = a.region || 'Unassigned' byRegionMap[r] = (byRegionMap[r] || 0) + (a.deal_value_usd || 0) }) const byRegion = Object.entries(byRegionMap).map(([region, value]) => ({ region, value })).sort((a: any, b: any) => b.value - a.value) // ── Signal score trend (weekly buckets) ─────────────────────────────── const weeklyScores: Record = {} signalHistory.forEach((h: any) => { const d = new Date(h.recorded_at) const weekStart = new Date(d); weekStart.setDate(d.getDate() - d.getDay()) const key = weekStart.toISOString().split('T')[0] if (!weeklyScores[key]) weeklyScores[key] = [] weeklyScores[key].push(h.signal_score) }) const signalTrend = Object.entries(weeklyScores).map(([week, scores]) => ({ week, avg: Math.round(scores.reduce((a, b) => a+b, 0) / scores.length), count: scores.length })).sort((a, b) => a.week.localeCompare(b.week)) // ── Coverage stats (from sequencing signals) ────────────────────────── const seqByRep: Record = {} seqSigs.forEach((s: any) => { if (!s.rep_user_id) return if (!seqByRep[s.rep_user_id]) seqByRep[s.rep_user_id] = { sent: 0, replied: 0 } if (s.event_type === 'sent') seqByRep[s.rep_user_id].sent++ if (s.replied) seqByRep[s.rep_user_id].replied++ }) // ── Won/Lost analysis ───────────────────────────────────────────────── const wonOpps = opps.filter((o: any) => o.status === 'won' && (!o.closed_at || o.closed_at >= sinceStr)) const lostOpps = opps.filter((o: any) => o.status === 'lost' && (!o.closed_at || o.closed_at >= sinceStr)) const wonValue = wonOpps.reduce((s: number, o: any) => s + (o.actual_value_usd || o.deal_value_usd || 0), 0) const lostValue = lostOpps.reduce((s: number, o: any) => s + (o.deal_value_usd || 0), 0) const lossReasons: Record = {} lostOpps.forEach((o: any) => { const r = o.close_reason || 'unspecified'; lossReasons[r] = (lossReasons[r]||0)+1 }) // ── Top accounts by signal score ────────────────────────────────────── const topAccounts = accounts.filter((a: any) => a.signal_score != null).sort((a: any, b: any) => (b.signal_score||0) - (a.signal_score||0)).slice(0, 10).map((a: any) => ({ account_name: a.account_name, signal_score: a.signal_score, deal_value_usd: a.deal_value_usd, deal_type: a.deal_type, region: a.region, icp_score: a.icp_score, rep_email: repEmailMap[a.user_id] })) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, period, since: sinceStr, pipeline: { total: totalPipeline, verified: verifiedPipeline, partial: partialPipeline, ai_extracted: aiPipeline, weighted_forecast: weightedForecast, total_accounts: accounts.length, accounts_with_value: accounts.filter((a: any) => a.deal_value_usd > 0).length }, by_rep: byRep, by_region: byRegion, signal_trend: signalTrend, seq_by_rep: seqByRep, won_lost: { won_count: wonOpps.length, lost_count: lostOpps.length, won_value: wonValue, lost_value: lostValue, win_rate: (wonOpps.length + lostOpps.length) > 0 ? Math.round(wonOpps.length / (wonOpps.length + lostOpps.length) * 100) : null, loss_reasons: Object.entries(lossReasons).map(([reason, count]) => ({ reason, count })).sort((a: any, b: any) => b.count - a.count) }, top_accounts: topAccounts }) } // ── get_signal_history ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns signal score history for one account — used for sparklines and // trend indicators in the pipeline card. Deduped: returns one reading per // calendar day so sparklines aren't noisy. if (action === 'get_signal_history') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { account_id, days = 60 } = payload if (!account_id) return jsonResponse({ error: 'account_id required' }, 400) const since = new Date(Date.now() - days * 86400000).toISOString() const res = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signal_history?account_id=eq.' + account_id + '&recorded_at=gte.' + since + '&order=recorded_at.asc&limit=90', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const rows = asArray(await res.json()) // Dedupe to one reading per day (keep latest) const byDay: Record = {} rows.forEach((r: any) => { byDay[r.recorded_at.slice(0,10)] = r }) const history = Object.values(byDay) const latest = history[history.length - 1] const earliest = history[0] const trend = history.length >= 2 ? (latest?.signal_score - earliest?.signal_score) : 0 return jsonResponse({ ok: true, history, trend, latest_score: latest?.signal_score, days_tracked: history.length }) } // ── get_account_timeline ────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Chronological feed of ALL signals for one account across every source: // Gmail emails, sequencing signals, completion notes, deal changes, // score changes, market intelligence. One scrollable truth. if (action === 'get_account_timeline') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { account_id, days = 90 } = payload if (!account_id) return jsonResponse({ error: 'account_id required' }, 400) const since = new Date(Date.now() - days * 86400000).toISOString() const orgId = orgCfg.org_id // Fetch in parallel from all signal sources const [seqRes, intelRes, histRes, oppRes] = await Promise.all([ fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/sequencing_signals?account_id=eq.' + account_id + '&created_at=gte.' + since + '&order=created_at.desc&limit=50&select=event_type,channel,campaign_name,prospect_name,prospect_email,replied,total_opens,created_at', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }), fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_intelligence?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&account_name=in.(' + account_id + ')&created_at=gte.' + since + '&order=meeting_date.desc&limit=20&select=meeting_date,meeting_subject,summary,sentiment,product_feedback,expansion_signals,risk_signals,source', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }), fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signal_history?account_id=eq.' + account_id + '&recorded_at=gte.' + since + '&order=recorded_at.desc&limit=30&select=signal_score,pipeline_tier,deal_type,source,recorded_at', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }), fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_opportunities?account_id=eq.' + account_id + '&select=id,status,closed_at,close_reason,actual_value_usd,deal_value_usd,probability,updated_at,product:org_products(name)', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) ]) const [seqSignals, intel, scoreHistory, opportunities] = await Promise.all([ seqRes.json().then(asArray), intelRes.json().then(asArray), histRes.json().then(asArray), oppRes.json().then(asArray) ]) // Normalise all events into a single timeline format const timeline: any[] = [] seqSignals.forEach((s: any) => { if (!['replied','opened','sent'].includes(s.event_type)) return timeline.push({ type: 'sequencing', date: s.created_at, channel: s.channel, title: s.event_type === 'replied' ? `↩ ${s.prospect_name || s.prospect_email} replied` : s.event_type === 'opened' ? `👁 ${s.prospect_name || s.prospect_email} opened email` : `✉ ${s.prospect_name || s.prospect_email} added to ${s.campaign_name}`, body: s.event_type === 'replied' ? `${s.total_opens} opens before reply` : s.campaign_name, sentiment: s.event_type === 'replied' ? 'positive' : 'neutral', source: 'smartreach' }) }) intel.forEach((i: any) => { const signals = [...(i.product_feedback||[]), ...(i.expansion_signals||[]), ...(i.risk_signals||[])] timeline.push({ type: 'intelligence', date: i.meeting_date + 'T12:00:00Z', title: `🧠 ${i.meeting_subject || 'Intelligence signal'}`, body: i.summary || '', sentiment: i.sentiment || 'neutral', signals: signals.slice(0,3), source: i.source || 'ai' }) }) scoreHistory.forEach((h: any) => { const isClose = ['closed_won','closed_lost'].includes(h.source) if (!isClose && h.source === 'system') return // skip routine system updates timeline.push({ type: 'score_change', date: h.recorded_at, title: isClose ? (h.source === 'closed_won' ? '🏆 Deal closed — Won' : '❌ Deal closed — Lost') : `📊 Signal score updated → ${h.signal_score}`, body: `${h.pipeline_tier || ''} · ${h.deal_type || ''}`.replace(/^·\s*|·\s*$/, ''), sentiment: h.source === 'closed_won' ? 'positive' : h.source === 'closed_lost' ? 'negative' : 'neutral', score: h.signal_score, source: h.source }) }) opportunities.forEach((o: any) => { if (o.status !== 'open') { timeline.push({ type: 'deal_change', date: o.closed_at ? o.closed_at + 'T12:00:00Z' : o.updated_at, title: o.status === 'won' ? `🏆 Won — ${o.product?.name || 'Deal'}` : `❌ Lost — ${o.product?.name || 'Deal'}`, body: o.status === 'won' ? `$${Math.round((o.actual_value_usd||o.deal_value_usd||0)/1000)}K closed` : (o.close_reason || 'No reason logged'), sentiment: o.status === 'won' ? 'positive' : 'negative', source: 'deal' }) } }) // Sort all events by date descending timeline.sort((a: any, b: any) => new Date(b.date).getTime() - new Date(a.date).getTime()) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, timeline, account_id, period_days: days, opportunities }) } // ── compute_icp_scores ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Uses Gemini to score each org account against the org's ICP definition. // Runs for all accounts in the org; updates icp_score + icp_notes on each. // Managers and above can trigger this; admins configure the ICP definition. // ── get_org_setting / save_org_setting ──────────────────────────────────── // Generic key-value store for org-level settings (ICP definition, etc.) // Uses org_settings table — key column stores the setting name, value column stores content. if (action === 'get_org_setting') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { key } = payload const orgId = orgCfg.org_id const res = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_settings?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&key=eq.' + encodeURIComponent(key) + '&select=value&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const rows = asArray(await res.json()) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, key, value: rows[0]?.value || null }) } if (action === 'save_org_setting') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { key, value } = payload const orgId = orgCfg.org_id // Upsert — merge on org_id + key const res = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_settings', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'resolution=merge-duplicates,return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: orgId, key, value }) }) if (!res.ok && res.status !== 204) { // org_settings may not have key/value columns — try updating a known column const fallbackRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_settings?org_id=eq.' + orgId, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ [key]: value }) } ) if (!fallbackRes.ok) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Save failed — org_settings table may need a key/value column. Run: ALTER TABLE org_settings ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS key text, ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS value text;' }, 500) } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, key, value }) } if (action === 'compute_icp_scores') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const orgId = orgCfg.org_id // Try key-value org_settings first (new approach), fall back to orgCfg.icp_definition (old JSON approach) let icpDesc = '' try { const icpSettingRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_settings?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&key=eq.icp_definition&select=value&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const icpRows = asArray(await icpSettingRes.json()) icpDesc = icpRows[0]?.value || '' } catch(e) { /* fall through */ } // Fall back to structured JSON ICP definition if (!icpDesc) { const icp = orgCfg.icp_definition as any if (icp && typeof icp === 'object') { icpDesc = [ icp.target_industries?.length ? 'Industries: ' + icp.target_industries.join(', ') : '', icp.target_company_size ? 'Company size: ' + icp.target_company_size : '', icp.target_geographies?.length ? 'Geographies: ' + icp.target_geographies.join(', ') : '', icp.ideal_use_case ? 'Use case: ' + icp.ideal_use_case : '', icp.keywords?.length ? 'Keywords: ' + icp.keywords.join(', ') : '' ].filter(Boolean).join('. ') } else if (typeof icp === 'string') { icpDesc = icp } } if (!icpDesc) return jsonResponse({ error: 'No ICP definition found. Add it in Admin → ICP definition.' }, 400) if (!GEMINI_KEY) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Gemini API key not configured.' }, 400) const acctRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=id,account_name,region,country_code,deal_value_usd,deal_type,signal_score', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const accounts = asArray(await acctRes.json()) const updated: string[] = [] const errors: string[] = [] for (const acct of accounts.slice(0, 30)) { // cap at 30 per call try { const prompt = `You are an ICP (Ideal Customer Profile) scoring assistant. ICP Definition: ${icpDesc} Account to score: - Name: ${acct.account_name} - Region: ${acct.region || 'unknown'} - Deal stage: ${acct.deal_type || 'unknown'} - Signal score: ${acct.signal_score || 0}/100 - Deal value (USD): ${acct.deal_value_usd || 0} Score this account from 0-100 against the ICP. 100 = perfect fit, 0 = no fit. Return ONLY JSON: {"score": , "reasoning": "<2 sentences max — what fits and what doesn't>"}` const gRes = await fetch(GEMINI_URL, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }], generationConfig: { temperature: 0.1, maxOutputTokens: 150 } }) }) const gData = await gRes.json() const text = gData?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || '' const match = text.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/) if (!match) continue const parsed = JSON.parse(match[0]) const score = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round(parsed.score || 0))) await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + acct.id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ icp_score: score, icp_notes: parsed.reasoning || '' }) }) updated.push(acct.account_name) } catch(e: any) { errors.push(acct.account_name + ': ' + e.message) } } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, scored: updated.length, updated, errors }) } // ── generate_daily_brief ───────────────────────────────────────────────── // The morning SAM brief: pipeline-weighted priorities for the day. // Reads signal scores, today's calendar, this week's tasks, sequencing stats. // Calls Gemini to produce a structured, account-specific brief. // Rep gets: 3 accounts to act on, calendar prep, coaching signal, single priority. // Manager gets: team coverage gaps, declining accounts, systemic patterns. // ── get_calendar_tasks ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── if (action === 'get_calendar_tasks') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { date } = payload const targetDate = date || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] const tokenRes2 = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=*&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const tokenRows2 = asArray(await tokenRes2.json()) if (!tokenRows2?.length) return jsonResponse({ error: 'No email connected', tasks: [] }) const tokRow2 = tokenRows2[0] const provider2 = tokRow2.provider || 'google' const tokenResult2 = provider2 === 'microsoft' ? { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const seqSignals = asArray(await seqRes.json()) const hotProspects = seqSignals.filter((s: any) => s.replied).map((s: any) => calendar events ───────────────────────────────────── let calendarEvents: any[] = [] try { // Use select=* to avoid explicit-column schema mismatch failures const tokenRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=*&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const tokenRows = asArray(await tokenRes.json()) if 'unscored'}/100, stage ${a.deal_type || 'unknown'}, value $${Math.round((a.deal_value_usd||0)/1000)}K${a.icp_score ? ', ICP '+a.icp_score : ''}` ).join('\n') const calLines = calendarEvents.length ? calendarEvents.map(e => `- ${e.time}: ${e.title}${e.isCustomer?' [CUSTOMER]':''}`).join('\n') : 'No meetings scheduled today' const weekActivity = `Tasks done: ${weekTasks.filter((t: any) => t.done).length}/${weekTasks.length}. Wins: ${weekWins.length}. Issues: ${weekIssues.length}.` const prompt = `You are SAM, a B2B sales intelligence agent. Today is ${today.toLocaleDateString('en-GB',{weekday:'long',day:'numeric',month:'long'})}. REP'S PIPELINE (signal 0-100): ${accountLines || 'No accounts assigned yet'} TODAY'S CALENDAR: ${calLines} THIS WEEK: ${weekActivity} ${hotProspects.length ? 'Replied to sequence: ' + hotProspects.slice(0,3).join(', ') : ''} ${openingProspects.length ? 'Opening emails: ' + openingProspects.join(', ') : ''} Tasks logged today: ${todayTasks.length} Return ONLY valid JSON — no markdown, no preamble: { "top_accounts": [ {"name": "account name", "score": signal_score_number, "reason": "why act today in one sentence", "action": "one specific action"}, {"name": "...", "score": 0, "reason": "...", "action": "..."}, {"name": "...", "score": 0, "reason": "...", "action": "..."} ], "calendar_prep": "one sentence for each customer meeting, or null if none", "coaching_signal": "one honest observation about this week's pattern", "priority_before_noon": "the single most important action right now, one sentence" }` const gRes = await fetch(GEMINI_URL, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }], generationConfig: { temperature: 0.2, maxOutputTokens: 2000 } }) }) const gData = await gRes.json() if (isGeminiQuotaError(gData)) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Gemini quota reached' }, 429) const rawText = gData?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || '' let briefData: any = null try { const jsonMatch = rawText.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/) if (jsonMatch) briefData = JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]) } catch(e) { // JSON was truncated — try to extract what we can from partial JSON try { const partial = rawText.substring(rawText.indexOf('{')) // Attempt to close the JSON by completing truncated strings/arrays const fixAttempt = partial .replace(/,\s*$/, '') // trailing comma .replace(/,?\s*\[?[^}\]]*$/, '') // incomplete array item + '}}' // close open objects briefData = JSON.parse(fixAttempt) } catch(e2) { // Fall back to plain text display briefData = null } } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, brief: briefData || rawText, // structured object preferred, raw text as fallback brief_structured: !!briefData, accounts: accounts.slice(0,5).map((a: any) => ({ name: a.account_name, score: a.signal_score, stage: a.deal_type, icp: a.icp_score })), calendar_count: calendarEvents.length, customer_meetings: calendarEvents.filter((e: any) => e.isCustomer).length, generated_at: new Date().toISOString() }) } // ── get_time_analytics ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Reads Google Calendar for the last N days, classifies each event by account // using the same name-matching logic as IVR, sums hours per account, and // overlays signal scores to surface time/signal mismatches. // "You spent 3.2 hours on TotalEnergies (signal 29) and 18 minutes on Gulf Oil (signal 88)." if (action === 'get_time_analytics') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { days = 30 } = payload const orgId = orgCfg.org_id // Get accounts for matching const acctRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=id,account_name,signal_score,deal_type,deal_value_usd', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const accounts = asArray(await acctRes.json()) // Get Gmail token for calendar access const tokenRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=*', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const tokenRows = asArray(await tokenRes.json()) if (!tokenRows?.length) (tokenResult.refreshFailed) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Gmail token expired' }, 401) const accessToken = tokenResult.accessToken const since = new Date(Date.now() - days * 86400000) const calRes = await fetch( 'https://www.googleapis.com/calendar/v3/calendars/primary/events' + '?timeMin=' + since.toISOString() + '&timeMax=' + new Date().toISOString() + '&singleEvents=true&orderBy=startTime&maxResults=500', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const calData = await calRes.json() const events = (calData.items || []).filter((e: any) => e.start?.dateTime && e.end?.dateTime) // Classify each event by account const timeByAccount: Record = {} let internalMinutes = 0, unclassifiedMinutes = 0 const INTERNAL_KEYWORDS = /\b(standup|stand.up|1.?on.?1|one.?on.?one|team sync|all.?hands|townhall|internal|retrospective|planning|review|catch.?up|check.?in|l&d|training|onboard|interview|hr|payroll|sprint|scrum|backlog)\b/i for (const event of events) { const duration = (new Date(event.end.dateTime).getTime() - new Date(event.start.dateTime).getTime()) / 60000 if (duration <= 0 || duration > 480) continue // skip all-day or absurd events const text = (event.summary + ' ' + (event.description || '')).toLowerCase() if (INTERNAL_KEYWORDS.test(text)) { internalMinutes += duration; continue } let matched = false for (const acct of accounts) { const acctLower = acct.account_name.toLowerCase() if (text.includes(acctLower) || acctLower.split(' ').filter((w: string) => w.length > 4).some((w: string) => text.includes(w))) { if (!timeByAccount[acct.id]) timeByAccount[acct.id] = { minutes: 0, events: 0, account: acct } timeByAccount[acct.id].minutes += duration timeByAccount[acct.id].events++ matched = true break } } if (!matched) unclassifiedMinutes += duration } const byAccount = Object.values(timeByAccount) .sort((a: any, b: any) => b.minutes - a.minutes) .map((r: any) => ({ account_name: r.account.account_name, signal_score: r.account.signal_score, deal_type: r.account.deal_type, deal_value_usd: r.account.deal_value_usd, minutes: Math.round(r.minutes), hours: Math.round(r.minutes / 60 * 10) / 10, events: r.events, // Mismatch: high time + low signal, or low time + high signal mismatch: r.account.signal_score != null ? (r.minutes > 120 && r.account.signal_score < 35 ? 'over_invested' : r.minutes < 30 && r.account.signal_score > 65 ? 'under_invested' : null) : null })) const totalCustomerMinutes = byAccount.reduce((s: number, r: any) => s + r.minutes, 0) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, period_days: days, by_account: byAccount, internal_hours: Math.round(internalMinutes / 60 * 10) / 10, customer_hours: Math.round(totalCustomerMinutes / 60 * 10) / 10, unclassified_hours: Math.round(unclassifiedMinutes / 60 * 10) / 10, mismatches: { over_invested: byAccount.filter((r: any) => r.mismatch === 'over_invested').map((r: any) => r.account_name), under_invested: byAccount.filter((r: any) => r.mismatch === 'under_invested').map((r: any) => r.account_name) } }) } // ── save_habits / get_habits ────────────────────────────────────────────── // Habits are recurring activity templates stored on user_profiles. // Each habit auto-generates a task on the matching days of the week. if (action === 'save_habits') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { habits } = payload if (!Array.isArray(habits)) return jsonResponse({ error: 'habits must be an array' }, 400) await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ habits }) }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, saved: habits.length }) } if (action === 'get_habits') { const res = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=habits', { headers: { 'apikey': Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + (Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey) } } ) const rows = asArray(await res.json()) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, habits: rows[0]?.habits || [] }) } // ── save_user_connection ────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Lets a rep connect their personal notetaker account (Fireflies, Fathom etc.) // independently of the org-level config. Per-user connections take priority // in the sync hierarchy: per-user → org-level → email parsing fallback. if (action === 'save_user_connection') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { provider, api_key, provider_email } = payload if (!provider) return jsonResponse({ error: 'provider required' }, 400) await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_connections', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'resolution=merge-duplicates' }, body: JSON.stringify({ user_id: userId, org_id: orgCfg.org_id, provider, api_key: api_key || null, provider_email: provider_email || null }) }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true }) } if (action === 'get_user_connections') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const res = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_connections?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=id,provider,provider_email,last_synced_at,connected_at', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, connections: asArray(await res.json()) }) } if (action === 'delete_user_connection') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { provider } = payload await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_connections?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&provider=eq.' + provider, { method: 'DELETE', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true }) } // ── scan_notetaker_emails ───────────────────────────────────────────────── // Standalone action (not tied to IvR) that scans Gmail for ALL notetaker // emails in the last N days, runs rich extraction on each, and stores results // in meeting_transcripts + account_intelligence. // // This is the universal Tier 1 approach — works for every rep regardless // of which notetaker they use, with zero additional config. null; let bestScore = 0 for (const a of acctRoots) { let score = 0 if (a.nameRoot && searchText.includes(a.nameRoot)) score = 80 else if (a.domainRoot && participants.some((p: string) => extractBrandRoot(p.split('@')[1] || '') === a.domainRoot)) score = 95 else if (a.account_name && searchText.includes(a.account_name.toLowerCase())) score = 70 if (score > bestScore) { bestScore = score; best = a } } return bestScore >= 70 ? { id: best.id, user_id: best.user_id } : null } // ── Fireflies adapter ───────────────────────────────────────────────── const syncFireflies = async () => Analyse this meeting transcript and extract verified signals. Meeting: "${t.title}" Participants: ${participants.join(', ')} Duration: ${Math.round((t.duration || 0) / 60)} minutes Notetaker summary: ${bulletSummary} FULL TRANSCRIPT (extract signals from this — it is far more accurate than the summary): ${fullText} Return ONLY valid JSON: { "sentiment": "positive|neutral|negative", "summary": "2-3 sentence deal summary — what was decided, what's next", "key_quotes": [{"speaker": "name", "quote": "exact verbatim quote", "signal_type": "budget|timeline|objection|expansion|competitor|positive|risk"}], "budget_signals": [{"amount": null_or_number, '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + acct.id + '&select=signal_score', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const curAcct = asArray(await curRes.json())[0] const newScore = Math.max(10, Math.min(95, (curAcct?.signal_score || 30) + (analysis.signal_score_delta || 0))) await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + acct.id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ signal_score: newScore, signal_score_at: new Date().toISOString() }) }) // Record in history await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signal_history', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: orgId, account_id: acct.id, signal_score: newScore, pipeline_tier: newScore >= 40 ? 'verified' : 'partial', source: 'notetaker_transcript' }) }).catch(() => {}) } } synced.push(t.title || t.id) } catch(e: any) { errors2.push((t.title || t.id) + ': ' + e.message) } } return { synced: synced.length, transcripts: transcripts.length, errors: errors2 } } // ── Read.ai adapter ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── // API: https://api.read.ai/v1 // Auth: Bearer token (from account settings or OAuth token) // Transcript: turns[] with speaker.name + text per turn const syncReadAi = async () => { const RA_BASE = 'https://api.read.ai/v1' const raH = { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + resolvedKey, 'Accept': 'application/json' } // Fetch meetings from the last 30 days const since = Date.now() - 30 * 86400000 const listRes = await fetch( RA_BASE + '/meetings?start_time_ms.gte=' + since + '&limit=20', { headers: raH } ) if (!listRes.ok) throw new Error('Read.ai meetings list: ' + listRes.status + ' ' + await listRes.text()) const listData = await listRes.json() const meetings = (listData.meetings || listData.results || []) .filter((m: any) => m.end_time_ms) // only completed meetings const synced: string[] = [] const errors3: string[] = [] for (const mtg of meetings.slice(0, 20)) { try { // Fetch full meeting with transcript expanded const detRes = await fetch( RA_BASE + '/meetings/' + mtg.id + '?expand[]=transcript', { headers: raH } ) if (!detRes.ok) continue const det: any = await detRes.json() const meetingDate = det.start_time_ms ? new Date(det.start_time_ms).toISOString().split('T')[0] : new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] const durationSecs = det.start_time_ms && det.end_time_ms ? Math.round((det.end_time_ms - det.start_time_ms) / 1000) : null const participants: string[] = (det.participants || []).map((p: any) => p.email ? p.name + ' <' + p.email + '>' : p.name ).filter(Boolean) // Build full transcript text from turns const turns = det.transcript?.turns || [] const fullTranscript = turns.map((t: any) => (t.speaker?.name || 'Speaker') + ': ' + t.text ).join('\n').slice(0, 12000) // Fallback: use summary if no transcript turns const analysisText = fullTranscript || det.summary || det.transcript?.text || '' if (!analysisText || analysisText.length < 50) continue const acct = matchTranscriptToAccount(det.title || '', participants) const prompt = buildNotetakerGeminiPrompt(analysisText, 'read_ai', acct ? acctRoots.find((a: any) => a.id === acct.id)?.account_name : undefined) const gRes = await callGeminiWithRetry(GEMINI_URL, { contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }], generationConfig: { temperature: 0.1, maxOutputTokens: 800 } }) if (isGeminiQuotaError(gRes)) { errors3.push('Gemini quota'); break } const gText = gRes?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || '' const jsonMatch = gText.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/) let intel: any = {} try { if (jsonMatch) intel = JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]) } catch(e) {} await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/meeting_transcripts', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'resolution=merge-duplicates,return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: orgId, account_id: acct?.id || null, rep_user_id: acct?.user_id || null, provider: 'read_ai', external_id: det.id, title: intel.title || det.title, meeting_date: meetingDate, duration_secs: durationSecs, participants, transcript_url: det.report_url, summary: intel.summary || det.summary || '', key_quotes: intel.key_quotes || [], action_items: intel.action_items || [], budget_signals: intel.budget_signals || [], objections: intel.objections || [], sentiment: intel.sentiment || (det.metrics?.sentiment > 0.3 ? 'positive' : det.metrics?.sentiment < -0.1 ? 'negative' : 'neutral'), next_steps: intel.next_steps || null, competitor_mentions: intel.competitor_mentions || [], signal_score_delta: intel.signal_score_delta || 0, raw_transcript: fullTranscript.slice(0, 50000), raw_payload: { read_score: det.metrics?.read_score, sentiment: det.metrics?.sentiment, engagement: det.metrics?.engagement, platform: det.platform, participants: det.participants } }) }) // Bump signal score for matched account if (acct?.id && (intel.signal_score_delta || 0) !== 0) { const curRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + acct.id + '&select=signal_score', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const cur = asArray(await curRes.json())[0] const newScore = Math.max(10, Math.min(95, (cur?.signal_score || 30) + intel.signal_score_delta)) await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + acct.id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ signal_score: newScore, signal_score_at: new Date().toISOString() }) }) await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signal_history', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: orgId, account_id: acct.id, signal_score: newScore, pipeline_tier: newScore >= 40 ? 'verified' : 'partial', source: 'notetaker_transcript' }) }).catch(() => {}) } synced.push(det.title || det.id) } catch(e: any) { errors3.push((mtg.title || mtg.id) + ': ' + e.message) } } return { synced: synced.length, transcripts: meetings.length, errors: errors3 } } let result: any if (resolvedProvider === 'fireflies') result = await syncFireflies() else if (resolvedProvider === 'read_ai' || resolvedProvider === 'readai') result = await syncReadAi() else return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unsupported notetaker: ' + resolvedProvider + '. Supported: fireflies, read_ai. For others, use email scanning.' }, 400) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, provider, transcripts_analysed: result.synced, transcripts_found: result.transcripts, errors: result.errors, synced_at: new Date().toISOString() }) } // ── get_meeting_transcripts ─────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns analysed meeting transcripts for one account or org-wide. if (action === 'get_meeting_transcripts') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { account_id, days = 30 } = payload const since = new Date(Date.now() - days * 86400000).toISOString() let filter = 'org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&meeting_date=gte.' + since.split('T')[0] if (account_id) filter += '&account_id=eq.' + account_id const res = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/meeting_transcripts?' + filter + '&order=meeting_date.desc&limit=20&select=id,title,meeting_date,duration_secs,participants,summary,sentiment,key_quotes,action_items,budget_signals,objections,next_steps,signal_score_delta,transcript_url,account_id,rep_user_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, transcripts: asArray(await res.json()) }) } // ── send_email_via_provider ─────────────────────────────────────────────── // Send an email via the rep's connected Gmail or Outlook account. // Called from the MCP server when Claude has drafted and the user has confirmed. // The sent email automatically appears in the Gmail/Outlook sent folder and // will be picked up as a verified signal on the next coverage check. if (action === 'send_email_via_provider') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { to, subject, body, cc, account_name } = payload if (!to || !subject || !body) return jsonResponse({ error: 'to, subject and body are required' }, 400) const tokenRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=*&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const tokenRows = asArray(await tokenRes.json()) if (!tokenRows?.length) return jsonResponse({ error: 'No email connected' }, 400) const tokRow = tokenRows[0] const provider = tokRow.provider || 'google' const tokenResult = provider === 'microsoft' ? await getValidMicrosoftToken(tokRow, userId, SUPABASE_URL, SVC) : await getValidGmailToken(tokRow, userId, SUPABASE_URL, SVC, GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET) if (tokenResult.refreshFailed) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Email token expired — reconnect in the You tab' }, 401) const accessToken = tokenResult.accessToken if (provider === 'microsoft') { // Send via Microsoft Graph const message: any = { subject, body: { contentType: 'HTML', content: body.includes('<') ? body : body.replace(/\n/g, '
') }, toRecipients: [{ emailAddress: { address: to } }] } if (cc) message.ccRecipients = cc.split(',').map((e: string) => ({ emailAddress: { address: e.trim() } })) const res = await fetch('https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/me/sendMail', { method: 'POST', headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ message, saveToSentItems: true }) }) if (!res.ok && res.status !== 202) { const err = await res.text() return jsonResponse({ error: 'Outlook send failed: ' + err }, 400) } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, provider: 'outlook', to, subject, sent_at: new Date().toISOString() }) } else { // Send via Gmail API — requires gmail.send scope // Build RFC 2822 message const fromName = tokRow.email || '' const ccLine = cc ? `Cc: ${cc}\r\n` : '' const rawMsg = `From: ${fromName}\r\nTo: ${to}\r\n${ccLine}Subject: ${subject}\r\nContent-Type: text/html; charset=utf-8\r\nMIME-Version: 1.0\r\n\r\n${body.includes('<') ? body : body.replace(/\n/g, '
')}` const encoded = btoa(unescape(encodeURIComponent(rawMsg))).replace(/\+/g, '-').replace(/\//g, '_').replace(/=+$/, '') const res = await fetch('https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages/send', { method: 'POST', headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ raw: encoded }) }) const data = await res.json() if (data.error) { // Likely missing gmail.send scope if (data.error?.code === 403 || data.error?.status === 'PERMISSION_DENIED') { return jsonResponse({ error: 'Gmail send permission not granted. In SamoraTrack: You tab → disconnect Gmail → reconnect (the new scope request includes send permission).', error_code: 'scope_missing' }, 403) } return jsonResponse({ error: 'Gmail send failed: ' + (data.error?.message || JSON.stringify(data.error)) }, 400) } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, provider: 'gmail', to, subject, message_id: data.id, sent_at: new Date().toISOString() }) } } // ── retag_seq_channels ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── // One-shot action: scans all sequencing_signals for this org and re-classifies // channel based on campaign name patterns. Fixes signals that were synced // before step-level detection was added and defaulted to 'email'. // Run once after deploying — afterwards new syncs tag correctly at source. if (action === 'retag_seq_channels') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const orgId = orgCfg.org_id const sigRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/sequencing_signals?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=id,campaign_name,channel', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } }) const sigs = asArray(await sigRes.json()) let retagged = 0 const updates: { id: string, channel: string }[] = [] for (const s of sigs) { const name = (s.campaign_name || '').toLowerCase() let newChannel = 'email' if (/\bcall\b|calling|phone|dialer|cold.?call|voice/i.test(name)) newChannel = 'call' else if (/\blinkedin\b|inmail|li\s/i.test(name)) newChannel = 'linkedin' else if (/whatsapp|wapp/i.test(name)) newChannel = 'whatsapp' if (newChannel !== (s.channel || 'email')) updates.push({ id: s.id, channel: newChannel }) } // Apply updates in batches for (const u of updates) { await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/sequencing_signals?id=eq.' + u.id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ channel: u.channel }) }) retagged++ } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, total: sigs.length, retagged, updates: updates.slice(0, 20) }) } // ── get_sequencing_signals ──────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns sequencing signals for one account or all accounts a rep can see. // Used by the pipeline to show sequencing activity alongside Gmail signals. if (action === 'get_sequencing_signals') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const { account_id, channel, days = 30 } = payload const since = new Date(Date.now() - days * 86400000).toISOString() let filter = 'org_id=eq.' + orgCfg.org_id + '&created_at=gte.' + since if (account_id) filter += '&account_id=eq.' + account_id if (channel) filter += '&channel=eq.' + channel const res = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/sequencing_signals?' + filter + '&order=created_at.desc&limit=200', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const signals = asArray(await res.json()) // Summarise by account for pipeline view const byAccount: Record = {} signals.forEach((s: any) => { const key = s.account_id || s.prospect_company || 'unknown' if (!byAccount[key]) byAccount[key] = { account_id: s.account_id, company: s.prospect_company, email: 0, linkedin: 0, call: 0, whatsapp: 0, replied: 0, total: 0 } byAccount[key][s.channel] = (byAccount[key][s.channel] || 0) + 1 byAccount[key].total++ if (s.replied) byAccount[key].replied++ }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, signals, by_account: Object.values(byAccount).sort((a: any, b: any) => b.total - a.total), synced_at: orgCfg.sequencing_synced_at || null }) } // ── upsert_org_settings ─────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Called by the Samora admin dashboard to save/update configuration for a // client org. Only Samora-level admins (rows in samora_admins table) can // call this — regular users including org super_admins cannot. if (action === 'upsert_org_settings') { const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const adminCheck = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/samora_admins?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=id&limit=1', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const adminRows = await adminCheck.json() if (!Array.isArray(adminRows) || !adminRows.length) { return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unauthorized — Samora admin access required' }, 403) } const { org_id, settings } = payload if (!org_id || !settings) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Missing org_id or settings' }, 400) // Strip any credential fields the client shouldn't be able to overwrite // via a spoofed payload — only update what's explicitly in the allowed list. const allowed = [ 'display_name','logo_url','primary_color', 'email_provider','google_client_id','google_client_secret', 'ms_client_id','ms_client_secret','ms_tenant_id', 'ai_engine','ai_model','ai_api_key', 'deal_stages','role_labels','features','channels', 'stale_days','unanswered_days','lookback_days','intel_lookback_days', 'revenue_stream_types', 'sequencing_provider','sequencing_api_key','sequencing_team_id', 'icp_definition', 'notetaker_provider','notetaker_api_key' ] const safe: Record = {} allowed.forEach(k => { if (settings[k] !== undefined) safe[k] = settings[k] }) // Try PATCH first (row exists) — fall back to POST (new org, no row yet) let upsertRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_settings?org_id=eq.' + org_id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=representation' }, body: JSON.stringify(safe) }) let upsertData = await upsertRes.json() // If PATCH returned empty (no row matched), do a POST insert instead if (Array.isArray(upsertData) && upsertData.length === 0) { safe['org_id'] = org_id upsertRes = await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_settings', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=representation' }, body: JSON.stringify(safe) }) upsertData = await upsertRes.json() } if (!upsertRes.ok) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Save failed', detail: upsertData }, 500) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, saved: upsertData }) } // ── get_org_config ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns the safe-to-expose subset of org_settings to the frontend so the // UI can adapt without any hardcoded values: deal stages render in the // client's own terminology, feature flags toggle surfaces on/off, channel // availability drives which badges show as active vs "coming soon". // Credentials (API keys, OAuth secrets) are NEVER included in this response. if (action === 'get_org_config') { return jsonResponse({ ok: true, orgId: orgCfg.org_id, googleClientId: orgCfg.google_client_id || '', dealStages: orgCfg.deal_stages, roleLabels: orgCfg.role_labels, features: orgCfg.features, channels: orgCfg.channels, revenueStreamTypes: (orgCfg as any).revenue_stream_types || [], thresholds: { stale_days: orgCfg.stale_days, unanswered_days: orgCfg.unanswered_days, lookback_days: orgCfg.lookback_days, intel_lookback_days: orgCfg.intel_lookback_days }, emailProvider: orgCfg.email_provider, aiEngine: orgCfg.ai_engine }) } // ── get_signals ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── if (action === 'get_signals') { const { data: tokenRow } = await supabase .from('gmail_tokens').select('*').eq('user_id', userId).single() if (!tokenRow) return jsonResponse({ error: 'No Gmail connection found.' }, 404) const SB_SERVICE0 = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const tokenResult = await getValidGmailToken(tokenRow, userId, SUPABASE_URL, SB_SERVICE0, GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET) if (tokenResult.refreshFailed) return gmailReconnectNeededResponse(false, tokenRow.email) let accessToken = tokenResult.accessToken // Get recent tasks AND completion notes for context const SB_SERVICE = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] const sevenDaysAgo = new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 86400000).toISOString().split('T')[0] const dtRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/daytrack?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&day_key=gte.' + sevenDaysAgo + '&day_key=lte.' + today + '&select=day_key,data', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const dtData = asArray(await dtRes.json()) const recentTasks: string[] = [] const completionNotes: string[] = [] for (const row of dtData) { const tasks = row.data?.tasks || [] const wins = row.data?.wins || [] tasks.forEach((t: any) => { if (t.text) recentTasks.push(t.text) }) // Completion notes are high-signal — rep described what actually happened wins.forEach((w: any) => { if (w.completionNote) completionNotes.push(`[${row.day_key}] ${w.text}: ${w.completionNote}`) else if (w.fromTask && w.text) completionNotes.push(`[${row.day_key}] Completed: ${w.text}`) }) } const taskContext = recentTasks.length ? 'The rep\'s recent tasks include:\n' + recentTasks.map((t: string) => '- ' + t).join('\n') + '\n\n' : '' const noteContext = completionNotes.length ? 'Completion notes from the rep (high signal — these describe actual meeting/call outcomes):\n' + completionNotes.map((n: string) => '- ' + n).join('\n') + '\n\n' : '' const gmailRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?labelIds=SENT&maxResults=8', { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}` } } ) const gmailData = await gmailRes.json() const messages = gmailData?.messages ?? [] if (!messages.length) { return jsonResponse({ ok: true, signals: [], analysis: { summary: 'No sent emails found.', signals: [] } }) } // Fetch subject + snippet for each email (not just snippet) const emailDetails: string[] = [] for (const m of messages.slice(0, 8)) { const mRes = await fetch( `https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages/${m.id}?format=metadata&metadataHeaders=Subject&metadataHeaders=To&metadataHeaders=Date`, { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}` } } ) const mData = await mRes.json() const hdrs = mData?.payload?.headers || [] const subject = hdrs.find((h: any) => h.name === 'Subject')?.value || '' const to = hdrs.find((h: any) => h.name === 'To')?.value || '' const date = hdrs.find((h: any) => h.name === 'Date')?.value || '' emailDetails.push(`Subject: ${subject}\nTo: ${to}\nDate: ${date}\nSnippet: ${mData.snippet || ''}`) } const snippets = emailDetails.join('\n\n---\n\n') let signals: any[] = [] let summary = '' if (GEMINI_KEY) { try { const geminiRes = await fetch( GEMINI_URL, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ contents: [{ parts: [{ text: `You are SAM, a B2B sales intelligence agent.\n\n${taskContext}${noteContext}Analyse these sent emails and return ONLY valid JSON with "signals" array and "summary" string.\n\nIMPORTANT: Map each signal to the SPECIFIC company/person in the email's To field or Subject — not a generic label. Only create a signal if you can identify a real company or person name from the email.\n\nEach signal: {"type":"hot|warm|cold|no_followup","account":"exact company or person name from email","title":"email subject","body":"one sentence about the deal status","action":"specific next step"}.\n\nEmails:\n${snippets}` }] }], generationConfig: { temperature: 0.2, maxOutputTokens: 800 } }) } ) const geminiData = await geminiRes.json() const text = geminiData?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text ?? '' const match = text.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/) const parsed = match ? JSON.parse(match[0]) : null if (parsed) { signals = parsed.signals ?? []; summary = parsed.summary ?? '' } } catch { /* keep empty */ } } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, signals, analysis: { signals, summary }, gmailEmail: tokenRow.email }) } // ── search_account ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── if (action === 'search_account') { const { query, days, date_from, date_to } = payload if (!query) return jsonResponse({ error: 'Missing query' }, 400) const { data: tokenRow } = await supabase .from('gmail_tokens').select('access_token').eq('user_id', userId).single() if (!tokenRow) return jsonResponse({ connected: false }) let dateFilter = '' if (date_from && date_to) { // Epoch-second boundaries — avoids Gmail resolving YYYY/MM/DD strings // in the account's own timezone, which silently shifts the window. // Also fixes before: previously excluding the entire end day. const epochAfter = Math.floor(new Date(date_from + 'T00:00:00Z').getTime() / 1000) const epochBefore = Math.floor(new Date(date_to + 'T23:59:59Z').getTime() / 1000) + 1 dateFilter = ' after:' + epochAfter + ' before:' + epochBefore } else if ((days ?? 0) > 0) { dateFilter = ' after:' + new Date(Date.now() - days * 86400000).toISOString().split('T')[0].replace(/-/g, '/') } const domainGuess = query.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '') const gmailQuery = 'in:sent ("' + query + '" OR to:' + domainGuess + ')' + dateFilter const searchRes = await fetch( `https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=${encodeURIComponent(gmailQuery)}&maxResults=100`, { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${tokenRow.access_token}` } } ) const searchData = await searchRes.json() const msgRefs = searchData?.messages ?? [] const totalFound = msgRefs.length const threads: any[] = [] for (const ref of msgRefs.slice(0, 30)) { const mRes = await fetch( `https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages/${ref.id}?format=full`, { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${tokenRow.access_token}` } } ) const m = await mRes.json() const hdrs = m.payload?.headers ?? [] const get = (n: string) => hdrs.find((h: any) => h.name === n)?.value ?? '' const extractText = (part: any): string => { if (!part) return '' if (part.mimeType === 'text/plain' && part.body?.data) { const b64 = part.body.data.replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/') try { return atob(b64) } catch { return '' } } if (part.parts) return part.parts.map(extractText).join(' ') return '' } const body = extractText(m.payload).slice(0, 1500).trim() || m.snippet || '' threads.push({ id: m.id, threadId: m.threadId, messageId: get('Message-ID'), inReplyTo: get('In-Reply-To'), subject: get('Subject'), to: get('To'), cc: get('Cc'), date: get('Date'), internalDate: m.internalDate, snippet: m.snippet ?? '', body }) } const inboxDomain = query.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '') const inboxQuery = 'in:inbox from:' + inboxDomain const inboxRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + encodeURIComponent(inboxQuery) + '&maxResults=50', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + tokenRow.access_token } } ) const inboxData = await inboxRes.json() const inboxRefs = inboxData?.messages ??
