string, parent_account_id?: string }[] = [] if (orgId) { const orgAccRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=id,account_name,domain,region,parent_account_id,additional_domains', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) assignedAccounts = asArray(await orgAccRes.json()) } const usedOrgAccounts = assignedAccounts.length > 0 // Same fuzzy resolution used in intent_vs_reality: prefer an assigned // account name match (exact, then first-significant-word), and only // Coverage is account-wise tracking against the rep's ASSIGNED account // list — unlike intent_vs_reality (which reasonably guesses at an // account for ad-hoc task verification), there is no good reason to // invent a pseudo-account from free text here. Doing so previously // produced rows like "Arun" (a colleague's name), "SKUs", "Kenya" — // capitalised words that happened to appear in a task but aren't // accounts at all. Tasks where resolveAccountForTask() didn't match // an assigned account are excluded from the coverage grid entirely. // Build per-account activity totals from LOGGED quantities — "Pladis // stakeholder UK 10 emails" contributes 10 to Pladis's email count, not // 1. This is what was missing before: every task counted as exactly // one unit regardless of what the rep actually wrote. type Bucket = { total: number, loggedTotal: number } type AccountBucket = { account: string, taskTexts: string[], searchTermsUnion: Set, call: Bucket, email: Bucket, meeting: Bucket, linkedin: Bucket, whatsapp: Bucket, other: Bucket } const accountsMap: Record = {} function freshBucket(): AccountBucket { return { account: '', taskTexts: [], searchTermsUnion: new Set(), call: { total: 0, loggedTotal: 0 }, email: { total: 0, loggedTotal: 0 }, meeting: { total: 0, loggedTotal: 0 }, linkedin: { total: 0, loggedTotal: 0 }, whatsapp: { total: 0, loggedTotal: 0 }, other: { total: 0, loggedTotal: 0 } } } tasks.forEach((t: any) => { const text = t.text || '' if (!text) return const resolved = resolveAccountForTask(text, assignedAccounts) const { quantity, type } = parseActivityQuantity(text) if (!resolved.matchedAssignedAccount || !resolved.displayName) { // Task didn't resolve to a specific account. // If it's a channel task (linkedin/whatsapp/call) with a number, // it's likely a general cadence — distribute across ALL accounts // that are in the map already, or store under a special __general__ key. if (['linkedin','whatsapp','call'].includes(type) && quantity > 1) { if (!accountsMap['__general__']) { accountsMap['__general__'] = freshBucket() accountsMap['__general__'].account = '__general__' } accountsMap['__general__'][type].total += 1 accountsMap['__general__'][type].loggedTotal += quantity if (!accountsMap['__general__'].taskTexts.includes(text)) accountsMap['__general__'].taskTexts.push(text) } return } const accountName = resolved.displayName if (!accountsMap[accountName]) { accountsMap[accountName] = freshBucket(); accountsMap[accountName].account = accountName } const bucket = accountsMap[accountName][type] bucket.total += 1 bucket.loggedTotal += quantity if (!accountsMap[accountName].taskTexts.includes(text)) accountsMap[accountName].taskTexts.push(text) resolved.searchTerms.forEach((term: string) => accountsMap[accountName].searchTermsUnion.add(term)) }) // Distribute __general__ channel tasks across all resolved accounts // (e.g. "LinkedIn 30" → split across all accounts working this period) const generalBucket = accountsMap['__general__'] if (generalBucket) { delete accountsMap['__general__'] const resolvedAccounts = Object.keys(accountsMap) if (resolvedAccounts.length > 0) { const perAccount = Math.ceil(generalBucket.linkedin.loggedTotal / resolvedAccounts.length) resolvedAccounts.forEach(a => { if (generalBucket.linkedin.loggedTotal > 0) { accountsMap[a].linkedin.total++ accountsMap[a].linkedin.loggedTotal += perAccount accountsMap[a].taskTexts.push(...generalBucket.taskTexts.filter((t: string) => !accountsMap[a].taskTexts.includes(t))) } }) } } const accounts = Object.keys(accountsMap) if (!accounts.length) { return jsonResponse({ connected: true, gmailEmail: tokenRows[0].email, dateRange: { from: coverageFrom, to: coverageTo }, accountGrid: [], usedOrgAccounts, noAssignedAccounts: !usedOrgAccounts, summary: { totalAccounts: 0, coveredAccounts: 0, totalLogged: 0, totalVerified: 0, coverageRate: 0 } }) } // ── Fetch sequencing signals for this rep's accounts in the date range ── const seqSignalsRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/sequencing_signals' + '?rep_user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&created_at=gte.' + coverageFrom + 'T00:00:00Z' + '&created_at=lte.' + coverageTo + 'T23:59:59Z' + '&select=account_id,channel,event_type,replied,completed,prospect_company,prospect_email,total_opens,total_clicks,campaign_name', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const seqSignals = asArray(await seqSignalsRes.json()) // Better fuzzy matching: normalise both sides to bare words for comparison const normaliseCompany = (s: string) => normCompanyName(s) // Build lookup by account_id (exact) and by normalised name + brand root (fuzzy) const seqByAccountId: Record }> = {} const seqByNorm: Record = {} const seqByRoot: Record = {} // brand root index const addSig = (key: string, map: any, sig: any) => { if (!map[key]) map[key] = { email:0, linkedin:0, call:0, whatsapp:0, replied:0, opens:0, clicks:0, campaigns:new Set() } const ch = sig.channel || 'email' if (['email','linkedin','call','whatsapp'].includes(ch)) map[key][ch]++ if (sig.replied) map[key].replied++ map[key].opens += sig.total_opens || 0 map[key].clicks += sig.total_clicks || 0 if (sig.campaign_name) map[key].campaigns.add(sig.campaign_name) } for (const sig of seqSignals) { if (sig.account_id) addSig(sig.account_id, seqByAccountId, sig) const norm = normaliseCompany(sig.prospect_company || '') if (norm.length >= 3) addSig(norm, seqByNorm, sig) // Also index by brand root extracted from prospect email domain const emailDomain = (sig.prospect_email || '').split('@')[1] || '' const root = extractBrandRoot(emailDomain) if (root.length >= 4) addSig(root, seqByRoot, sig) } // For each account, find best match: id > norm > brand-root-from-domain > prefix const getSeqData = (accountName: string, accountId?: string) => { if (accountId && seqByAccountId[accountId]) return seqByAccountId[accountId] const norm = normaliseCompany(accountName) if (seqByNorm[norm]) return seqByNorm[norm] // Try matching account's stored domain brand root against signal email domain roots const acctMatch = (assignedAccounts as any[]).find(a => a.account_name === accountName) const acctRoot = acctMatch?.domain ? extractBrandRoot(acctMatch.domain) : normCompanyName(accountName) if (acctRoot.length >= 4 && seqByRoot[acctRoot]) return seqByRoot[acctRoot] // Prefix fallback for (const key of Object.keys(seqByNorm)) { if (norm.length >= 4 && (key.startsWith(norm) || norm.startsWith(key))) return seqByNorm[key] } return null } // ── Gmail date-boundary fix ─────────────────────────────────────────── // Gmail's after:/before: operators with YYYY/MM/DD strings are resolved // in the GMAIL ACCOUNT's own timezone setting — not the rep's local // timezone, and not UTC. For a rep in IST with a Gmail account whose // timezone differs (common default/unconfigured cases), this silently // shifts the search window by several hours, pulling in part of the // adjacent day — exactly the "Today picks up today + yesterday" bug. // Fix: use Unix epoch SECONDS instead. Gmail resolves epoch values // unambiguously with no timezone interpretation at all. const afterDate = Math.floor(new Date(coverageFrom + 'T00:00:00Z').getTime() / 1000) const beforeDate = Math.floor(new Date(coverageTo + 'T23:59:59Z').getTime() / 1000) + 1 const accountGrid: any[] = [] const coverageApiErrors: any[] = [] // ── Fetch SamoraTrack daytracks for the coverage period ──────────────── // Used to surface self-attested call signals from the structured close-out // form (activityOutcome field). Third and weakest layer of call verification. let daytracksForPeriod: any[] = [] try { const dtRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/daytrack?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&day_key=gte.' + coverageFrom + '&day_key=lte.' + coverageTo + '&select=day_key,data', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) daytracksForPeriod = asArray(await dtRes.json()) } catch(e) { /* non-fatal */ } for (const account of accounts.slice(0, 20)) { const bucket = accountsMap[account] const assignedMatch = assignedAccounts.find(a => a.account_name === account) const accountDomain = assignedMatch?.domain || '' const extraDomains: string[] = (assignedMatch as any)?.additional_domains || [] // Brand root catches ALL domain variants for this account without knowing each one // e.g. 'lactalis' catches in.lactalis.com, fr.lactalis.com, lactalis-international.fr, lactalis.sa const brandRoot = accountDomain ? extractBrandRoot(accountDomain) : normCompanyName(account) const seqData = getSeqData(account, assignedMatch?.id) // Build Gmail query using brand root — catches all subdomain/TLD variants const termsForSearch = new Set(bucket.searchTermsUnion) termsForSearch.add(account) const orClause = Array.from(termsForSearch).map(t => '"' + t + '"').join(' OR ') const domainParts: string[] = [] if (brandRoot.length >= 4) domainParts.push('to:@' + brandRoot) // partial domain match in Gmail else if (accountDomain) domainParts.push('to:' + accountDomain) extraDomains.forEach(d => domainParts.push('to:' + d)) const domainFilter = domainParts.join(' OR ') const q = encodeURIComponent('in:sent (' + orClause + (domainFilter ? ' OR ' + domainFilter : '') + ') after:' + afterDate + ' before:' + beforeDate) // ── Email search — provider-aware routing ───────────────────────────── // Gmail uses query string syntax; Microsoft Graph uses OData filter. // Both paths return a simple count + message list, keeping all // downstream logic identical regardless of which email provider the rep uses. let verifiedEmailCount = 0 let replyCount = 0 let linkedinVerified = 0 if (emailProvider === 'microsoft') { // Microsoft Graph — Outlook/Exchange/Hotmail const termsList = Array.from(termsForSearch) as string[] const { count: sentCount } = await searchOutlookSent(accessToken, termsList, brandRoot, afterDate, beforeDate) verifiedEmailCount = sentCount const { count: inboxCount, messages: inboxMsgs } = await searchOutlookInbox(accessToken, [brandRoot, ...termsList], brandRoot, afterDate, beforeDate) replyCount = inboxCount // LinkedIn notifications also come via email — works the same in Outlook try { const liFilter = `receivedDateTime ge ${new Date(afterDate * 1000).toISOString()} and receivedDateTime le ${new Date(beforeDate * 1000).toISOString()}` const liRes = await fetch( 'https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/me/mailFolders/Inbox/messages' + '?$filter=' + encodeURIComponent(liFilter) + '&$search=' + encodeURIComponent('"linkedin.com" AND (' + termsList.map(t => '"' + t + '"').join(' OR ') + ')') + '&$top=20&$select=id,subject,from', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) if (liRes.ok) { const liData = await liRes.json(); linkedinVerified = liData?.value?.length || 0 } } catch(e) { /* non-fatal */ } } else { // Gmail API — existing path const res = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + q + '&maxResults=50', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const data = await res.json() if (isScopeError(data)) { return jsonResponse({ connected: true, scopeError: true, gmailEmail: tokenRows[0].email, error: (rep_user_id ? 'This rep\u2019s' : 'Your') + ' Gmail connection is missing required permissions. Reconnect Gmail to re-grant access.' }, 403) } verifiedEmailCount = data?.messages?.length || 0 if (data?.error) coverageApiErrors.push({ account, error: data.error }) const inboxQ = encodeURIComponent('in:inbox from:' + brandRoot + ' after:' + afterDate + ' before:' + beforeDate) const inboxRes = await fetch('https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + inboxQ + '&maxResults=20', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } }) const inboxData = await inboxRes.json() replyCount = inboxData?.messages?.length || 0 try { const liQ = encodeURIComponent('(from:notification@linkedin.com OR from:notifications-noreply@linkedin.com) (' + Array.from(termsForSearch).map(t => '"' + t + '"').join(' OR ') + ') after:' + afterDate + ' before:' + beforeDate) const liRes = await fetch('https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + liQ + '&maxResults=20', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } }) const liData = await liRes.json() linkedinVerified = liData?.messages?.length || 0 } catch(e) { /* non-fatal */ } } // ── Fetch calendar events for this account (calls + meetings) ───────── // Broad search: any event mentioning the account — not just call-keyword events. // Callers of resolveChannelSignals get the full event list; the function // itself classifies call vs meeting based on duration and keywords. let calendarEventsForAccount: any[] = [] try { const calProvider = emailProvider === 'microsoft' ? 'https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/me/calendarView' + '?startDateTime=' + encodeURIComponent(coverageFrom + 'T00:00:00Z') + '&endDateTime=' + encodeURIComponent(coverageTo + 'T23:59:59Z') + '&$top=20&$select=id,subject,start,end,attendees,bodyPreview' : 'https://www.googleapis.com/calendar/v3/calendars/primary/events' + '?q=' + encodeURIComponent(account) + '&timeMin=' + new Date(coverageFrom + 'T00:00:00Z').toISOString() + '&timeMax=' + new Date(coverageTo + 'T23:59:59Z').toISOString() + '&singleEvents=true&maxResults=20' const calRes = await fetch(calProvider, { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } }) if (calRes.ok) { const calData = await calRes.json() calendarEventsForAccount = (calData.items || calData.value || []).filter((e: any) => (e.summary || e.subject || '').toLowerCase().includes(account.toLowerCase()) ) } } catch(e) { /* non-fatal */ } // ── Normalise sequencing signals for this account ───────────────────── // Simple filter on the raw signal rows — plain array, no map/fromEntries. const acctSeqSignals = seqSignals.filter((s: any) => (assignedMatch?.id && s.account_id === assignedMatch.id) || normCompanyName(s.prospect_company || '') === normCompanyName(account) || (assignedMatch?.domain && extractBrandRoot(s.prospect_email?.split('@')[1] || '') === extractBrandRoot(assignedMatch.domain)) ) // ── Resolve all channels via framework function ─────────────────────── const signals = resolveChannelSignals({ account, dateFrom: coverageFrom, dateTo: coverageTo, daytracks: daytracksForPeriod, seqSignals: acctSeqSignals, seqDataTotals: seqData || null, // ← fuzzy-matched totals from getSeqData() emailVerifiedCount: verifiedEmailCount, inboxReplyCount: replyCount, linkedinNotifCount: linkedinVerified, calendarEvents: calendarEventsForAccount }) // Email: apply the narrow-window protection (seq signals are date-imprecise) const periodSpanDays = Math.max(1, Math.round((new Date(coverageTo).getTime() - new Date(coverageFrom).getTime()) / 86400000) + 1) const isNarrowWindow = periodSpanDays <= 1 const seqEmailCount = (seqData?.email || 0) if (isNarrowWindow && seqEmailCount > verifiedEmailCount) { // For single-day: keep only Gmail/Outlook count (dated), surface seq as note signals.email.verified = verifiedEmailCount signals.email.seqNotDateAccurate = true signals.email.seqVerified = seqEmailCount } accountGrid.push({ account, accountId: assignedMatch?.id || null, call: { logged: bucket.call.loggedTotal, verified: signals.call.verified, source: signals.call.source, detail: signals.call.detail, selfAttested: signals.call.selfAttested }, email: { logged: bucket.email.loggedTotal, verified: signals.email.verified, source: signals.email.source, detail: signals.email.detail, gmailVerified: verifiedEmailCount, seqVerified: seqEmailCount, seqNotDateAccurate: (signals.email as any).seqNotDateAccurate || false }, linkedin: { logged: bucket.linkedin.loggedTotal, verified: signals.linkedin.verified, source: signals.linkedin.source, detail: signals.linkedin.detail }, whatsapp: { logged: bucket.whatsapp.loggedTotal, verified: signals.whatsapp.verified, source: signals.whatsapp.source, detail: signals.whatsapp.detail }, meeting: { logged: bucket.meeting.loggedTotal, verified: signals.meeting.verified, source: signals.meeting.source, detail: '' }, repliesReceived: signals.replies, seqOpens: seqData?.opens || 0, seqClicks: seqData?.clicks || 0, campaigns: seqData ? Array.from(seqData.campaigns || []).join(', ') : null, taskTexts: bucket.taskTexts }) } const totalLogged = accountGrid.reduce((s, a) => s + a.call.logged + a.email.logged + a.meeting.logged + a.linkedin.logged + a.whatsapp.logged, 0) const totalVerified = accountGrid.reduce((s, a) => s + a.email.verified + a.call.verified + a.linkedin.verified + a.whatsapp.verified, 0) const coveredAccounts = accountGrid.filter(a => a.email.verified > 0 || a.call.verified > 0 || a.linkedin.verified > 0 || a.whatsapp.verified > 0).length const hasSeqData = seqSignals.length > 0 return jsonResponse({ connected: true, gmailEmail: tokenRows[0].email, usedOrgAccounts, dateRange: { from: coverageFrom, to: coverageTo }, accountGrid, hasSeqData, apiErrors: coverageApiErrors.length ? coverageApiErrors : undefined, summary: { totalAccounts: accountGrid.length, coveredAccounts, totalLogged, totalVerified, coverageRate: accountGrid.length ? Math.round((coveredAccounts / accountGrid.length) * 100) : 0 } }) } // ── intent_vs_reality ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── if (action === 'intent_vs_reality') { const { rep_user_id, date_from, date_to } = payload const targetUserId = rep_user_id || userId if (rep_user_id) { const SB_SERVICE_IVR = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const profileRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=role', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE_IVR, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE_IVR } } ) const profiles = asArray(await profileRes.json()) const role = profiles?.[0]?.role if (!canSeeTeam(role)) { return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unauthorized', connected: false }, 403) } } const SB_SERVICE = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const tokenRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&select=*', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const tokenRows = asArray(await tokenRes.json()) if (!tokenRows?.length) return jsonResponse({ connected: false, error: 'Gmail not connected' }) let accessToken = tokenRows[0].access_token const tokenResultIVR = await getValidGmailToken(tokenRows[0], targetUserId, SUPABASE_URL, SB_SERVICE, GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET) if (tokenResultIVR.refreshFailed) return gmailReconnectNeededResponse(!!rep_user_id, tokenRows[0].email) accessToken = tokenResultIVR.accessToken const fromDate = date_from || new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 86400000).toISOString().split('T')[0] const toDate = date_to || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] const dtRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/daytrack?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&day_key=gte.' + fromDate + '&day_key=lte.' + toDate + '&select=day_key,data&order=day_key.desc', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const dtData = asArray(await dtRes.json()) // Load the rep's actual assigned accounts — these are ground truth and // far more reliable than guessing proper nouns out of free text. A task // like "send Ferrero NDA to Laxmi" should match on "Ferrero" (an assigned // account), not "Laxmi" (an internal colleague who happens to be capitalised). const repProfileRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&select=org_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const repProfileData = asArray(await repProfileRes.json()) const repOrgId = repProfileData?.[0]?.org_id let assignedAccounts: { id: string, account_name: string, domain: string, region?: string, parent_account_id?: string }[] = [] if (repOrgId) { const orgAccRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&org_id=eq.' + repOrgId + '&select=id,account_name,domain,region,parent_account_id,additional_domains', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) assignedAccounts = asArray(await orgAccRes.json()) } // ── Collect tasks — exclude pure internal tasks at collection time ────── // parseTaskIntent tells us whether a task is verifiable at all. // Internal tasks (MOM, deck prep, CRM update) are collected but flagged; // they get signal='internal' and skip all Gmail/calendar searches. const allTasks: any[] = [] for (const row of dtData) { const tasks = row.data?.tasks || row.data?.priorities || [] tasks.forEach((t: any) => { if (!t.text) return const intent = parseTaskIntent(t.text) // Only include tasks that have some kind of verifiable activity or are internal-but-done // Exclude purely passive tasks with no action component const hasAccountContext = resolveAccountForTask(t.text, assignedAccounts).displayName !== null if (intent.intentType !== 'unknown' || hasAccountContext) { allTasks.push({ date: row.day_key, text: t.text, done: t.done || false, priority: t.priority || t.text?.startsWith('*') || false, intent, activityOutcome: t.activityOutcome || null, completionNote: t.completionNote || null }) } }) } const results: any[] = [] const ivrDebug: any[] = [] // lacks gmail.readonly scope, every subsequent search would otherwise // silently return zero evidence (an error object has no `.messages`, // so `gData?.messages?.length > 0` is just false) and every task would // wrongly show as unverified with no explanation. Fail fast instead. if (allTasks.length > 0) { const probeRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?maxResults=1', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const probeData = await probeRes.json() if (isScopeError(probeData)) { return jsonResponse({ connected: true, scopeError: true, gmailEmail: tokenRows[0].email, error: (rep_user_id ? 'This rep\u2019s' : 'Your') + ' Gmail connection is missing required permissions. ' + (rep_user_id ? 'They need' : 'Go') + ' to re-connect Gmail to re-grant access \u2014 refreshing the token will not fix this.' }, 403) } } for (const task of allTasks) { const intent = task.intent || parseTaskIntent(task.text || '') const resolved = resolveAccountForTask(task.text || '', assignedAccounts) const account = resolved.displayName const candidates = resolved.allCandidates.length ? resolved.allCandidates : [resolved.displayName].filter(Boolean) const strongTerms = resolved.searchTerms // ── INTERNAL TASKS: skip all verification, return with 'internal' signal ── if (intent.intentType === 'internal') { results.push({ date: task.date, text: task.text, done: task.done, priority: task.priority, account, signal: task.done ? 'internal' : 'internal_pending', emailEvidence: false, replyEvidence: false, emailSubject: '', emailTo: '', source: 'none', activityType: 'other', replyAnalysis: null, intent: intent.intentType, quantityClaimed: intent.quantityClaimed }) continue } // ── CHANNEL-SPECIFIC NO-EXTERNAL-VERIFICATION TASKS ────────────────── // For calls, LinkedIn, and WhatsApp, no external system sees the activity. // The rep's own log is the primary evidence — prioritise it accordingly. // Signal levels: // attested → rep marked done + structured outcome (strongest rep signal) // task_done → rep marked done, no structured outcome (confirmed completion) // no_source → rep marked done but truly no verification path available // gap → not done at all if (['linkedin', 'whatsapp', 'call'].includes(intent.intentType)) { let repSignal: string if (!task.done) { repSignal = 'gap' } else if (intent.intentType === 'call') { const CALL_OUTCOMES = ['no_answer','spoke_briefly','full_conversation','meeting_booked','not_interested'] if (CALL_OUTCOMES.includes(task.activityOutcome || '')) { repSignal = 'attested' // rep confirmed outcome via structured form } else { // task_done + SmartReach has ANY activity for this account = verified // Even if SR call signals are wrongly tagged as 'email', the presence // of SR activity corroborates the rep's completed call task. const seqForAcct = getSeqData(account) const hasSeqActivity = seqForAcct && ((seqForAcct.email||0) + (seqForAcct.call||0) + (seqForAcct.linkedin||0) + (seqForAcct.opens||0)) > 0 repSignal = hasSeqActivity ? 'verified' : 'task_done' } } else if (intent.intentType === 'linkedin') { const LI_OUTCOMES = ['requests_sent','connections_accepted','messages_sent','replies_received','meeting_booked'] repSignal = LI_OUTCOMES.includes(task.activityOutcome || '') ? 'attested' : task.done ? 'task_done' : 'gap' } else { // WhatsApp repSignal = task.done ? 'task_done' : 'gap' } results.push({ date: task.date, text: task.text, done: task.done, priority: task.priority, account, signal: repSignal, emailEvidence: false, replyEvidence: false, emailSubject: '', emailTo: '', source: 'none', activityType: intent.intentType as any, replyAnalysis: null, intent: intent.intentType, quantityClaimed: intent.quantityClaimed, emailsFound: 0, verificationRatio: 0, activityOutcome: task.activityOutcome || null, completionNote: task.completionNote || null }) continue } let emailEvidence = false let replyEvidence = false let emailSubject = '' let emailTo = '' let bestScore = 0 let emailsFoundCount = 0 // actual count found in Gmail (for quantity comparison) if (candidates.length > 0 && (intent.isVerifiableViaGmail || intent.isVerifiableViaCalendar)) { // Epoch-second boundaries — see account_coverage for why YYYY/MM/DD // string dates are unreliable (Gmail resolves them in the account's // own timezone, not the rep's, silently shifting the day boundary). const after = Math.floor(new Date(fromDate + 'T00:00:00Z').getTime() / 1000) const before = Math.floor(new Date(toDate + 'T23:59:59Z').getTime() / 1000) + 1 // Search Gmail sent folder. // For bulk email tasks (quantityClaimed > 1), also add brand-root domain // filter so we catch emails sent TO the account, not just emails about them. const searchTerms = strongTerms.map(c => '"' + c + '"').join(' OR ') const acctMatch = assignedAccounts.find((a: any) => a.account_name === account) const acctBrandRoot = acctMatch?.domain ? extractBrandRoot(acctMatch.domain) : normCompanyName(account || '') // For outreach tasks: add to-domain filter (verifies emails actually SENT TO the company) const toDomainFilter = (intent.intentType === 'email_outreach' && acctBrandRoot.length >= 4) ? ' OR to:@' + acctBrandRoot : '' const q = encodeURIComponent('in:sent (' + searchTerms + toDomainFilter + ') after:' + after + ' before:' + before) try { const gRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + q + '&maxResults=50', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const gData = await gRes.json() emailsFoundCount = gData?.messages?.length || 0 // actual count for comparison const debugEntry: any = { task: task.text, account, intent: intent.intentType, quantityClaimed: intent.quantityClaimed, emailsFound: emailsFoundCount, query: decodeURIComponent(q), gmailApiError: gData?.error || null } if (gData?.messages?.length > 0) { // ── IMPROVED: pick the BEST matching email, not just the first ── let bestMsgId = gData.messages[0].id let bestSubject = '' let bestTo = '' let bestSnippet = '' for (const msg of gData.messages.slice(0, 10)) { const mRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages/' + msg.id + '?format=metadata&metadataHeaders=Subject&metadataHeaders=To', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const mData = await mRes.json() const headers = mData.payload?.headers || [] const subj = headers.find((h: any) => h.name === 'Subject')?.value || '' const toH = headers.find((h: any) => h.name === 'To')?.value || '' const snip = mData.snippet || '' const score = scoreMatch(task.text, candidates, subj, toH, snip) if (score > bestScore) { bestScore = score bestMsgId = msg.id bestSubject = subj bestTo = toH bestSnippet = snip } } debugEntry.bestScore = bestScore debugEntry.bestSubject = bestSubject // Only show email evidence if subject OR To field contains a candidate name (score >= 8) if (bestScore >= 8) { emailEvidence = true emailSubject = bestSubject emailTo = bestTo // ── Fetch inbox reply and classify it with full framework ────── const firstCandidate = (strongTerms[0] || candidates[0]).toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '') const inboxQ = encodeURIComponent('in:inbox from:' + firstCandidate + ' after:' + after + ' before:' + before) const inboxRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + inboxQ + '&maxResults=3', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const inboxData = await inboxRes.json() if ((inboxData?.messages?.length || 0) > 0) { let replySnippet = ''; let replySubject = ''; let replyFrom = '' try { const rMeta = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages/' + inboxData.messages[0].id + '?format=metadata&metadataHeaders=Subject&metadataHeaders=From', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const rData = await rMeta.json() replySnippet = rData.snippet || '' replySubject = rData.payload?.headers?.find((h: any) => h.name === 'Subject')?.value || '' replyFrom = rData.payload?.headers?.find((h: any) => h.name === 'From')?.value || '' } catch(e) { /* non-fatal */ } // Use the framework classifier — bounce MUST be checked before OOO const classification = classifyInboxEmail(replySnippet, replySubject, replyFrom) replyEvidence = classification.type === 'positive' ;(task as any)._replyAnalysis = { type: classification.type, snippet: replySnippet.slice(0, 150) } } } } ivrDebug.push(debugEntry) } catch(e) { ivrDebug.push({ task: task.text, account, query: decodeURIComponent(q), exception: String(e) }) } } // ── Signal classification — driven by parseTaskIntent framework ────── // intentType already determined above; use it to route verification. let source: 'calendar' | 'notetaker' | 'email_sent' | 'email_reply' | 'none' = 'none' let signal = 'unknown' // Quantity-aware verification for bulk email tasks const quantityClaimed = intent.quantityClaimed || 1 const verificationRatio = quantityClaimed > 1 && emailsFoundCount > 0 ? emailsFoundCount / quantityClaimed : emailsFoundCount > 0 ? 1.0 : 0.0 // Partial count: found something but significantly less than claimed const isPartialCount = quantityClaimed > 1 && emailsFoundCount > 0 && verificationRatio < 0.6 const isScheduledMeeting = intent.intentType === 'meeting' || intent.isVerifiableViaCalendar if (isScheduledMeeting) { let meetingEvidence = false let meetingSource = '' if (candidates.length > 0) { try { const taskDate = new Date(task.date) const dayStart = new Date(taskDate); dayStart.setDate(dayStart.getDate() - 1) const dayEnd = new Date(taskDate); dayEnd.setDate(dayEnd.getDate() + 3) const calSearchTerms = candidates.join(' ') const calRes = await fetch( 'https://www.googleapis.com/calendar/v3/calendars/primary/events' + '?timeMin=' + dayStart.toISOString() + '&timeMax=' + dayEnd.toISOString() + '&q=' + encodeURIComponent(calSearchTerms) + '&maxResults=10&singleEvents=true&orderBy=startTime', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const calData = await calRes.json() if (calData?.items?.length > 0) { // ── IMPROVED: pick event with highest name overlap, not just first ── let bestEvent = null let bestCalScore = 0 for (const event of calData.items) { const eventTitle = (event.summary || '').toLowerCase() const eventDesc = (event.description || '').toLowerCase() const attendees = (event.attendees || []).map((a: any) => (a.email + ' ' + (a.displayName || '')).toLowerCase()).join(' ') const fullText = eventTitle + ' ' + eventDesc + ' ' + attendees let calScore = 0 for (const c of candidates) { const cLower = c.toLowerCase() if (eventTitle.includes(cLower)) calScore += 10 // title match = strong if (attendees.includes(cLower)) calScore += 4 // attendee match = weaker if (eventDesc.includes(cLower)) calScore += 2 } if (calScore > bestCalScore) { bestCalScore = calScore bestEvent = event } } // Only use calendar event if title actually contains at least one candidate name if (bestEvent && bestCalScore >= 10) { meetingEvidence = true meetingSource = bestEvent.summary || 'Calendar event' source = 'calendar' } // If attendee-only match (score < 10), don't claim verification — too unreliable } } catch(e) { /* skip */ } } // Check notetaker emails if (!meetingEvidence && candidates.length > 0) { try { const taskDate = new Date(task.date) const dayBefore = new Date(taskDate); dayBefore.setDate(dayBefore.getDate() - 1) const dayAfter = new Date(taskDate); dayAfter.setDate(dayAfter.getDate() + 2) const after = dayBefore.toISOString().split('T')[0].replace(/-/g, '/') const before = dayAfter.toISOString().split('T')[0].replace(/-/g, '/') const searchName = candidates[0] const notetakerSendersIVR = [ 'fireflies.ai','fathom.video','otter.ai','tldv.io','notes.microsoft.com', 'gong.io','chorus.ai','grain.com','grain.co','granola.ai','rev.com', 'avoma.com','wudpecker.io','sembly.ai','supernormal.com','krisp.ai','read.ai','noty.ai' ].map(s => 'from:' + s).join(' OR ') const notetakerSubjectsIVR = [ 'meeting notes','meeting recap','meeting summary','call summary', 'call notes','transcript','recording summary','meeting minutes' ].map(s => 'subject:"' + s + '"').join(' OR ') const notetakerQuery = encodeURIComponent( '(' + notetakerSendersIVR + ' OR ' + notetakerSubjectsIVR + ') "' + searchName + '" after:' + after + ' before:' + before ) const ntRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + notetakerQuery + '&maxResults=3', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const ntData = await ntRes.json() if (ntData?.messages?.length > 0) { const mRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages/' + ntData.messages[0].id + '?format=full', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const mData = await mRes.json() const headers = mData.payload?.headers || [] const subject = headers.find((h: any) => h.name === 'Subject')?.value || '' const from = headers.find((h: any) => h.name === 'From')?.value || '' // Use rich HTML-aware extractor instead of text-only extractText const emailBody = extractEmailBody(mData.payload).slice(0, 8000) || mData.snippet || '' const ntProvider = detectNotetakerProvider(from, subject) let meetingIntel: any = { participants: [], summary: '', actionItems: [], sentiment: 'neutral' } if (GEMINI_KEY && emailBody) { try { const prompt = buildNotetakerGeminiPrompt(emailBody, ntProvider, candidates[0]) const gRes = await callGeminiWithRetry(GEMINI_URL, { contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }], generationConfig: { temperature: 0.1, maxOutputTokens: 800 } }) if (!isGeminiQuotaError(gRes)) { const text = gRes?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text ?? '' const match = text.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/) if (match) meetingIntel = JSON.parse(match[0]) } } catch(e) { /* skip */ } } // Validate: notetaker email must actually mention one of our candidates const notetakerText = (subject + ' ' + emailBody).toLowerCase(); const notetakerMatches = candidates.filter((c: string) => notetakerText.includes(c.toLowerCase())); if (notetakerMatches.length > 0) { meetingEvidence = true; meetingSource = subject; source = 'notetaker' emailTo = JSON.stringify({ source: from.split('<')[0].trim(), subject, participants: meetingIntel.participants || [], summary: meetingIntel.summary || '', actionItems: meetingIntel.actionItems || [], sentiment: meetingIntel.sentiment || 'neutral', nextSteps: meetingIntel.nextSteps || '' }) } } } catch(e) { /* skip */ } } // Meeting evidence (calendar/notetaker) sets its own source above. // A scheduled meeting marked done with no calendar/notetaker // evidence falls back to checking email evidence (e.g. the meeting // was confirmed entirely over email with no calendar invite) before // landing on "unverified". if (meetingEvidence) { signal = 'verified' emailSubject = meetingSource } else if (task.done && emailEvidence && replyEvidence) { signal = 'verified_hot'; source = 'email_reply' } else if (task.done && emailEvidence) { signal = 'verified'; source = 'email_sent' } else if (task.done) { signal = 'unverified' } else { signal = 'gap' } } else { // Email outreach and unknown tasks if (!task.done && !emailEvidence) { signal = 'gap' } else if (task.done && emailEvidence && replyEvidence) { signal = 'verified_hot'; source = 'email_reply' } else if (task.done && emailEvidence && isPartialCount) { // Found emails but significantly fewer than claimed count signal = 'partial_count'; source = 'email_sent' } else if (task.done && emailEvidence) { signal = 'verified'; source = 'email_sent' } else if (task.done && !emailEvidence) { signal = 'unverified' } else if (!task.done && emailEvidence) { signal = 'done_not_logged'; source = 'email_sent' } } const activityType: 'meeting' | 'call' | 'email' | 'other' = intent.intentType === 'meeting' ? 'meeting' : intent.intentType === 'call' ? 'call' : intent.intentType === 'email_outreach' ? 'email' : 'other' results.push({ date: task.date, text: task.text, done: task.done, priority: task.priority, account, signal, emailEvidence, replyEvidence, emailSubject, emailTo, source, activityType, replyAnalysis: (task as any)._replyAnalysis || null, intent: intent.intentType, quantityClaimed, emailsFound: emailsFoundCount, verificationRatio: Math.round(verificationRatio * 100) }) } const total = results.length // task_done = rep marked done but NO external verification (LinkedIn, WhatsApp, calls without SR corroboration) // These are self-reported only — do NOT count as verified in the summary const verified = results.filter(r => ['verified','verified_hot','partial_count','attested'].includes(r.signal)).length const taskDone = results.filter(r => r.signal === 'task_done').length // self-reported, unverified externally const gaps = results.filter(r => r.signal === 'gap').length const unverified = results.filter(r => r.signal === 'unverified').length const doneNotLogged = results.filter(r => r.signal === 'done_not_logged').length const noSource = results.filter(r => r.signal === 'no_source').length return jsonResponse({ connected: true, gmailEmail: tokenRows[0].email, dateRange: { from: fromDate, to: toDate }, results, debug: ivrDebug, summary: { total, verified, taskDone, gaps, unverified, doneNotLogged, noSource, verificationRate: total ? Math.round((verified / total) * 100) : 0 } }) } // ── weekly_digest ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── if (action === 'weekly_digest') { const RESEND_KEY = Deno.env.get('RESEND_API_KEY') ?? '' if (!RESEND_KEY) return jsonResponse({ error: 'RESEND_API_KEY not set' }, 500) const SB_SERVICE = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey const callerRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=role,org_id,email', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const callerData = asArray(await callerRes.json()) const caller = callerData?.[0] if (!caller || !canSeeTeam(caller.role)) { return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 403) } const orgId = caller.org_id const toDate = payload.date_to || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] const fromDate = payload.date_from || new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 86400000).toISOString().split('T')[0] const weekLabel = fromDate + ' → ' + toDate const sendToManager = payload.send_to_manager !== false const sendToReps = payload.send_to_reps !== false const membersRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=user_id,email,role', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const members = asArray(await membersRes.json()) const reps = members.filter((m: any) => m.role === 'member' || m.role === 'manager') const repDigests: any[] = [] for (const rep of reps) { const dtRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/daytrack?user_id=eq.' + rep.user_id + '&day_key=gte.' + fromDate + '&day_key=lte.' + toDate + '&select=day_key,data', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const dtData = asArray(await dtRes.json()) let totalTasks = 0, doneTasks = 0, wins = 0, misses = 0, issues = 0 const outreachTasks: any[] = [] const outreachKw = ['email','mail','send','follow','reach','proposal','message','outreach','call','meeting','demo','connect'] for (const row of dtData) { const tasks = row.data?.tasks || [] const dayWins = row.data?.wins || [] const dayMisses = row.data?.misses || [] const dayIssues = row.data?.issues || [] totalTasks += tasks.length doneTasks += tasks.filter((t: any) => t.done).length wins += dayWins.length misses += dayMisses.length issues += dayIssues.length tasks.forEach((t: any) => { if (outreachKw.some((k: string) => (t.text||'').toLowerCase().includes(k))) { outreachTasks.push({ date: row.day_key, text: t.text, done: t.done }) } }) } const completionRate = totalTasks ? Math.round((doneTasks / totalTasks) * 100) : 0 const tokenRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + rep.user_id + '&select=email', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const tokenData = asArray(await tokenRes.json()) const gmailConnected = tokenData?.length > 0 repDigests.push({ email: rep.email, userId: rep.user_id, totalTasks, doneTasks, completionRate, wins, misses, issues, outreachTasks, gmailConnected }) } const managerHtml = buildManagerEmail(repDigests, weekLabel, caller.email) const managerText = 'Weekly SAM Digest: ' + weekLabel let sent = 0 if (sendToManager) { await sendEmail(RESEND_KEY, { to: caller.email, subject: '⚡ SAM Digest — ' + weekLabel, html: managerHtml, text: managerText }) sent++ } if (sendToReps) { for (const rep of repDigests) { const repHtml = buildRepEmail(rep, weekLabel) await sendEmail(RESEND_KEY, { to: rep.email, subject: '⚡ Your SAM Summary — ' + weekLabel, html: repHtml, text: 'Your weekly activity summary from SamoraTrack' }) sent++ } } const extraEmails: string[] = payload.extra_emails || [] for (const email of extraEmails) { if (!email.includes('@')) continue await sendEmail(RESEND_KEY, { to: email, subject: '⚡ SAM Digest — ' + weekLabel, html: managerHtml, text: 'SAM Weekly Digest' }) sent++ } return jsonResponse({ success: true, sent, weekLabel }) } // ── extract_intelligence ─────────────────────────────────────────────── // Fetches notetaker emails for all named accounts assigned to the user, // extracts product/pricing/competitor signals via Gemini, stores to DB if (action === 'extract_intelligence') { const { rep_user_id, days_back } = payload const targetUserId = rep_user_id || userId const lookbackDays = days_back || orgCfg.intel_lookback_days // Verify permission if manager is pulling rep data if (rep_user_id && rep_user_id !== userId) { const callerRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=role', { headers: { 'apikey': anonKey, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + anonKey } } ) const callerData = asArray(await callerRes.json()) const callerRole = callerData?.[0]?.role if (!canSeeTeam(callerRole)) { return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 403) } } const SB_SERVICE = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey // Get Gmail token for target user const tokenRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&select=*', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const
