if expired — explicit failure check, since the probe // immediately below would otherwise just see a 401 with no context. const tokenResultExtract = await getValidGmailToken(tokenRows[0], targetUserId, SUPABASE_URL, SB_SERVICE, GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET) if (tokenResultExtract.refreshFailed) return gmailReconnectNeededResponse(!!rep_user_id, tokenRows[0].email) accessToken = tokenResultExtract.accessToken // Get user profile for org_id const profileRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&select=org_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const profileData = asArray(await profileRes.json()) const orgId = profileData?.[0]?.org_id if (!orgId) return jsonResponse({ error: 'No org found for user' }, 400) // Get named accounts assigned to this user const accountsRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=id,account_name,domain,region,parent_account_id,additional_domains', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const accounts = asArray(await accountsRes.json()) if (!accounts?.length) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, processed: 0, message: 'No named accounts assigned to this user' }) // Same parent-filtering logic as local_intelligence — skip anchor-only // parent rows that have no domain/region and exist only for rollup views. const _parentIds = new Set(accounts.filter((a: any) => a.parent_account_id).map((a: any) => a.parent_account_id)) const scannableAccounts = accounts.filter((a: any) => !(_parentIds.has(a.id) && !a.parent_account_id && !a.domain && !a.region)) const afterDate = new Date(Date.now() - lookbackDays * 86400000).toISOString().split('T')[0].replace(/-/g, '/') const results: any[] = [] let processed = 0 let skipped = 0 let geminiQuotaExhausted = false const debugLog: any[] = [] // Probe Gmail access once before looping every account — if the stored // token lacks gmail.readonly scope, every subsequent call will 403 the // same way. Fail fast with one clear message instead of N identical errors. const probeRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?maxResults=1', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const probeData = await probeRes.json() if (isScopeError(probeData)) { return jsonResponse({ ok: false, error: 'Gmail connection for this user is missing required permissions (read access to email). They need to disconnect and reconnect Gmail in the SAM tab to re-grant access.', scopeError: true, targetUserId }, 403) } for (const account of scannableAccounts) { if (geminiQuotaExhausted) break // no point searching further accounts — every email would just fail the same way const accountName = account.account_name const region = account.region || null const domain = account.domain || accountName.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '') // Broad sender list covering common notetaker/transcription tools, plus // generic subject-keyword matches so we're not locked to a fixed vendor list. const notetakerSenders = [ 'fireflies.ai','fathom.video','otter.ai','tldv.io','notes.microsoft.com', 'gong.io','chorus.ai','grain.com','grain.co','granola.ai','rev.com', 'zoom.us','avoma.com','wudpecker.io','sembly.ai','supernormal.com', 'krisp.ai','read.ai','noty.ai','superhuman.com','clari.com' ].map(s => 'from:' + s).join(' OR ') const notetakerSubjects = [ 'meeting notes','meeting recap','meeting summary','call summary', 'call notes','transcript','recording summary','meeting minutes', 'notes from','summary of your call','your meeting recap' ].map(s => 'subject:"' + s + '"').join(' OR ') // Excludes common internal-only meeting patterns (1:1s, standups, // appraisals, performance reviews, HR/compensation discussions) so // they're never even fetched as candidates — these are NOT client // account intelligence and must not be summarised into a view a // manager or other reps might read while researching an account. const internalExclusions = '-subject:"1:1" -subject:"one on one" -subject:"weekly kickoff" -subject:"standup" -subject:"stand-up" -subject:appraisal -subject:"performance review" -subject:"performance appraisal" -subject:compensation -subject:salary -subject:payroll -subject:"pip" -subject:"internal sync" -subject:"team sync"' const strictQuery = encodeURIComponent( '(' + notetakerSenders + ' OR ' + notetakerSubjects + ') ("' + accountName + '" OR "' + domain + '") ' + internalExclusions + ' after:' + afterDate ) const ntRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + strictQuery + '&maxResults=10', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const ntData = await ntRes.json() let messages = ntData?.messages || [] let usedFallback = false // Fallback: if the strict sender/subject search finds nothing, try a looser // search — any email (regardless of sender) whose subject or body looks like // a meeting summary AND mentions the account name. Catches tools not in our // sender list and notetakers that don't use a recognisable subject line. if (!messages.length) { const looseQuery = encodeURIComponent( '("' + accountName + '" OR "' + domain + '") (transcript OR "meeting" OR "recap" OR "summary" OR "notes") ' + internalExclusions + ' after:' + afterDate ) const ntRes2 = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + looseQuery + '&maxResults=10', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const ntData2 = await ntRes2.json() messages = ntData2?.messages || [] usedFallback = true debugLog.push({ account: accountName, strictSearchFound: 0, fallbackSearchFound: messages.length, gmailApiError: ntData2?.error || ntData?.error || null }) } else { debugLog.push({ account: accountName, notetakerEmailsFound: messages.length, usedFallback, gmailApiError: ntData?.error || null }) } if (!messages.length) { skipped++; continue; } for (const msg of messages) { if (geminiQuotaExhausted) { skipped++; continue } // stop calling Gemini, but still count remaining messages as skipped for accurate reporting // Check if already extracted — guard against Postgrest error objects const existingRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_intelligence?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&account_name=eq.' + encodeURIComponent(accountName) + '&select=id,meeting_subject', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const existingJson = await existingRes.json() const existing: any[] = asArray(existingJson) if (!existingRes.ok && !Array.isArray(existingJson)) { debugLog.push({ account: accountName, dbReadError: existingJson }) } // Fetch full email const mRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages/' + msg.id + '?format=full', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const m = await mRes.json() const hdrs = m.payload?.headers || [] const getH = (n: string) => hdrs.find((h: any) => h.name === n)?.value || '' const subject = getH('Subject') const from = getH('From') const date = getH('Date') // Skip if this exact meeting already extracted if (existing.find((e: any) => e.meeting_subject === subject)) { skipped++; continue; } // Extract email body const extractText = (part: any): string => { if (!part) return '' if (part.mimeType === 'text/plain' && part.body?.data) { const b64 = part.body.data.replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/') try { return atob(b64) } catch { return '' } } if (part.parts) return part.parts.map(extractText).join('\n') return '' } const emailBody = extractText(m.payload).slice(0, 4000) || m.snippet || '' if (!emailBody) { skipped++; continue; } // Use Gemini to extract structured intelligence let intelligence: any = { product_feedback: [], pricing_signals: [], competitor_mentions: [], expansion_signals: [], risk_signals: [], summary: '', sentiment: 'neutral', action_items: [] } if (GEMINI_KEY) { try { const prompt = `You are a B2B product intelligence analyst. Extract structured signals from this meeting notes email for the account "${accountName}". IMPORTANT — internal content check FIRST: before extracting anything, determine whether this email is actually about a conversation WITH the client account "${accountName}", versus an INTERNAL team meeting (standup, 1:1, weekly kickoff, performance review, appraisal, compensation discussion, internal planning) that merely mentions "${accountName}" in passing as one of several topics or accounts discussed internally. If this is internal content NOT a client-facing conversation, return ONLY this JSON and nothing else: {"is_internal": true, "summary": "", "sentiment": "neutral", "product_feedback": [], "pricing_signals": [], "competitor_mentions": [], "expansion_signals": [], "risk_signals": [], "action_items": []} If this IS a genuine client-facing meeting/conversation with ${accountName}, return ONLY valid JSON with this exact structure: { "is_internal": false, "summary": "2-3 sentence summary of the meeting and deal status", "sentiment": "positive|neutral|negative", "product_feedback": [{"quote": "exact or paraphrased quote", "category": "feature_gap|integration|usability|performance|missing_feature", "severity": "high|medium|low"}], "pricing_signals": [{"quote": "exact or paraphrased", "type": "too_expensive|budget_constraint|competitor_cheaper|asking_discount|pilot_request|positive", "amount_mentioned": "if any specific amount or % was mentioned or null"}], "competitor_mentions": [{"name": "competitor name", "context": "what was said about them"}], "expansion_signals": [{"quote": "quote", "type": "more_seats|new_team|new_use_case|upsell"}], "risk_signals": [{"quote": "quote", "type": "budget_freeze|champion_left|competitor_evaluation|timeline_delay|procurement_block"}], "action_items": ["specific next actions mentioned"], "deal_signals": { "value_hint": {"amount": null, "currency": null, "amount_usd_approx": null, "context": "quote where amount was mentioned or null"}, "units_hint": {"count": null, "unit": "outlets|licenses|seats|skus|stores|users|null", "context": "quote or null"}, "timeline_hint": {"close_date_text": "e.g. Q3 2026 or end of year or null", "urgency": "high|medium|low|null", "context": "quote or null"}, "contract_hint": {"duration_months": null, "context": "quote or null"}, "budget_confirmed": false, "deal_type_hint": "new_business|expansion|renewal|upsell|null" } } Never include any compensation, salary, appraisal, performance review, or other HR/personnel information in any field, even if present in the source text — this data must never appear in client account intelligence. Only extract what is explicitly mentioned. If nothing found for a category, return empty array. Meeting email for ${accountName}: Subject: ${subject} ${emailBody}` const gData = await callGeminiWithRetry(GEMINI_URL, { contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }], generationConfig: { temperature: 0.1, maxOutputTokens: 1500 } }) if (gData?.error) { const quotaHit = isGeminiQuotaError(gData) debugLog.push({ account: accountName, subject, geminiApiError: gData.error, geminiModelUsed: GEMINI_MODEL, hint: gData.error?.code === 404 ? 'Model retired/unavailable — set GEMINI_MODEL env var to a current model name (check https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/models)' : quotaHit ? 'Gemini free-tier daily quota exhausted (commonly 20 requests/day per model). Remaining emails this run were skipped rather than failing one-by-one. Upgrade to a paid Gemini API plan, or wait until the quota resets, then run \u21bb Refresh again to pick up where this left off.' : undefined }) if (quotaHit) { geminiQuotaExhausted = true } } let text = gData?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text ?? '' // Strip markdown code fences (```json ... ``` or ``` ... ```) if present text = text.replace(/```json\s*/gi, '').replace(/```\s*/g, '').trim() const match = text.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/) const finishReason = gData?.candidates?.[0]?.finishReason if (match) { try { const parsed = JSON.parse(match[0]) if (parsed.is_internal === true) { debugLog.push({ account: accountName, subject, skippedReason: 'internal_content_detected' }) } else { intelligence = { product_feedback: parsed.product_feedback || [], pricing_signals: parsed.pricing_signals || [], competitor_mentions: parsed.competitor_mentions || [], expansion_signals: parsed.expansion_signals || [], risk_signals: parsed.risk_signals || [], summary: parsed.summary || '', sentiment: parsed.sentiment || 'neutral', action_items: parsed.action_items || [] } } } catch(parseErr) { debugLog.push({ account: accountName, subject, geminiJsonParseError: String(parseErr), geminiFinishReason: finishReason, geminiRawText: text.slice(0, 500) }) } } else { debugLog.push({ account: accountName, subject, geminiNoMatch: true, geminiFinishReason: finishReason, geminiRawText: text.slice(0, 500) }) } } catch(e) { debugLog.push({ account: accountName, subject, geminiError: String(e) }) } } else { debugLog.push({ account: accountName, subject, geminiKeyMissing: true }) } // Hard safety-net: scan the assembled text for HR/compensation // keywords regardless of what Gemini decided. This is deliberately // blunt — false positives (skipping a legitimate client meeting // that happens to mention "salary" in some unrelated context) are // far preferable to leaking internal HR/comp data into a view // managers and reps read while researching client accounts. const hrKeywords = /\b(appraisal|performance review|performance appraisal|compensation|salary|payroll|pip\b|promotion review|pay rise|pay raise|increment letter|disciplinary)\b/i const allExtractedText = [ intelligence.summary, ...intelligence.product_feedback.map((s: any) => s.quote || ''), ...intelligence.pricing_signals.map((s: any) => s.quote || ''), ...intelligence.risk_signals.map((s: any) => s.quote || ''), ...intelligence.expansion_signals.map((s: any) => s.quote || ''), ...intelligence.action_items ].join(' ') if (hrKeywords.test(subject) || hrKeywords.test(allExtractedText)) { debugLog.push({ account: accountName, subject, skippedReason: 'hr_keyword_safety_net' }) skipped++ continue } // Skip if no signals found at all const hasSignals = intelligence.product_feedback.length > 0 || intelligence.pricing_signals.length > 0 || intelligence.competitor_mentions.length > 0 || intelligence.expansion_signals.length > 0 || intelligence.risk_signals.length > 0 if (!hasSignals && !intelligence.summary) { skipped++; continue; } // Parse meeting date let meetingDate = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] try { if (date) meetingDate = new Date(date).toISOString().split('T')[0] } catch {} // Store in account_intelligence table const insertRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_intelligence', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: orgId, user_id: targetUserId, account_name: accountName, meeting_date: meetingDate, meeting_subject: subject, notetaker_source: from.split('<')[0].trim() || from, source: 'ai', product_feedback: intelligence.product_feedback, pricing_signals: intelligence.pricing_signals, competitor_mentions: intelligence.competitor_mentions, expansion_signals: intelligence.expansion_signals, risk_signals: intelligence.risk_signals, summary: intelligence.summary, sentiment: intelligence.sentiment, action_items: intelligence.action_items, raw_email_snippet: emailBody.slice(0, 500) }) } ) if (insertRes.ok || insertRes.status === 201) { processed++ results.push({ account: accountName, subject, date: meetingDate, sentiment: intelligence.sentiment, signals: { product: intelligence.product_feedback.length, pricing: intelligence.pricing_signals.length, competitors: intelligence.competitor_mentions.length, expansion: intelligence.expansion_signals.length, risk: intelligence.risk_signals.length } }) // Persist deal signals to account_signals table if Gemini // extracted any — these feed the buying signal score and // pipeline view without any rep input. const ds = intelligence.deal_signals if (ds) { const accountRow = account const signalsToInsert: any[] = [] if (ds.value_hint?.amount) signalsToInsert.push({ org_id: orgId, account_id: accountRow.id, signal_type: 'value_hint', source: 'gemini', raw_text: ds.value_hint.context || subject, extracted: ds.value_hint, score_weight: 15, confidence: 80, expires_at: new Date(Date.now() + 30*86400000).toISOString() }) if (ds.units_hint?.count) signalsToInsert.push({ org_id: orgId, account_id: accountRow.id, signal_type: 'units_hint', source: 'gemini', raw_text: ds.units_hint.context || subject, extracted: ds.units_hint, score_weight: 10, confidence: 80, expires_at: new Date(Date.now() + 30*86400000).toISOString() }) if (ds.timeline_hint?.close_date_text) signalsToInsert.push({ org_id: orgId, account_id: accountRow.id, signal_type: 'timeline_hint', source: 'gemini', raw_text: ds.timeline_hint.context || subject, extracted: ds.timeline_hint, score_weight: ds.timeline_hint.urgency === 'high' ? 15 : 8, confidence: 75, expires_at: new Date(Date.now() + 14*86400000).toISOString() }) if (ds.budget_confirmed) signalsToInsert.push({ org_id: orgId, account_id: accountRow.id, signal_type: 'budget_confirmed', source: 'gemini', raw_text: subject, extracted: { confirmed: true }, score_weight: 18, confidence: 90, expires_at: new Date(Date.now() + 30*86400000).toISOString() }) for (const sig of signalsToInsert) { try { await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signals', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify(sig) }) } catch(e) { /* non-fatal */ } } } } else { const insertErr = await insertRes.text() debugLog.push({ account: accountName, subject, dbInsertError: insertErr, status: insertRes.status }) } } } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, processed, skipped, results, debug: debugLog, geminiQuotaExhausted, message: geminiQuotaExhausted ? 'Stopped early — Gemini\u2019s free-tier daily quota was exhausted partway through this run. ' + processed + ' meeting' + (processed===1?'':'s') + ' processed before hitting the limit; the rest were skipped, not failed. Run \u21bb Refresh again later (quota resets daily) or upgrade your Gemini API plan to process everything in one pass.' : undefined }) } // ── local_intelligence ─────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Rule-based deterministic signals — NO Gemini calls, so this never hits // the API quota and always returns instantly. Detects classic patterns // directly from Gmail + stored account_intelligence data: // - proposal sent and acknowledged (reply received) -> active negotiation // - NDA being exchanged -> deal progression // - no reply in X days since last sent -> going cold // - customer's email sitting unanswered for X days -> response gap // - action items from a past meeting that don't appear to be actioned yet if (action === 'local_intelligence') { const { rep_user_id, stale_days, unanswered_days } = payload const targetUserId = rep_user_id || userId const staleDays = stale_days || orgCfg.stale_days const unansweredDays = unanswered_days || orgCfg.unanswered_days const SVC = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey if (rep_user_id && rep_user_id !== userId) { const callerRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=role', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const callerData = asArray(await callerRes.json()) if (!canSeeTeam(callerData?.[0]?.role)) { return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 403) } } // Use the user's own JWT (authHeader) to fetch their gmail token. // This is the most reliable approach — auth.uid() is set correctly, // RLS policy "Users manage own gmail token" (auth.uid() = user_id) allows it, // and it doesn't depend on the service role key being set correctly. let tokenRows: any[] = [] if (targetUserId === userId) { // Self-scan: use user's own JWT — guaranteed by RLS const tokenRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&select=*', { headers: { 'apikey': anonKey, 'Authorization': authHeader } } ) tokenRows = asArray(await tokenRes.json()) } else { // Manager scanning a rep: must use service role to read another user's token const tokenRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/gmail_tokens?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&select=*', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) tokenRows = asArray(await tokenRes.json()) } if (!tokenRows?.length) return jsonResponse({ connected: false, error: 'Gmail not connected for this user' }) let accessToken = tokenRows[0].access_token const tokenResultLocal = await getValidGmailToken(tokenRows[0], targetUserId, SUPABASE_URL, SVC, GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET) if (tokenResultLocal.refreshFailed) return gmailReconnectNeededResponse(!!rep_user_id, tokenRows[0].email) accessToken = tokenResultLocal.accessToken const profileRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&select=org_id', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const profileData = asArray(await profileRes.json()) const orgId = profileData?.[0]?.org_id if (!orgId) return jsonResponse({ error: 'No org found for user' }, 400) const accountsRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&select=id,account_name,domain,region,parent_account_id,additional_domains', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const accounts = asArray(await accountsRes.json()) if (!accounts?.length) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, accounts: [], message: 'No named accounts assigned to this user' }) // Filter out pure parent/anchor rows — those exist only for manager // rollup views and have no rep assignment, no domain, and no emails // to scan. A parent row is one that HAS children (other rows point to // it as parent_account_id) but has no parent itself. In practice: // if a row has no domain AND no region it's almost certainly a global // anchor, not a real scannable entity. We keep all rows that either // have a domain, have a region, OR have no children (standalone account). const allIds = new Set(accounts.map((a: any) => a.id)) const parentIds = new Set(accounts.filter((a: any) => a.parent_account_id).map((a: any) => a.parent_account_id)) const scannable = accounts.filter((a: any) => { const isParentOnly = parentIds.has(a.id) && !a.parent_account_id && !a.domain && !a.region return !isParentOnly }) const now = Date.now() const lookbackDate = new Date(now - orgCfg.lookback_days * 86400000).toISOString().split('T')[0].replace(/-/g, '/') const lookbackISO = new Date(now - orgCfg.lookback_days * 86400000).toISOString() const nowISO = new Date(now).toISOString() // Keyword patterns for proposal/NDA/demo detection — kept narrow and // specific on purpose, to minimise false positives from unrelated // emails that happen to share a word. const proposalPattern = /\b(proposal|commercial proposal|quotation|quote|pricing proposal|sow|statement of work|commercials)\b/i const ndaPattern = /\b(nda|non[\s-]?disclosure agreement|confidentiality agreement)\b/i const demoPattern = /\b(demo|product walkthrough|product demonstration)\b/i const requirementsPattern = /\b(requirement|requirements|use case|discovery call|scoping)\b/i // Every account this rep is assigned gets a row in the response, even // with zero channel activity — previously accounts with no email // evidence in the lookback window were silently dropped entirely, // which is why a manager reviewing a rep's coverage would only ever // see 1-2 of their accounts instead of the full assigned list. const accountReports: any[] = [] // Build stage label map and inference function before the account loop // so they're available inside it. Must be declared here (not inside the // loop) to avoid the temporal dead zone error from const hoisting. const stageKeyOrder = orgCfg.deal_stages.map((s: any) => s.key) const stageLabel: Record = { unknown: 'Unknown' } orgCfg.deal_stages.forEach((s: any) => { stageLabel[s.key] = s.label }) const stageForSignal = (signal: 'commercial'|'value_prop'|'prospective'): string => { const standardMap: Record = {commercial:'commercial',value_prop:'value_prop',prospective:'prospective'} if (stageKeyOrder.includes(standardMap[signal])) return standardMap[signal] if (!stageKeyOrder.length) return signal if (signal === 'commercial') return stageKeyOrder[stageKeyOrder.length - 1] if (signal === 'prospective') return stageKeyOrder[0] return stageKeyOrder[Math.floor(stageKeyOrder.length / 2)] || stageKeyOrder[0] } for (const account of scannable.slice(0, 20)) { const accountName = account.account_name const region = account.region || null const parentAccountId = account.parent_account_id || null const domain = account.domain || accountName.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '') // ── Channel 1: Email (sent + inbox replies) ── const sentQ = encodeURIComponent('in:sent ("' + accountName + '"' + (account.domain ? ' OR to:' + account.domain : ' OR to:' + domain) + ') after:' + lookbackDate) const sentRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + sentQ + '&maxResults=20', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const sentData = await sentRes.json() const sentRefs = sentData?.messages || [] const inboxQ = encodeURIComponent('in:inbox from:' + domain + ' after:' + lookbackDate) const inboxRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + inboxQ + '&maxResults=20', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const inboxData = await inboxRes.json() const inboxRefs = inboxData?.messages || [] const fetchMeta = async (refs: any[]) => { const out: any[] = [] for (const ref of refs.slice(0, 15)) { const mRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages/' + ref.id + '?format=metadata&metadataHeaders=Subject&metadataHeaders=Date&metadataHeaders=From', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const m = await mRes.json() const hdrs = m.payload?.headers || [] out.push({ id: m.id, threadId: m.threadId, subject: hdrs.find((h: any) => h.name === 'Subject')?.value || '', date: hdrs.find((h: any) => h.name === 'Date')?.value || '', from: hdrs.find((h: any) => h.name === 'From')?.value || '', internalDate: m.internalDate ? parseInt(m.internalDate) : 0, snippet: m.snippet || '' }) } return out.sort((a, b) => b.internalDate - a.internalDate) } const sentMeta = await fetchMeta(sentRefs) const inboxMeta = await fetchMeta(inboxRefs) const lastSent = sentMeta[0] const lastInbox = inboxMeta[0] // ── Channel 2: Calendar meetings mentioning this account ── let calendarEvents: any[] = [] try { const calRes = await fetch( 'https://www.googleapis.com/calendar/v3/calendars/primary/events' + '?timeMin=' + lookbackISO + '&timeMax=' + nowISO + '&q=' + encodeURIComponent(accountName) + '&maxResults=10&singleEvents=true&orderBy=startTime', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const calData = await calRes.json() calendarEvents = (calData?.items || []).filter((e: any) => { const title = (e.summary || '').toLowerCase() return title.includes(accountName.toLowerCase()) || (account.domain && (e.attendees || []).some((a: any) => (a.email || '').includes(account.domain))) }) } catch(e) { /* calendar check is best-effort, never fails the whole scan */ } // ── Channel 3: Notetaker emails mentioning this account ── let notetakerMessages: any[] = [] try { const ntQ = encodeURIComponent(notetakerGmailQueryFragment() + ' "' + accountName + '" after:' + lookbackDate) const ntRes = await fetch( 'https://gmail.googleapis.com/gmail/v1/users/me/messages?q=' + ntQ + '&maxResults=5', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken } } ) const ntData = await ntRes.json() notetakerMessages = ntData?.messages || [] } catch(e) { /* best-effort */ } // ── Pattern detection across all fetched email content ── const allEmailText = [...sentMeta, ...inboxMeta].map(m => m.subject + ' ' + m.snippet).join(' \n ') const hasProposal = proposalPattern.test(allEmailText) const hasNDA = ndaPattern.test(allEmailText) const hasDemo = demoPattern.test(allEmailText) || calendarEvents.length > 0 const hasRequirementsDiscussion = requirementsPattern.test(allEmailText) const hasReply = inboxMeta.length > 0 const channels: any = { email: { sent: sentMeta.length, replies: inboxMeta.length, lastActivity: lastSent?.date || lastInbox?.date || null }, calendar: { meetings: calendarEvents.length, lastMeeting: calendarEvents[0]?.start?.dateTime || calendarEvents[0]?.start?.date || null }, notetaker: { count: notetakerMessages.length }, // Placeholders for future channels — wiring these in later is a // matter of populating these fields from a real integration, the // stage-inference and UI below already treat them as first-class. call: { count: 0, integrated: false }, whatsapp: { count: 0, integrated: false }, linkedin: { count: 0, integrated: false } } const hasAnyActivity = sentMeta.length > 0 || inboxMeta.length > 0 || calendarEvents.length > 0 || notetakerMessages.length > 0 // ── Deal stage inference ── // Commercial: NDA or proposal/pricing has been exchanged. // Value Prop: a demo/meeting happened OR requirements are being // discussed, but nothing commercial yet. // Prospective: outreach exists but no demo/meeting confirmed yet. // Unknown: assigned account with zero detected activity at all. let stage: 'commercial' | 'value_prop' | 'prospective' | 'unknown' = 'unknown' if (hasProposal || hasNDA) stage = stageForSignal('commercial') else if (hasDemo || hasRequirementsDiscussion) stage = stageForSignal('value_prop') else if (hasAnyActivity) stage = stageForSignal('prospective') // ── Risk/staleness overlay — independent of stage, can apply at any stage ── let staleness: 'fresh' | 'stale' | 'cold' | null = null const lastActivityDate = [lastSent?.internalDate, lastInbox?.internalDate, calendarEvents[0] ? new Date(calendarEvents[0].start?.dateTime || calendarEvents[0].start?.date).getTime() : 0] .filter(Boolean).sort((a, b) => (b as number) - (a as number))[0] as number | undefined if (lastActivityDate) { const daysSince = Math.floor((now - lastActivityDate) / 86400000) staleness = daysSince >= staleDays * 2 ? 'cold' : daysSince >= staleDays ? 'stale' : 'fresh' } accountReports.push({ account: accountName, region, parentAccountId, stage, staleness, hasAnyActivity, channels, flags: { hasProposal, hasNDA, hasDemo, hasRequirementsDiscussion, hasReply }, lastSentSubject: lastSent?.subject || null, lastInboxSubject: lastInbox?.subject || null }) // ── Persist signal score to org_accounts ─────────────────────────── // Convert stage + staleness into a rough signal score so the pipeline // view can classify this account as verified/partial without needing // a separate score_account call. Real scores from account_signals // will overwrite this on the next get_pipeline call. if (hasAnyActivity && account.id) { const stageScore = stage === 'commercial' ? 65 : stage === 'value_prop' ? 45 : stage === 'prospective' ? 30 : 15 const stalenessAdj = staleness === 'cold' ? -15 : staleness === 'stale' ? -8 : 0 const computedScore = Math.max(10, Math.min(80, stageScore + stalenessAdj)) const tier = computedScore >= 40 ? 'verified' : computedScore >= 25 ? 'partial' : 'unverified' try { await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/org_accounts?id=eq.' + account.id, { method: 'PATCH', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ signal_score: computedScore, signal_score_at: new Date().toISOString(), deal_type: stage }) }) // Auto-record to signal history — enables sparklines + longitudinal analysis await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_signal_history', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: orgId, account_id: account.id, signal_score: computedScore, pipeline_tier: tier, deal_type: stage, source: 'local_intelligence' }) }) } catch(e) { /* non-fatal */ } } } // ── Persist as SAM-sourced rows in account_intelligence (same as // before) so this shows up in the Intel tab and account search, tagged // distinctly from AI-extracted rows. Only persists accounts with real // detected activity — "unknown" stage accounts with zero signal aren't // worth a row, they'd just be noise. const todayStr = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] const existingSamRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_intelligence?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&user_id=eq.' + targetUserId + '&source=eq.sam&meeting_date=eq.' + todayStr + '&select=account_name,meeting_subject', { headers: { 'apikey': SVC, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SVC } } ) const existingSam = asArray(await existingSamRes.json()) const existingKeys = new Set(existingSam.map((r: any) => r.account_name + '||' + r.meeting_subject)) for (const report of accountReports) { if (!report.hasAnyActivity) continue const subjectLabel = 'SAM scan \u2014 ' + stageLabel[report.stage] + ' stage' if (existingKeys.has(report.account + '||' + subjectLabel)) continue const summaryParts: string[] = [] if (report.flags.hasNDA) summaryParts.push('NDA being exchanged') if (report.flags.hasProposal) summaryParts.push('Proposal/commercial discussion in progress') if (report.flags.hasDemo) summaryParts.push('Demo or product discussion held') if (report.flags.hasRequirementsDiscussion) summaryParts.push('Requirements/use-case discussion underway') if (report.staleness === 'cold') summaryParts.push('No activity for an extended period \u2014 going cold') else if (report.staleness === 'stale') summaryParts.push('Activity slowing \u2014 worth a check-in') if (!summaryParts.length) summaryParts.push('Active outreach \u2014 ' + report.channels.email.sent + ' email(s) sent, ' + report.channels.email.replies + ' repl(y/ies)') const expansionLike = (report.flags.hasProposal || report.flags.hasNDA) ? [{ quote: summaryParts.join('; '), type: 'deal_progression' }] : [] const riskLike = (report.staleness === 'cold' || report.staleness === 'stale') ? [{ quote: summaryParts.join('; '), type: 'staleness' }] : [] try { await fetch(SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_intelligence', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'return=minimal' }, body: JSON.stringify({ org_id: orgId, user_id: targetUserId, account_name: report.account, meeting_date: todayStr, meeting_subject: subjectLabel, notetaker_source: 'SAM rule-based scan', source: 'sam', product_feedback: [], pricing_signals: [], competitor_mentions: [], expansion_signals: expansionLike, risk_signals: riskLike, summary: summaryParts.join('. '), sentiment: report.staleness === 'cold' ? 'negative' : (expansionLike.length ? 'positive' : 'neutral'), action_items: [] }) }) } catch(e) { /* non-fatal */ } } const stageCounts = { prospective: 0, value_prop: 0, commercial: 0, unknown: 0 } accountReports.forEach(r => { stageCounts[r.stage as keyof typeof stageCounts]++ }) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, connected: true, accounts: accountReports, stageCounts, count: accountReports.filter(r => r.hasAnyActivity).length }) } // ── get_intelligence ────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Returns extracted intelligence for display — per account (rep view) or org-wide (manager view) if (action === 'get_intelligence') { const { rep_user_id, account_name, days_back, view } = payload const lookbackDays = days_back || orgCfg.intel_lookback_days const SB_SERVICE = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') ?? anonKey // Get org_id const profileRes = await fetch( SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/user_profiles?user_id=eq.' + userId + '&select=org_id,role', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } } ) const profileData = asArray(await profileRes.json()) const orgId = profileData?.[0]?.org_id const callerRole = profileData?.[0]?.role if (!orgId) return jsonResponse({ ok: true, view: 'accounts', rows: [] }) const sinceDate = new Date(Date.now() - lookbackDays * 86400000).toISOString().split('T')[0] let url = SUPABASE_URL + '/rest/v1/account_intelligence?org_id=eq.' + orgId + '&meeting_date=gte.' + sinceDate + '&order=meeting_date.desc' // Manager/exec sees all reps (or a specific rep if rep_user_id is set) — rep sees only own const isManager = canSeeTeam(callerRole) if (!isManager) { url += '&user_id=eq.' + userId } else if (rep_user_id) { url += '&user_id=eq.' + rep_user_id } if (account_name) { url += '&account_name=eq.' + encodeURIComponent(account_name) } const res = await fetch(url + '&limit=200', { headers: { 'apikey': SB_SERVICE, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SB_SERVICE } }) const rowsJson = await res.json() const rows = asArray(rowsJson) if (!res.ok && !Array.isArray(rowsJson)) { return jsonResponse({ ok: false, error: 'DB read failed', detail: rowsJson }, 500) } // For manager feed view — aggregate by signal type across all reps if (isManager && view === 'feed') { const feed: any = { product_feedback: [], pricing_signals: [], competitor_mentions: [], expansion_signals: [], risk_signals: [] } for (const row of rows) { const base = { account: row.account_name, rep_id: row.user_id, date: row.meeting_date, subject: row.meeting_subject } ;(row.product_feedback || []).forEach((s: any) => feed.product_feedback.push({ ...s, ...base })) ;(row.pricing_signals || []).forEach((s: any) => feed.pricing_signals.push({ ...s, ...base })) ;(row.competitor_mentions || []).forEach((s: any) => feed.competitor_mentions.push({ ...s, ...base })) ;(row.expansion_signals || []).forEach((s: any) => feed.expansion_signals.push({ ...s, ...base })) ;(row.risk_signals || []).forEach((s: any) => feed.risk_signals.push({ ...s, ...base })) } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, view: 'feed', feed, rows, total_meetings: rows.length }) } return jsonResponse({ ok: true, view: 'accounts', rows }) } return jsonResponse({ error: 'Unknown action' }, 400) } catch (err) { return jsonResponse({ error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err) }, 500) } }) function buildManagerEmail(repDigests: any[], weekLabel: string, managerEmail: string) { const rows = repDigests.map(r => { const bar = r.completionRate >= 80 ? '#4A8C5C' : r.completionRate >= 50 ? '#C9973E' : '#C0523F' const gaps = r.outreachTasks.filter((t: any) => !t.done).length return `${r.email.split('@')[0]}${r.completionRate}%${r.totalTasks}${r.wins}${r.misses}${gaps}${r.gmailConnected ? '✓' : '○'}` }).join('') return `
⚡ SAM Weekly Digest
${weekLabel}
${rows}
RepDone %TasksWinsMissesGapsGmail
What gaps mean
Gaps are outreach tasks that were logged but not completed and have no email evidence in Gmail.
SamoraTrack · Samora Intelligence Platform
samoratrack.vercel.app
` } function buildRepEmail(rep: any, weekLabel: string) { const bar = rep.completionRate >= 80 ? '#4A8C5C' : rep.completionRate >= 50 ? '#C9973E' : '#C0523F' const pending = rep.outreachTasks.filter((t: any) => !t.done) const completed = rep.outreachTasks.filter((t: any) => t.done) const pendingRows = pending.map((t: any) => `
${t.text}
${t.date}
`).join('') const completedRows = completed.slice(0,5).map((t: any) => `
✓ ${t.text}
${t.date}
`).join('') return `
⚡ Your Weekly Summary
${weekLabel}
${pending.length ? `
Pending (${pending.length})
${pendingRows}
` : ''}${completed.length ? `
Completed (${completed.length})
${completedRows}
` : ''}
SamoraTrack · Samora Intelligence Platform
` } async function sendEmail(apiKey: string, opts: { to: string, subject: string, html: string, text: string }) { const res = await fetch('https://api.resend.com/emails', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + apiKey, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ from: 'SAM by Samora ', to: [opts.to], subject: opts.subject, html: opts.html, text: opts.text }) }) return await res.json() }
